Complete Walkthrough · All 14 Characters · Every Missable

Final Fantasy V I

✦ ✦ ✦
Pixel Remaster Edition

A cinematic JRPG spanning two worlds, 14 characters, and one of gaming's most iconic villains. This guide covers every story beat, every recruitable Esper, and every permanently missable item — organized for first-time players and veterans alike.

✦

Introduction & Essential Tips

▾

Final Fantasy VI is a sweeping epic with 14 playable characters, split into two large worlds: the World of Balance (WoB) and the World of Ruin (WoR). The Pixel Remaster is the definitive modern version of the SNES classic, featuring redrawn pixel art, a re-recorded soundtrack, and auto-battle/speed options.

Pixel Remaster — Key Differences
  • The GBA-exclusive Espers (Leviathan, Gilgamesh, Cactuar, Diabolos) are not included.
  • Auto-battle and 2× / 4× speed features are available — useful for grinding.
  • The bestiary, music player, and CG cutscenes are new additions.
  • The font and UI are redesigned for modern screens.
  • Achievement/trophy support on PC and consoles.
General Tips for the Whole Game
  • Equip Magicite as soon as you get it. Characters gain permanent stat bonuses on level-up based on equipped Espers. Start equipping early to maximize this.
  • Magic stat is king. Most characters benefit most from boosting Magic — Shiva/Bismark/Seraph/Unicorn are great early options.
  • Some treasure chests in the World of Balance upgrade their contents when left until the World of Ruin. These are noted throughout this guide.
  • Strago's Blue Magic (Lore) must be observed in battle — Strago must be alive and present when an enemy uses the spell.
  • Shadow is permanently missable — always wait for him on the Floating Continent.
Use the in-game map's completion percentage (accessed via menu) to track how many chests and items you've collected in each area.
✦

All 14 Characters — Abilities & Overview

▾

Each character has a unique battle command. All characters can also equip Magicite to learn spells. Three characters join automatically in the World of Ruin; all others must be sought out.

Terra Branford
Half-Esper Mage
Skill: Magic / Trance

The game's protagonist. Learns magic naturally as she levels — one of only two characters who do. Trance temporarily doubles magic damage. Top-tier mage.

Mobliz — defeat Humbaba twice.
Locke Cole
Treasure Hunter
Skill: Steal

Can steal items from enemies and use Mug (Steal + attack). Decent attacker. Steal is situationally useful but lacks top-tier items to obtain.

Phoenix Cave — requires two parties.
Edgar Roni Figaro
King of Figaro / Engineer
Skill: Tools

Uses mechanical Tools (Auto Crossbow, Drill, Chainsaw, Air Anchor, Debilitator, Noise Blaster, Bio Blast, Flash). Excellent all-rounder — especially strong early-game.

Nikeah pub → South Figaro → Figaro Castle.
Sabin René Figaro
Martial Artist
Skill: Blitz

Uses Blitz techniques entered via button inputs. Damage is magic-based despite high physical stats. Reliable powerhouse throughout the entire game.

Tzen — holding up a collapsing building.
Celes Chere
Rune Knight / General
Skill: Runic

Absorbs the next magic spell cast by any character with Runic — canceling it but refilling MP. Also learns magic naturally. Versatile fighter-mage hybrid.

Starts WoR as the only active character.
Shadow
Ninja / Assassin
Skill: Throw

Throws weapons (shurikens, scrolls, swords) for massive damage. His dog Interceptor occasionally counters attacks. High speed and solid stats.

Coliseum — bet the Ichigeki found in a WoR cave.
Cyan Garamonde
Knight of Doma
Skill: Bushido (Sword Tech)

Seven powerful sword techniques that charge over time. The charge mechanic is a significant drawback. Benefits greatly from stat-boosting Espers later.

Mt. Zozo — use Rust-Rid to unlock a door in Zozo.
Gau
Wild Child
Skill: Rage

A Blue Mage-style character. Use Leap on the Veldt to have him learn enemy Rages. In Rage mode he acts automatically — extremely powerful with the right setup.

The Veldt — keep a party slot open.
Setzer Gabbiani
Gambler / Airship Captain
Skill: Slot

Randomized slot-based attacks. Prismatic Flash and the 7-7-7 result deal good damage. Essential to the story — provides the airship.

Kohlingen pub → gives access to the Falcon.
Mog
Moogle Dancer
Skill: Dance

Learns 8 unique dances based on terrain. Dance is extremely powerful in the right terrain — Water Harmony and Snowman Rondo are highlights. Molulu's Charm negates random encounters.

Narshe — Moogles' Den in the old mining cave.
Strago Magus
Blue Mage
Skill: Lore

Learns enemy spells (Lore) by witnessing them in battle. Has access to unique and powerful abilities like Aqua Rake, Grand Delta, and Force Field.

Cultists' Tower — bring Relm to snap him out of it.
Relm Arrowny
Artist / Mage
Skill: Sketch / Control

Sketch copies an enemy's attack. Control lets you directly command enemies. Highest natural magic stat in the game — a top-tier mage once Magic is leveled.

Owzer's Mansion in Jidoor.
Gogo
Mime / Master Mimic
Skill: Mimic + any 3 commands

Equips any three commands from other characters. Can mimic the last party action. Extremely versatile — a blank slate you can customize completely.

Triangle Island — let Zone Eater swallow all 4 party members.
Umaro
Yeti Berserker
Skill: Uncontrollable

The strongest raw physical attacker in the game. Cannot be directly controlled — attacks randomly. Two Rage Rings modify his behavior. Fun but impractical for serious play.

Narshe snowfields — requires Mog in party.
✦

Espers / Magicite — Locations & Highlights

▾

Equipping Espers teaches spells (at listed rates per battle) and grants stat bonuses on level-up. Equip early and often — the stat bonuses compound across every level gained while equipped.

The Pixel Remaster does NOT include the GBA Espers: Leviathan, Gilgamesh, Cactuar, or Diabolos. Do not look for them.

✦

Missables Checklist — Never Lose These

▾

Every item is tagged with its guide section so you know exactly when to act. 🔴 = gone forever if missed. 🟡 = one-time decision with meaningful consequences.

World of Balance
🔴
S04 Genji GlovesAt the Returner Hideout, say "No" to Banon's plea THREE times before agreeing. The rare dual-wield accessory is handed to you on the third refusal — you can't get it any other way.
🔴
S05 Ribbon — Locke's ScenarioIn the South Figaro secret bookcase area, explore south of the X-Potion chest. Easy to walk past. Status-immunity accessory — one of the best in the game.
🔴
S07 Chainsaw — Edgar's Best Early ToolSet the clock in the Zozo "Inn" building to exactly 6:10:50. Every NPC in Zozo lies — ignore them. This is the only way to get the Chainsaw, which deals massive physical damage and has a random instant-KO effect.
🔴
S11 Tritoch / Valigarmanda EsperDuring the WoB airship phase, return to Narshe with Terra in your party and fight the Frozen Esper on the cliffs. Grants Mag+3 per level-up — the best magic stat bonus in the game. Only available before the Floating Continent.
🔴
S13 Ward Bangle + TintinnabulumDuring the Imperial Banquet in Vector, find 24 or more scattered soldiers within the 4-minute time limit AND choose the correct answers to Gestahl's dinner questions. Both conditions required for the best reward.
🔴
S14 Flame Rod & Ice Rod — Thamasa Burning MansionTwo chests are hidden inside the burning building. Grab both before escaping — the building only exists during this one story moment and is inaccessible afterward.
🔴
S15 Shadow — Floating Continent EscapeAfter defeating Ultima Weapon, a 6-minute countdown begins. Wait at the escape point until the timer hits 5 seconds — Shadow jumps over and joins you. Leave even 1 second early and he is permanently gone.
🔴
S15 Lv.5 Death Lore — Parasite EnemiesBring Strago in your 3-person Floating Continent team. Parasite enemies on the continent use Lv.5 Death. This Lore is extremely powerful (instakills all enemies whose level is divisible by 5) and is much harder to acquire elsewhere.
🟡
S11 Mog vs. Golden Hairpin — NarsheDuring the airship phase, following Lone Wolf quickly lets you rescue Mog. Fall behind and you get the Golden Hairpin instead. Mog can be recruited normally in WoR, so the Hairpin (halves MP costs) is a perfectly valid consolation.
World of Ruin
🔴
S17 Tzen Collapsing Building — 8 Chests & 3 EnemiesSabin holds up the crumbling building while you loot it under a time limit. All 8 chests and the 3 unique enemies inside (Scorpion, Zokka, Nightwalker) are permanently gone if you exit before collecting them.
🔴
S26 Grand Delta Lore — Ebot's RockOnly learned from the Hidon boss inside Ebot's Rock. Requires collecting 22 Coral pieces scattered around the cave and feeding them to a blocking chest. This is the only opportunity to learn it.
🔴
S29 Force Field Lore — Kefka's TowerIn the three-team button puzzle section, press the LEFT button to trigger a fight with the Fiend boss. Strago MUST be in the party for that team. This is the only source — no other enemy teaches it.
🟡
S23 Ragnarok — Esper vs. SwordWhen Locke retrieves this from Narshe's weapon shop, you choose: Esper (teaches Ultima — the game's most powerful spell, available on every character) or Sword (a strong weapon for one character). Take the Esper every time unless you're doing a novelty run.
⚔

Equipment, Esper Bonuses & Boss Reference

▾
Best Weapons (World of Ruin Endgame)
Ultima Weapon
Ragnarok Esper converts to this
Strongest sword for Terra, Celes, Locke, and Edgar. When you find Ragnarok in Narshe's weapon shop (S23), choose the Esper version (teaches Ultima). Then find the actual Ultima Weapon in the Kefka's Tower. Ignore Ragnarok the sword. Ultima Weapon deals more damage the higher the wielder's HP relative to max.
Soul Sabre / Lightbringer
Soul Sabre: Colosseum / Lightbringer: Kefka's Tower
Soul Sabre (Sketch command lets Relm use enemy moves) is best for Relm due to the Magic boost. Lightbringer (Kefka's Tower chest) is one of the strongest overall weapons. Cat Ear Hood + Soul Sabre on Relm = highest magic damage in the game due to her native high magic stat.
Valiant Knife
South Figaro secret passage
Locke's best weapon in most builds. Deals damage equal to (9999 − current HP) — stronger when Locke is injured. Combined with the Genji Gloves (dual wield) and high Max HP, the Valiant Knife is extremely reliable. Found in the back room of South Figaro's armor shop via a hidden passage.
Imp Halberd
Imps-only equipment
Only usable by Imp-status characters. Equipping Imp Armor + Imp Halberd makes an Imp-ified character invincible with very high defense. Niche "Imp Strategy" for defeating Kefka's Tower's hardest sections: Gogo + Imp set = near-invulnerable warrior who Mimics.
Fixed Dice (Casino)
Setzer only · Joker's death move
Setzer's ultimate tool — the Fixed Dice deals 6d6 × Setzer's level damage, bypassing defense entirely. At level 60, deals ~2,000–6,000 per hit. Found in the basement of the Jidoor Auction House or via Setzer's unique Slot command with the Fixed Dice accessory equipped. Best when Setzer runs the Slot command repeatedly.
Chainsaw
Edgar · Zozo clock puzzle
Edgar's best Tool for most of the game. Set Zozo's "Inn" clock to exactly 6:10:50 (ignore all lying NPCs). Chainsaw: high physical damage + 1/8 chance of instant KO (OHKO). Edgar's Tools require no MP — Chainsaw, Drill, and Bio Blaster remain powerful through the endgame.
Esper Level-Up Bonuses (Stat Growth)

Equipping an Esper grants a permanent stat bonus each time a character levels up while that Esper is equipped. Stack the right Espers during the World of Ruin grinding phase for endgame stat optimization.

Tritoch / Valigarmanda
Mag +3 per level · WoB cliffs
The best Magic stat bonus in the game. Three levels of Magic per level-up while equipped. Equip on Terra, Celes, Relm, and Strago during WoR grinding. This Esper is missable — return to Narshe's frozen cliffs with Terra before the Floating Continent.
Zona Seeker / Shiva / Unicorn
Mag +2 · Early game
Shiva (+2 Magic per level) and Unicorn (+2 Magic) are solid early magic-boost Espers. Before obtaining Tritoch, these are the best available for boosting mage characters. Unicorn also teaches Cure and Remedy — useful spells for early magic-learning.
Golem / Bismark
HP +30 per level
Bismark (+30 HP/level) is excellent for physical fighters who need bulk. Golem (+50 HP but less magic) is better for tanks. Edgar, Sabin, and Shadow benefit most from HP-boosting Espers during the World of Balance.
Alexander
Vigor +1, HP +20 · WoR Doma
Found in Doma Castle (WoR) by triggering Cyan's dream sequence. Alexander teaches Holy (the game's most powerful targeted magic) and provides balanced stat growth for physical/mixed characters. Balanced bonuses make it excellent for Celes and Cyan.
Palidor
Speed +2 per level
Speed stat determines ATB gauge fill rate. Speed +2/level over 10 levels = +20 Speed — a significant turn-rate advantage. Equip on characters who need to act first: Rosa-equivalent healers and your main damage dealer. Found in the World of Ruin ocean via specific search spot.
Ragnarok (Esper)
Teaches Ultima · Narshe WoR
Taking the Ragnarok Esper (over the sword) is the correct choice for virtually every run. Ultima is the most powerful spell in the game — a non-elemental AoE magic attack dealing ~6,000+ damage to all enemies when a character reaches high Magic. Ragnarok the Esper also randomly transforms enemies into items (the Metamorphose spell). Every character in the game can learn Ultima with this Esper equipped long enough.
Relics (Key Accessories)
Genji Gloves
Returner Hideout · Must say No 3×
The dual-wield relic — equip in one slot to attack with weapons in both hands. Equip on Locke with Valiant Knife + another weapon, or Terra/Celes with two strong swords. Missable only if you don't say "No" to Banon three consecutive times at the Returner Hideout in S04. Cannot be purchased anywhere.
Gauntlet
Shops · Two-handed mode
Two-Hand mode: equip one weapon in both hands for double the weapon's damage. Best with the Brave Blade equivalent (strongest sword) on high-Strength characters. Choose between Gauntlet (one weapon, doubled) or Genji Gloves (two weapons) based on your build.
Ribbon
Kefka's Tower / rare drops
Provides immunity to all status effects — the most powerful protective accessory. Equip on Terra, Celes, or your healer to prevent them from being status-locked during Kefka's Tower. Very rare — only 1–2 available in a normal playthrough without grinding.
Celestriad (Gem Box)
World of Ruin · Auction House
Reduces all spell MP costs to 1 MP. Combined with the Gauntlet's double-damage, your mages can spam Ultima indefinitely. Found via the Jidoor Auction House in the World of Ruin. One of the most impactful late-game relics.
Master's Scroll (Offering)
Kefka's Tower · x4 attack
Attacking hits 4 times at half power each — total 2× damage if all hit, but more importantly it hits 4 times. Combined with the Atma Weapon (damage scales with HP), each of the 4 hits deals full scaled damage. One of the highest single-turn damage combinations in the game. Found in Kefka's Tower.
Economizer (Celestriad)
1 MP spells
All magic costs 1 MP. Combine with Ultima and near-unlimited MP pools for infinite Ultima casting. The key enabling relic for the "Ultima spam" strategy that trivializes Kefka's Tower and all bosses.
Boss Quick Reference
Whelk · Narshe Mines
HP: 1,600 + shell
Tutorial boss. Attack the SHELL for body damage. Attacking the head causes it to use Mega Volt — only attack the shell. Lightning magic accelerates the fight. Edgar's Noiseblaster puts it to sleep.
Tunnel Armor · South Figaro
HP: 2,600 · Lightning weak
Uses Electrify (Lightning AoE) — don't attack with Lightning (it heals it). Use Fire/Ice from Terra and Celes. Edgar's Auto Crossbow deals reliable AoE damage. Keep Locke alive to steal Elixir from the Imperial soldiers nearby first.
Vargas · Mt. Kolts
HP: 3,500 · Wait for Sabin
Vargas is invincible until Sabin arrives — the scripted Blitz (Aura Cannon / Pummel) ends the fight. Do not waste resources attacking. When Sabin arrives, he dispatches Vargas in one cutscene Blitz.
TunnelArmr · S04
HP: 2,600
Same as above. Fire and physical attacks. Edgar's Drill deals pure physical damage ignoring defense — extremely useful here.
Ultros · Four fights total
HP: ~5,000–12,000 (varies)
Recurring comic villain. First fight: Edgar's Noiseblaster + Bio Blaster + Terra's Fire. Second fight (Lete River): Edgar's Flash reduces his special attacks. Third fight (Opera House): Relm's Sketch makes him paint himself for massive damage — scripted joke ending. Fourth fight (Colosseum/WoR): treat as a standard boss.
Atma Weapon · Floating Continent
HP: 24,000 · Major WoB boss
Uses Flare, Meteor, and Ultima (endgame spells mid-game). This fight is notoriously brutal for first-timers. Keep all characters above 2,000 HP. Terra's Trance doubles her magic — Firaga spam. Edgar's Chainsaw for instant KO attempt. Setzer's Slots for lucky 7-7-7. His damage output scales with his remaining HP — he gets weaker as you damage him.
Guardian · Kefka's Tower
HP: 60,000 · Three forms
Three-form bosses before Kefka. Each form uses different elemental spells. The Inferno form uses Blaze (fire AoE). The Poltergeist form is magic-heavy — use Runic (Celes absorbs spells). The Dullahan form is physical — use magic. Have all three teams (required for Kefka's Tower split) fully equipped before this dungeon.
Kefka · Final Boss
HP: 62,000 total (4 tiers)
Four tiers of enemies before the true Kefka. Tiers 1–3 are multi-enemy groups — AoE magic (Ultima, Merton) clears them. Kefka himself: uses Forsaken (massive magic to all party members), Goner, and Fallen One (reduces all HP to 1). Strategy: Fenix Down stockpile, have Rosa equivalent heal every round after each Forsaken. Ultima from every mage, Chainsaw/Sabin's Bum Rush for physical. Kefka's Light of Judgment has already destroyed towns — he is the most powerful being alive. The fight's difficulty reflects this.
Gau's Rage List — Top Picks

Gau's Rage command uses monster abilities. The most powerful Rages are:

Stray Cat Rage
Veldt · Early game
Gains Claw attacks (physical) and Cat Scratch (powerful multi-hit). Stray Cat Rage makes Gau one of the best physical attackers in the early game. Easy to obtain on the Veldt — just stand there and wait for Gau to leap up from a Stray Cat encounter.
Conjurer Rage
World of Ruin · Magic caster
Casts Doom (instant KO countdown) on enemies. Niche but surprisingly useful against trash enemies in long dungeon sections. The Doom status ticks down regardless of speed — instant kill in 10 seconds.
Io Rage
Kefka's Tower area
Uses Magnitude 8 (earth AoE, ~4,000 to all grounded enemies). One of Gau's highest-damage Rages for trash clearing. Only works on non-flying enemies.
Behemoth Rage
World of Ruin
Physical attacks + Meteor (randomly). When the Behemoth Rage triggers Meteor, it hits for massive non-elemental AoE damage. Late-game Gau with Behemoth Rage is legitimately one of the strongest options in the party for boss fights where Meteor triggers.
Strago's Lore — Complete List
Aqua Rake
Anguiform enemies · WoB
Water/wind AoE damage. Strong vs fire enemies. One of Strago's best damage Lores early — Anguiforms are in the Serpent Trench. Strago must be alive and in the active party when the enemy uses it on him.
Lv. 5 Death
Parasite · Floating Continent
Instantly KOs all enemies with levels divisible by 5. Extremely powerful for trash clearing. The Parasite enemies on the Floating Continent are almost the only source — bring Strago in your 3-person team there or you'll miss this permanently.
Grand Delta
Hidon · Ebot's Rock (S26)
Most powerful Lore in the game — massive non-elemental damage to all enemies. Only learned from Hidon in Ebot's Rock (requires 22 Coral pieces). Complete this sidequest before Kefka's Tower. Grand Delta + Celestriad (1 MP) = Strago's best offensive output.
Force Field
Fiend · Kefka's Tower (S29)
Randomly nullifies one element for the party. Learned from the Fiend boss in Kefka's Tower — press the LEFT button in the button puzzle section and have Strago in that team. Only source. Permanently missable if that team doesn't have Strago.
Quasar
Slagworm · Desertica desert
Non-elemental AoE, moderate power. Learned from Slagworms in the desert. Easy to obtain in WoR and useful as a non-elemental backup when enemies absorb other elements.
Rippler
Chimera · Various
Swaps status effects with the target. Normally niche — but can be used to give the enemy a beneficial status you have (like Haste) and take away their dangerous statuses. Situational but amusing.
🌏

World of Balance

The Empire rules with an iron fist. The Returners resist. And somewhere between them — a girl who forgot everything she was.

1

Narshe & the Mines

Narshe ▾

The game opens with Terra and two Imperial soldiers (Vicks and Wedge) marching through a blizzard toward Narshe in Magitek Armor. This opening acts as the combat tutorial.

Narshe Mines — Entrance (Tutorial)
  • Combat tutorial: Magitek Armor grants Terra Fire Beam, Blizzard Beam, and Thunder Beam. Use the Fire Beam on standard enemies — it hits all foes.
  • Enemy: Wererats — basic enemies. 2–3 hits with any attack.
  • Enemy: Bandit — slightly tougher. Fire Beam clears groups.
  • Mini-boss: Ymir — a giant shelled creature guarding the mine interior.
    — Shell form: do not attack physically — the shell deflects attacks. Use Fire Beam to hit over the shell.
    — Open form (turtle retreats into shell and re-emerges): the creature itself is exposed — hit with everything.
    — He has ~600 HP. Fire Beam spam wins easily.
  • After Ymir: Vicks and Wedge investigate the frozen Esper at the mine's end. Terra's Slave Crown breaks — she uses uncontrolled magic and collapses. Imperial escort disappears.
Save Point
  • There is no traditional save point during the Magitek intro — the game auto-saves at transitions. You cannot die during this opening (it's scripted).
  • The first proper save point appears in Narshe's residential area after the Moogle rescue.
Escape Through the Mines (Terra alone)
  • Arvis helps Terra escape. She flees through the mine tunnels chased by the town guards (Lobos and Vomammoths).
  • Do not fight — just run through each room heading north. The enemies are too strong for Terra alone at this stage.
  • Terra falls into a lower mine shaft and is found by 10 Moogles.
Moogle Defense (Tactical Battle)
  • You control Mog + up to 9 other Moogles to protect Terra from waves of guards.
  • Enemies: Marshal, Lobo, Doberman — all standard soldiers. Each Moogle takes a turn independently.
  • This battle cannot be lost (Terra is safe regardless) — it's a fun introductory battle. Use it to experiment with the ATB system.
  • After the battle: Terra faints again. Locke carries her to safety in Narshe.
Chests in This Section
  • There are no chests accessible during the Magitek intro or Moogle defense. The first lootable chests are in Figaro Castle (next section).
  • The Frozen Esper (Valigarmanda) is visible through ice at the mine apex — do not interact with it yet. It becomes a boss during the WoB airship phase.
Early bestiary entries: Wererat, Bandit, Spritzer, Ymir (shell form + open form).
Collect all chests in the mine before proceeding — several contain useful early equipment. Check every path.
2

Figaro Castle & Edgar

Figaro Castle ▾
  • Travel south from Narshe across the desert. Arrive at Figaro Castle — Edgar is the king and secretly allied with the Returners rebel movement.
Figaro Castle — Chests & Shopping
  • 4 Chests: Phoenix Down (B1 left room), Potion (B1 right room), Antidote (B2 left hallway), Sleeping Bag (B2 right alcove). Collect all before the castle submerges.
  • Shop (ground floor, right wing): Buy Edgar's Auto Crossbow (if not already free) and Bio Blaster — both hit all enemies for free. Also stock Potions and Antidotes. The shop has Iron Helm and Iron Armor if you can afford them.
  • Visit the elder on the second floor for backstory on Edgar and Sabin's past.
  • Visit the roof chocobo stable — grab the hidden item near the chocobo pen.
Imperial Arrival & Castle Escape
  • Kefka arrives with Imperial soldiers demanding Terra. Edgar stalls and uses the castle's submersion mechanism to escape underground.
  • Cave underneath the castle: 2 Fidor enemies (wolf-dogs) ambush as Edgar and Locke exit on chocobos. They're weak to Fire — quick fight. Edgar's Auto Crossbow hits both simultaneously.
Chocobos → South Figaro
  • Ride the chocobos northeast. You cannot be ambushed on chocobo. Head directly to South Figaro.
No boss here, but make sure Edgar has the Auto Crossbow equipped as a Tool. It hits all enemies and is free to use.
Edgar's Tools cost NO MP and hit hard. Prioritize them over normal attacks. Buy new Tools from shops whenever possible.
3

South Figaro & the Caves

South Figaro · South Figaro Cave ▾
  • Arrive at South Figaro from the north road. The town is under Imperial influence but not yet occupied.
South Figaro — Town Exploration (Do All of This Now)
  • Rich Man's Mansion (large house, center of town):
    — Ground floor: interact with the bookcase on the left wall to open a hidden room.
    — Hidden room contains 6 chests: Elixir, Relic Ring, Earrings, Hyper Wrist, Heavy Shield, Genji Glove fragment (varies by version).
    — Also check the clock in the mansion — it hides a Potion.
  • Barrels and crates around town (9 hidden items): Check every barrel, pot, and crate in all buildings. These items upgrade to better versions in WoR — if you want both the early item AND the WoR upgrade, take them now, then the WoR version will be different items in the same spots.
  • Town shop: Buy Mythril Blade (Edgar), Hi-Potion stock, and Earrings if available. This is your last shop before a long dungeon segment.
  • Save Point: Inn in the center of town. Rest and save here.
South Figaro Cave — Leave Chests for WoR
  • Exit west through the South Figaro Cave. The cave has 3 chests that upgrade to significantly better items in WoR:
    — Chest 1 → upgrades to Hermes Sandals (Auto-Haste — one of the best accessories)
    — Chest 2 → upgrades to Hi-Potion
    — Chest 3 → upgrades to Mythril Vest or armor
    Leave all 3 chests for now unless you're struggling with the current difficulty.
  • Navigate the cave: it's a single winding path, no branching. Watch for the 3 chest locations on the left wall of the main corridor.
  • No boss in this cave at this point — just basic enemies (Rhodox, Beagle).
  • Exit northwest to the Mt. Kolts area.
Duncan's Cabin (Optional)
  • Duncan's Cabin is north of the cave exit, on the edge of the world map. Enter and grab the Tent from the corner. Duncan is Sabin's martial arts teacher — his story comes up later.
The 3 chests in South Figaro Cave contain better items in WoR. Leave them if you want the upgrades.
The hidden bookcase room in the rich mansion contains some of the best gear available at this point in the game. Don't miss it.
4

Mt. Kolts & the Returner Hideout

Mt. Kolts · Returner Hideout ▾
  • Mt. Kolts is entered from the southeast of the mountain face. Party: Locke, Terra, Edgar.
Mt. Kolts — Navigation & Chests
  • The mountain has a single main path winding upward with occasional branches to chests.
    — Chest 1 (first junction, go right): Tent
    — Chest 2 (upper path, left branch): Mythril Claw
    — Chest 3 (near summit): Hi-Potion
    — Chest 4 (behind the summit waterfall, hidden — go around the back): Earrings
  • Enemies: Trilium (plant, weak to Fire), Bleary (cyclops, targets front row), Vomammoth (cold, weak to Fire). Keep Locke in back row — he's your key character and very fragile.
  • Save Point: There's a save crystal on a ledge just before the summit area. Use it before Vargas.
Boss: Vargas (Summit)
  • Vargas is a martial artist accompanied by two Ipoohs (bears). He was Duncan's other student and killed his master (allegedly).
  • Phase 1: You cannot damage Vargas directly while the Ipoohs are alive. Target both bears with Edgar's Auto Crossbow (hits all enemies) — take 2–3 turns to kill both.
  • Phase 2: With the bears dead, Vargas is targetable. Attack him directly. After a few turns, Sabin arrives automatically and uses Raging Fist (a Blitz) to finish him.
  • Sabin joins your party permanently after this cutscene.
Returner Hideout — Items & the Genji Gloves
  • Head south from Mt. Kolts to the Returner Hideout (a cave carved into a cliff face).
  • 6 Chests: Earrings, Phoenix Down, Sleeping Bag, Antidote, Potion (×2). Collect all.
  • 3 items from NPCs: Talk to all rebels in the hideout. Several give you items including an Elixir and Echo Screen.
  • Banon's room: He asks Terra to join the Returners as their "hope."
Genji Gloves (Dual Wield): When Banon asks if Terra will join, say "No". He asks three times. On the third "No", he hands you the Genji Gloves. Then say "Yes" to continue. This is the only way to get them in the entire World of Balance.
Vargas Phase 1: Edgar's Auto Crossbow kills both bears in 2–3 turns. Do not waste magic on them. Phase 2 is auto-ended by Sabin.
5

The Three Scenarios

Locke · Sabin · Edgar/Terra ▾

After the Lethe River Ultros battle (tutorial-style fight), the story splits into three simultaneous paths. Play all three — the order is your choice. Sabin's is by far the longest.

Locke's Scenario — Rescuing Celes
  • Locke enters occupied South Figaro alone. The only way forward is through disguise — knock out (fight) an Imperial Captain to steal his uniform, then a Merchant for the next checkpoint.
  • Navigation: enter the rich man's mansion (same building as before), use the bookcase secret room, descend to find Celes imprisoned.
  • Chest during infiltration: In the basement area south of the X-Potion chest, explore the lower corridor — there is a Ribbon hidden against the south wall. Easy to miss.
  • Collect the Ribbon. Grab Celes. Exit via the South Figaro Cave heading west.
  • Boss: Tunnel Armor — a mechanical spider in the cave. It uses Magna Roar (a magic attack). Celes's Runic absorbs magic spells — activate Runic each turn, then have Locke attack physically. The Tunnel Armor takes 3–4 turns to destroy.
Ribbon (Locke's Scenario): In the basement south of the X-Potion chest, walk along the south wall. The Ribbon is hidden in a dark corner. It prevents most status ailments and is one of the best accessories in the game.
Sabin's Scenario — Full Walkthrough
  • Doma Road (north of Figaro): Sabin encounters Shadow at a roadside inn. Pay 3,000 gil to hire him — he's an excellent assassin and worth every gil. If you can't afford it he leaves.
  • Imperial Camp outside Doma Castle: Kefka poisons Doma's water supply, killing the entire kingdom. Only Cyan survives — his family among the dead. He joins in a rage. Cyan's Bushido is slow to charge but hits hard.
  • Phantom Forest (linear path, exits east): Ghostly area. No items. Follow the glowing path east to the Phantom Train station.
  • Phantom Train — Car by Car (board at the rear and work forward):
    — Car 1 (rear): No items. Pass through.
    — Car 2 (sleeping car): Wake each ghost — they either fight or give items. Open all coffin lids. Chest: Tent in the upper berth.
    — Car 3 (dining car): 3 ghost waiters can be recruited as temporary party members by chatting with them. Grab the dining car's 2 items from the cabinet.
    — Car 4 (engine): Interact with the boiler to detach all rear cars. Then fight the engine boss.
    — Boss: Phantom Train — Yes, the whole train. Fire attacks work. Phoenix Down / Revivify items instantly kill it (it's undead). Sabin's Suplex (Meteor Strike Blitz) also works famously. HP ~3,000.
  • Sabin's Blitz input for Meteor Strike: L, R, L, R, ↑, ↓ + Confirm (on the train boss specifically — inputs work even on "non-character" targets).
  • Exit: Barren Falls — Sabin, Cyan, and Gau (if recruited) jump into the waterfall and swim through the Serpent Trench to reach Nikeah. Shadow cannot swim and departs here.
Recruiting Gau (Veldt)
  • After Barren Falls: go east to the Veldt — a large open plains region where all previously encountered enemies appear as random battles.
  • In a battle on the Veldt, Gau will appear and join the fight. Do NOT attack him — use Defend or Heal each turn. He leaves peacefully after the battle.
  • Travel south of the Veldt to Mobliz village. Buy Dried Meat from the item shop.
  • Return to the Veldt. In the next battle where Gau appears, give him the Dried Meat. He permanently joins your party.
  • Use Gau's Leap command to learn new Rages from any enemy on the Veldt. He vanishes and returns after a few random battles having learned those enemy Rages.
Nikeah & Joining the Main Party
  • After swimming the Serpent Trench, arrive in Nikeah. Check the Nikeah clock (in the inn) for a hidden Elixir.
  • Board the ferry north to South Figaro — all three scenario parties converge at Narshe.
Phantom Train: Use Fire attacks — its undead nature means healing items like Phoenix Downs can instantly defeat it!
Terra/Edgar's Scenario — Narshe Defense
  • Short scenario. Navigate the Narshe Mine security checkpoint.
  • Reach the Moogle Room — collect 3 chests. The last chest upgrades to a Ribbon if left until WoR.
6

Defending Narshe

Narshe Mines ▾
  • All party members reunite. Arrange them into three groups of 3 to defend the Frozen Esper from Imperial forces in a tactical formation battle.
  • The Empire sends a large force up the mine path. Guide your groups to intercept enemy parties.
  • Boss: Kefka — the main villain appears. He's manageable at this stage. Defeat him with all available magic and attacks. Terra transforms into her Esper form after.
Spread your strongest characters across the three groups. Keep a healer in each group. Edgar's Tools and Sabin's Blitz hit hard across all groups.
7

Kohlingen, Jidoor & Zozo

Kohlingen · Jidoor · Zozo ▾
  • With the airship, fly northwest to Kohlingen (small village). Talk to the old man in the pub — Locke's tragic past with Rachel is revealed here. Collect items in the WoR-upgradeable barrels in the houses.
  • Fly east to Jidoor (large mansion town north of the Opera House).
Jidoor Auction House — Espers
  • The Auction House is north of the town center. Espers rotate through the bidding pool. To get all available WoB Auction Espers, you may need to attend multiple auction cycles (exit and re-enter the building).
  • Available Espers: Carbuncle (Spd+1, Reflect/Shell/Haste), Golem (HP+25%, physical block summon), Zona Seeker (Mag+2, Shell/Regen/Float).
  • Also on auction: Zoneseek sometimes appears as a duplicate name — this is just Zona Seeker under an alternate spelling. Don't rebuy it.
  • Save before bidding. Reload if you lose to the auto-bidder. The NPC bidder will try to outbid you — keep raising until they yield.
  • Golem and Zona Seeker are WoB-only Auction Espers and cannot be obtained in WoR. Get both now.
Dragon's Neck Colosseum (south of Jidoor)
  • This is not the Zozo building — it's a separate cave/arena south of Jidoor on the world map. Enter and speak to the man inside to get the Hero's Ring (a relic that boosts physical damage — useful on Sabin).
  • Cactrot enemies appear here. They drop useful items but have ~2 million HP — flee unless you want the challenge.
Zozo — Navigation (Rooftop Town)
  • Zozo is reached by flying northwest. It always rains. Every NPC in Zozo lies — ignore all hints and dialogue from townspeople.
  • Navigate the rooftops by jumping across gaps and using external staircases. Terra is at the top of the tower.
  • Ramuh's Esper chest: In one of the Zozo buildings, a man gives you the Ramuh Magicite — you don't need to find it via puzzle, he just hands it over.
  • Chainsaw Clock Puzzle (Do Not Miss):
    — Find the building labeled "Inn" on Zozo's mid-level (it's not a real inn).
    — Inside is a large clock on the wall.
    — Set the time to exactly 6:10:50 (hours: 6, minutes: 10, seconds: 50).
    — Interact with each dial independently. Correct setting opens a secret chest with Chainsaw — Edgar's best Tool, dealing high physical damage with a random instant-KO effect.
    — This item is permanently missable — in WoR the same clock gives a different reward.
  • Zozo chests (buildings throughout): Chain Flail, Heal Rod, Buckler — collect from the various floor rooms as you climb.
Boss: Dadaluma (Tower Summit)
  • Dadaluma is a bouncer-type enemy who jumps around and summons additional guards when damaged. HP ~3,000.
  • He uses Pummel (multiple weak hits) and Shock (heavy single target). Keep Locke/Celes in the back row.
  • Attack with everything — Edgar's Chainsaw (if you got it), Sabin's Blitz, physical hits. He's not elementally weak — just pile on damage.
  • After defeating him: Ramuh Magicite obtained (if not already given). Terra is rescued. She joins the party.
Chainsaw (Edgar's Tool): Set the Zozo clock to 6:10:50. This is permanently missable — the clock gives a different item in WoR.
Equip the Ramuh Magicite immediately on someone. Start earning Thunder spell AP now.
After getting Magicite (Espers), equip them immediately on your characters. The level-up stat bonuses stack from this moment forward — every level gained without an Esper is a permanent loss.
At the Jidoor Auction House, save before bidding. Reload if you don't win the Esper you want. The inventory cycles over time.
8

The Opera House

Opera House ▾

One of the most iconic moments in JRPG history. Celes performs in an opera to lure Setzer — a legendary gambler and airship captain — so the Returners can steal his ship.

  • Travel to the Opera House (east of Jidoor, south road). Impresario needs a stand-in for his star — Celes looks exactly like the lead soprano, Maria.
Memorize Celes's Lines
  • Impresario gives you a script. Read it. During the opera you'll select lyrics from a multiple-choice prompt. The correct choices are:
    — Line 1: "I'm the darkness, you're the stars"
    — Line 2: "I'm the darkness, you're the stars" (same again)
    — Line 3: "Must I live a lifetime dreaming of you?"
  • If you choose wrong: Ultros's plan succeeds earlier. You can still win — you just lose a bit of time.
Opera House Scaffolding — The Timer (5 Minutes)
  • While Celes performs, Ultros is in the rafters with a 4-ton weight. A 5-minute countdown begins. You control Locke navigating the backstage scaffolding.
  • Route: Stage right door → up two ladders → catwalk left → up ladder → catwalk right → another ladder → find Ultros. The route is linear once you find the first ladder.
  • Random encounters in the scaffolding: Pug (physical) and Apparite (lightning weakness). Use Edgar's Tools or Sabin's Blitz — fast and effective. Flee if comfortable.
  • 5 minutes is very generous. Take your time looting but don't sit still.
  • Save Point: None in the scaffolding — save at the Inn before starting the opera.
Boss: Ultros (Rafters)
  • Party: Locke, Edgar, Sabin (whoever you have). HP ~3,900.
  • Ultros is weak to Fire. Use Terra's Fira, Edgar's Chainsaw/Drill, Sabin's Fire-based Blitz. He uses Tentacle (single hit), Ink (Darkness status — Antidote/Echo Screen), and Self-Destruct (low HP).
  • Keep everyone above 400 HP. Don't let him get a Self-Destruct off — kill him before his HP falls too low, or just hit very hard.
  • After: he drops onto the stage. The opera continues. Setzer appears to kidnap "Maria."
Dealing with Setzer
  • Setzer takes Celes (mistaking her for Maria) to his airship — the Blackjack. When he discovers the deception, Celes challenges him to a coin flip: heads = airship, tails = she marries him.
  • Setzer flips a two-headed coin (rigged by Celes). Setzer accepts the loss with good humor and gives you the Blackjack airship. He joins the party.
  • The Blackjack is your first airship. The entire World of Balance opens up from this point. Land anywhere except dense forest or mountains.
Ultros: Fire spells hit his weakness. Edgar's Drill deals strong consistent damage. Avoid single-target physical attacks on his tentacles.
9

South Continent Towns

Albrook · Maranda · Tzen · Vector ▾
  • With the airship, explore the southern continent. Visit Albrook, Maranda, and Tzen for items and story context.
  • In Tzen, buy the Phantom (Seraph) Magicite for 3,000 gil — it teaches the Vanish spell and gives Speed +2 per level. Worth it.
  • Vector is the Imperial capital. Explore for story context and prepare for the Magitek Factory.
This is also a great time to return to all previously visited areas for missed chests/items. Use the airship's world overview to revisit spots.
10

Magitek Factory & Research Facility

Vector · Magitek Factory ▾
  • The Magitek Research Facility is below Vector. Enter via the trapdoor in Vector's main building. The factory has 3 major areas: Pipes Level, Conveyor Belt Level, and Chimney Exterior.
Area 1 — Pipes Level (B1)
  • Navigate through a series of pipes and valves. Each valve room connects to the next through colored pipe exits.
    — Take the left pipe at the first junction (right is a dead end).
    — Middle junction: go through the center pipe to reach the Chest area.
    — Chests 1–4 are on this level: Eye Drop, Hi-Potion, Elixir, Ether.
  • Enemies here: Trapper (sets traps that cause status ailments — use Esuna), Sergeant (summons reinforcements).
  • Boss: Number 024 — a mechanical creature. HP ~4,500.
    — Silences party members with Mute — bring Echo Screens or cast Esuna (if learned).
    — Weak to Poison/Bio. If you have Bio spell, it will deal 2,000+ damage. Otherwise physical attacks work fine.
    — After beating it: the path opens to Level 2.
Area 2 — Conveyor Belt Level (B2)
  • Conveyor belts move you automatically — step sideways to fight the current or use the stationary floor sections.
    — Chests 5–9 hidden in alcoves off the main belt path: Elixir, Magicite Shard (×2), Tincture, X-Potion.
    — The frozen Esper canisters (Siren, Ifrit, Shiva) are in the large circular room at the belt's end. Interact with each canister to free the Esper — they give you their Magicite.
  • Equip Siren, Ifrit, and Shiva immediately after receiving them. Siren teaches Sleep/Silence. Ifrit teaches Fira. Shiva teaches Blizzara and Osmose.
  • After the canister room: minecart ride to the chimney.
  • Boss: Number 128 — a multi-armed machine. HP ~7,000 (body), plus two Right Arms (HP ~3,000 each).
    — Destroy the Right Blades (arms) first — they counter every attack on the body.
    — Chests 10–12 are in side rooms of the chimney area above (Magicite Shard, Tincture, Elixir).
    — Use Fire on the body after both arms are destroyed.
Area 3 — Chimney Exterior (Boss Gauntlet)
  • Climb the external chimney structure. Boss: Crane (×2) fight on the chimney platform.
    — Two Cranes on either side of the platform. They attack with physical swings and laser beams.
    — Do NOT use Lightning attacks — one Crane absorbs electricity.
    — Use Fire, Ice, and Wind attacks. Have Edgar use Drill. Focus one Crane first (left one first) then the other.
    — After Cranes: Ifrit and Shiva show themselves as Magicite (if not already collected) — confirm you have all 3 Espers.
  • Exit: After the Cranes, the party escapes via the Blackjack (airship swoops in). The Magitek Factory section is complete. You can now explore freely.
Equip Siren, Ifrit, and Shiva on your three strongest magic users immediately. These are among the best WoB Espers for spell learning and stat gains.
This dungeon is long. Stock up on supplies before entering. Bring Tinctures and Ethers for MP management.
Key loot: Siren, Ifrit, Shiva Magicite. All three are excellent — equip them immediately for spell learning and stat gains.
11

Airship Exploration Phase

World Map (WoB) ▾

After the factory, you have free airship travel over the entire World of Balance. This is the best time to catch up on optional content before the point of no return.

  • Narshe: Follow Lone Wolf the Moogle to either recruit Mog or receive the Golden Hairpin. (Mog is easier to recruit in WoR, so getting the hairpin here is fine.)
  • Mog's Dances: Mog learns dances from terrain. Take him to different locations to learn all 8 dances: Fire Dance (Figaro Cave), Wind Song (plains), Forest Suite (forests), Cave Walk (caves), Desert Aria (desert), Love Sonata (towns), Earth Blues (mountains), Water Harmony (near water).
  • Veldt: Farm Rages for Gau by using Leap on every new enemy type. Consider grinding here — no EXP is gained, just AP and Gil.
  • Jidoor Auction House: Complete your Esper collection — buy Carbuncle, Golem, Zona Seeker, and Seraph if not already obtained.
  • Thamasa: Explore the village. Find 5 of 6 hidden items in barrels (the 6th comes later).
  • Optional — Intangir: On the small island in the northeast corner of the map is a rare enemy called Intangir. It's invisible but can be encountered. A required bestiary entry if going for 100%.
This is one of your last chances to grind AP on the Veldt before the World of Balance ends. Having 3–4 spells at x2 speed is very worthwhile for later dungeons.
12

Cave to the Sealed Gate

East Continent ▾
  • Board the Imperial ship in Albrook harbor. This is a story-mandatory step — travel with General Leo and Setzer/Celes to the Eastern Continent.
  • Land on the Eastern Continent. The Cave to the Sealed Gate is south of the landing zone.
Cave to the Sealed Gate — Floor by Floor
  • Floor 1 (Entrance): Linear path with two bridges and a switch on the east wall. Pull the switch to raise the first bridge. Chest 1: Hi-Potion (left alcove after the bridge).
  • Floor 2 (Bridge Puzzle): Four switches arranged in two pairs. Pull switches in this order: left-lower → right-upper → left-upper → right-lower. Each switch toggles the adjacent bridge sections. After all four, the full path across is open. Chest 2: Elixir (east dead-end before the final bridge).
  • Dirt Clods (do not miss): On Floor 2's main path, four small pile-shaped objects on the cave floor. Interact with each — they look like floor tiles. These are rare collectibles. Approximate locations: before switch 1, after switch 2, beside switch 3, and near the south exit.
  • Floor 3 (Descent): Follow the spiral path downward. Chest 3 (Thunder Rod) is at the bottom of the spiral. Chest 4 (Remedy) is at the base of the stairs.
  • Save Point: At the base of Floor 3, just before the Sealed Gate room.
  • Enemies: Primordite (stone, weak to Lightning), Ninja (swift, can throw swords for big damage), Grenadin (bomb, fire element — don't use Fire).
The Sealed Gate
  • Terra approaches the Sealed Gate with the party. The gate is the passage between the Esper World and the human world.
  • Terra uses her power to open the Gate — Espers flood out into the human world, which has major story consequences.
  • Cait Sith Magicite is obtained from an Esper here. Equip it immediately — it teaches Imp, Reflect, and Hastega (the only source of Hastega in WoB).
Return Path — Imperial Observation Post
  • Exit the cave the same way you came in. Outside, there's now an Imperial Observation Post — it appeared while you were in the cave.
  • The post has 3 chests (X-Potion, Elixir, Thunder Blade) in the side rooms. All worth taking.
  • Fight or flee through the post's guards and return to the airship landing zone. The Imperial ship takes you back west.
Don't miss the dirt clods on the cave floor — they look like regular floor tiles. Check every suspicious-looking spot.
13

The Imperial Banquet

Vector · Imperial Palace ▾
  • Return to Vector. The Empire appears to be extending an olive branch. Celes, Locke, and Setzer attend a state dinner with Emperor Gestahl himself.
The Soldier Hunt (4-Minute Timer)
  • Before dinner, the game gives you 4 minutes to find 24 soldiers scattered around the Imperial Castle grounds. Finding more = better rewards.
  • Soldier locations (work quickly):
    — Banquet hall: 3 soldiers along the walls
    — Kitchen (south of banquet): 4 soldiers near the cooking areas
    — West garden: 5 soldiers patrolling the hedges
    — East gallery: 3 soldiers near the paintings
    — Upstairs (second floor): 6 soldiers in the two side rooms
    — Outside south gate: 3 soldiers near the entrance guardpost
  • Total: 24. Getting all 24 gives the best reward at dinner.
Gestahl's Dinner — Correct Answers
  • The Emperor asks a series of questions during dinner. Your answers determine what additional items you receive:
  • Q1 "Tell me about the Returners": Answer → "They are our allies."
  • Q2 "What about the Espers?": Answer → "We must consider the Espers' interests."
  • Q3 "What about the war?": Answer → "We should stop the war."
  • Q4 Toast: Choose to toast "To the Empire" (not yourself).
  • Best reward (24 soldiers + correct answers): Ward Bangle (defense relic) + Tintinnabulum (Regen effect relic). Both are excellent and obtainable only here.
After the Banquet
  • Gestahl asks you to accompany him to Thamasa. General Leo accompanies the group. The Empire claims they want to negotiate with the Espers.
  • Before leaving Vector: Re-explore the castle — several chests are now accessible including a Gauntlet (front row damage without penalty) in the weapon vault.
Finding 24+ soldiers and choosing correct answers earns the best rewards: Ward Bangle + Tintinnabulum. Fewer soldiers = lesser rewards. Memorize the patrol routes or act quickly.
Correct answer sequence for Gestahl's questions: Show mercy, honor peace, support the ceasefire. The game rewards diplomatic but firm responses.
14

Thamasa & the Esper Cave

Thamasa · Esper Cave ▾
  • Fly to Thamasa (a remote village on a peninsula, northeast of the Serpent Trench area). General Leo accompanies the diplomatic mission.
  • Explore town. Talk to Strago — an old man who knows about the Espers. He and his granddaughter Relm live here.
The Burning Mansion — Do NOT Miss These Chests
  • Overnight, the town's children are trapped in a burning building. Strago rushes in to rescue them. You accompany him.
  • The burning mansion has only 3 rooms. Both chests are permanently missable — get them before reaching Relm.
  • Room 1 (entrance): Fire everywhere. Head east. Chest 1: Flame Rod — in the northeast corner behind flames you can walk through.
  • Room 2 (center): Take the north door. Chest 2: Ice Rod — northwest corner of this room.
  • Room 3 (Relm's location): Find Relm and get the story cutscene. Relm joins your party.
  • Boss: Flame Eater — appears when you try to exit with Relm. HP ~12,000.
    — Absorbs Fire. Weak to Ice.
    — Use the Ice Rods you just collected (throw them as items for ~1,500 damage each), Blizzara spell, Shiva summon.
    — It counters with Fireball — keep HP above 800.
    — Strago observes: Fire Ball Lore can be learned here if Flame Eater uses it with Strago alive.
  • After: Strago and Relm both join your party permanently.
Esper Cave (North of Thamasa)
  • The next morning, the Esper Cave appears to be the source of the Espers' power. Head north of Thamasa on foot (save before entering).
  • Dungeon layout: The cave has collapsing patch-floors (step off them quickly or fall). Navigate carefully — most have solid edges, only the center patches fall.
  • 5 Chests:
    — Chest 1: Hi-Potion (left branch, first chamber)
    — Chest 2: Ether (center right of the patch-floor room)
    — Chest 3: X-Potion (hidden alcove behind a false wall, second patch floor)
    — Chest 4: Magicite Shard (spiral descent section)
    — Chest 5: Elixir (final room before the Espers)
  • Boss: Ultros (final Ultros fight) — Relm can use Sketch on him, which makes him flee immediately and skip the fight entirely. Or fight normally: Fire weakness, HP ~4,800. After the fight: Relm sketches him anyway, providing comic relief.
  • Obtain Starlet (Seraph) Magicite from an Esper after the Ultros encounter.
  • At the cave's deepest room: massive drama unfolds. General Leo confronts Kefka. Watch the cutscene — Leo's fight with Kefka is one of the game's most emotional moments. The outcome changes everything.
  • After cutscene: multiple new Magicite pieces are automatically obtained. Equip them all.
Flame Rod + Ice Rod: Room 1 and Room 2 of the burning mansion. Get both before reaching Relm. Permanently missable once you exit.
Flame Eater: Don't use Fire. Throw Ice Rods as items for fast damage. Shiva summon deals ~2,000+ damage.
The Flame Rod and Ice Rod chests in the burning mansion are permanently missable. Enter the building, grab both immediately, then escape.
Flame Eater: Stack Ice attacks. Shiva deals massive damage. Equip Fire-absorbing armor if you have it.
☑

Step-by-Step Instructions

Each item in the checklist above links directly to its section here. Click → How to get it on any item to jump down.

Chainsaw — Zozo Clock Puzzle
  1. Fly to Zozo — the rainy, perpetually overcast town on the west continent, northeast of Jidoor along the coast.
  2. Every NPC in Zozo is a liar by design. Do not trust the clock hints any of them give you.
  3. Enter the tall building labeled "Inn" (it is not actually an inn). Go up the stairs and find the clock on the wall.
  4. Set the time to exactly 6 hours : 10 minutes : 50 seconds using the clock controls. Dial each value in separately.
  5. A treasure chest appears immediately — open it to receive the Chainsaw.
Jidoor Auction House — Golem & Zona Seeker

Note: only Golem and Zona Seeker are sold at the Auction House. Other espers (Kirin, Unicorn, Carbuncle, Seraph, etc.) are obtained through story events and are not missable.

  1. Jidoor is the wealthy city on the southwest continent, directly south of Zozo. The Auction House is in the northeast corner of town.
  2. Walk up to the auctioneer. Items cycle each time you enter — if neither Golem nor Zona Seeker is up for auction, leave and re-enter to rotate the selection.
  3. When your esper appears, press confirm to bid. Keep bidding — rival bidders fold after 2–3 raises. You'll always win eventually.
  4. Save your game before entering the Auction House in case you run out of gil.
Phantom Esper — Tzen Item Shop
  1. Fly to Tzen — a town on the northwestern coast of the south continent (west of the jungle, easy to spot from the air).
  2. Enter Tzen and go to the item shop. Look for the Phantom Magicite in the shop inventory — it's sold directly for 3,000 gil.
  3. Buy it and equip it immediately on your fastest character. Phantom gives Spd+2 per level-up and teaches Vanish, which makes a character untargetable by enemies.
  4. This shop changes inventory in the World of Ruin and no longer carries Phantom — buy it now.
Tritoch / Valigarmanda — Narshe Snowfield Cliffs
  1. Make sure Terra is in your active party — the fight won't trigger without her present.
  2. Fly to Narshe (the snowy mining town in the far northwest). Land outside and walk in through the front gate.
  3. From inside town, head to the snowfield cliffs — the elevated snowy area above and behind the mine entrance. Follow the path up past the spot where the Moogles defended Terra at the beginning of the game.
  4. At the top you'll see the Frozen Esper still locked in the ice. Approach it with Terra at the front of the party.
  5. A boss fight begins: Tritoch (Valigarmanda). It uses powerful fire, ice, and thunder attacks. Use your strongest magic (Terra's Thundaga works well) and Sabin's Blitzes. Be prepared — this is a real fight.
  6. After winning you receive the Tritoch Magicite. Equip it immediately. Mag+3 per level is the best magic growth in the entire game.
Hero's Ring — Dragon's Neck Colosseum
  1. The Dragon's Neck Colosseum is a small arena located on a peninsula directly south of Jidoor — it looks like a circular building on the coast. Fly there by airship.
  2. Inside the Colosseum, you wager items to fight enemies for better prizes. To get the Hero's Ring specifically, you do not fight here during the World of Balance — the Colosseum becomes fully active in the World of Ruin.
  3. In the World of Balance, the Hero's Ring can also be found in a chest inside the Cave on the Veldt (Dragon's Neck area) — enter the cave at the base of the colosseum peninsula and look for the chest on the right side of the cave interior.
  4. The ring boosts the power of Sabin's Blitz attacks and Celes's Runic ability. Equip it on whichever of those two you use most.
Mog or Golden Hairpin — Narshe Mine (Lone Wolf Event)
  1. After getting the airship, fly to Narshe and enter the town. The Lone Wolf moogle thief (who was locked up in the jail earlier) has escaped and is running through the old mine shafts.
  2. Follow Lone Wolf through the mine passages. He's running through the tunnels with a hostage moogle — keep chasing him.
  3. He reaches a cliff edge and the hostage moogle falls. You must choose to catch Lone Wolf or save the moogle:
    • Save the moogle → that moogle is Mog, who joins your party. He has the Dance command and can wear the Moogle Suit.
    • Catch Lone Wolf → he drops the Golden Hairpin relic, which permanently halves MP costs for the equipped character. Extremely powerful on mages.
  4. You cannot get both in a single playthrough. Mog is also recruitable in the World of Ruin; the Golden Hairpin is not available anywhere else.
Gau — Recruiting from the Veldt
  1. Before heading to the Veldt, visit Nikeah — the port town on the north coast of the south continent. Buy Dried Meat from the item shop there.
  2. Travel to the Veldt — the wide flat grasslands east of the Serpent Trench, accessible by crossing the Trench or flying.
  3. Fight random battles on the Veldt until a wild boy appears and engages you. This is Gau. Do NOT attack him — use Defend, or just wait. He will leap away on his own after a few turns.
  4. Continue fighting random battles on the Veldt. After several encounters, Gau reappears and recognizes you. When prompted, give him the Dried Meat.
  5. Gau joins your party. Use his Leap command on the Veldt to absorb enemy types as Rages — his Rage command lets him mimic monster abilities in battle.
Aqua Rake Lore — Strago from Aspik on the Veldt
  1. Put Strago in your active party and travel to the Veldt.
  2. Wander in random encounters until you fight an Aspik — a blue/purple serpent enemy. They appear fairly frequently on the Veldt.
  3. In battle, let the Aspik use Aqua Rake on the party. Strago must be alive and conscious when the spell hits — if he's KO'd he won't learn it.
  4. Strago learns Aqua Rake automatically after surviving the hit. It deals water/wind damage to all enemies for very low MP — one of the most reliable AoE tools in the game.
Floating Continent — Lv.5 Death, Skip Chests, & Shadow
  1. Lv.5 Death: When selecting your 3-person FC party, include Strago. On the continent, Parasite enemies (floating spiked orbs) will occasionally cast Lv.5 Death. Let them cast it — Strago must be alive and present. He learns it automatically. It instantly kills any enemy whose level is divisible by 5.
  2. Skip Chests 1 & 2: The first two chests on the FC's linear path contain items that upgrade to better gear after the world shifts. Leave them — collect the improved versions in the World of Ruin instead.
  3. Shadow: After defeating Ultima Weapon, a 6-minute countdown begins. Fight your way back to the escape ledge. When you reach the jump-off point, a prompt appears — DO NOT jump immediately. Wait at the ledge. At exactly 5 seconds remaining on the timer, Shadow runs in and joins you. Now jump. If you jump at 6+ seconds, Shadow is left behind and is gone forever from the game.
All Characters Esper-Equipped
  1. Open the Abilities menu from the main menu. Select each character one by one.
  2. Look at the bottom slot — this is the Magicite (Esper) equip slot. It should have an Esper assigned.
  3. If any character shows an empty Magicite slot, assign any Esper to them. Even a basic one is better than none.
  4. Stat bonuses from Espers are applied at each level-up. Any level gained without one equipped is a permanently lost stat point — there is no way to recover it.
  5. Prioritize Mag+2 and Mag+3 Espers (Seraph, Zona Seeker, Tritoch) on your magic users, and Spd+2 Espers (Phantom) on characters who act often.
Edgar's Tools — Figaro Castle Shop
  1. Fly or walk to Figaro Castle — the desert castle on the south continent that submerges underground. Enter from the south gate.
  2. Inside, find the item shop on the ground floor (right side of the entrance hall).
  3. The shop sells all four of Edgar's WoB Tools: Auto Crossbow (hits all enemies), Bio Blaster (poisons all enemies), Drill (ignores defense), and Noise Blaster (confuses all enemies). Each costs a few hundred gil.
  4. Edgar uses Tools for 0 MP with no random chance — they always do exactly what they say. Rotate between them based on the fight: Drill for armored single targets, Bio Blaster for groups, Auto Crossbow for mixed encounters.
  5. Note: Chainsaw and Air Anchor are not in the shop — Chainsaw is the Zozo clock puzzle, Air Anchor was in the Magitek Factory. The four shop tools listed here are never missable.
15

The Floating Continent

Floating Continent ▾
Point of No Return. Once you board the Floating Continent you cannot return to the World of Balance. Complete every item on the Pre-FC Checklist above before proceeding. Save outside before boarding.
Party Selection
  • Choose exactly 3 characters. Strago is strongly recommended — Parasite enemies on the continent use Lv.5 Death, which he can learn as a Lore. This is one of the best Lores in the game and much harder to obtain elsewhere.
  • Good choices alongside Strago: Terra (strong magic), Celes (Runic absorbs the Air Force's Magitek Laser), Edgar (Chainsaw/Drill for physical damage).
  • Avoid having characters at levels divisible by 5 — Parasite's Lv.5 Death will instantly kill them.
Area 1 — Entry Platform (Save Here First)
  • Land on the continent. The Save Point is immediately east of the landing zone — use it before doing anything else.
  • Sky Armor enemies patrol visibly (they move on screen). Engage them: their Missile attack halves one character's HP; their Launcher can inflict Confused status — bring Echo Screens.
  • Chest 1 (Elixir) — grab it, this one does not upgrade in WoR.
  • Head northeast toward the first blue teleporter pad. Step on it to warp to the next platform.
Area 2 — Mid Continent (Strago Lore Zone)
  • This area has Parasite enemies. They roam as visible sprites. Walk into one with Strago in your party — when Parasite casts Lv.5 Death, Strago observes and learns the Lore. Make sure Strago is alive and conscious when the spell fires.
  • Chest 2 — this chest contains equipment that upgrades to a better item if left until the World of Ruin. Leave it if you want the upgrade.
  • Path splits briefly near a bridge. Take either route — they rejoin. Continue to the second teleporter.
Boss: Ultros & Typhon (Mid-Platform)
  • Ultros appears on a bridge. He's comedically trying to drop a 4-ton weight. After a few turns, Typhon (a giant nostril-monster) arrives and starts using Snort to blow party members off.
  • Priority: Kill Ultros before Typhon uses Snort twice. Snort removes a character from the battle permanently (they're fine after, but can't fight here). Use Fire attacks — Ultros is weak to Fire. Edgar's Chainsaw, Terra's Fire magic.
  • If Typhon Snorts everyone off: the battle ends without winning. You can still progress, but it's humiliating.
Boss: Air Force (Upper Platform)
  • Air Force has three components: Laser Gun (left), Wave Cannon (right), and the Air Force body (center).
  • STEP 1 — Destroy the Laser Gun ONLY. When it breaks, it releases the Bit enemy (bestiary entry #112). Record the Bit in your bestiary, then kill it.
  • STEP 2 — Destroy the Wave Cannon. It fires a charge beam every few turns; destroying it eliminates the threat.
  • STEP 3 — Finish the Air Force body with physical attacks. Celes can use Runic to absorb the Magitek Laser spell.
  • Do NOT destroy the Wave Cannon before the Laser Gun — you'll miss the Bit forever.
Boss: Ultima Weapon (Summit)
  • HP ~24,000. Uses Blaze (party fire damage), Quake (party earth damage), and Cutter (single target, deals damage proportional to current HP).
  • Cast Slow immediately — it reduces Ultima Weapon's attack frequency dramatically. This is the single most impactful action in this fight.
  • Use Runic (Celes) to absorb Blaze. Edgar's Chainsaw and Sabin's Bum Rush deal strong physical damage since Ultima Weapon has high magic defense.
  • Below 25% HP, Ultima Weapon enters a counterattack mode — it starts hitting very hard. Be ready with healing.
  • After victory: the 6-minute escape countdown begins.
Six-Minute Escape — Step by Step
  • The timer starts immediately. 6 minutes is actually plenty of time — don't panic, but don't dawdle.
  • Take the LONG ROUTE (go left/around), not the shortcut. The long route has an additional chest at the far end.
  • You'll encounter Naudes enemies on the escape path. They use Lv.5 Death — still risky. Fight or flee quickly.
  • Mini-boss: Nelapa — appears blocking the path. Magic does not work on Nelapa. Use only physical attacks. Edgar's Chainsaw, Sabin's Blitz.
  • Chest 3 (long route only) — grab it on the way through.
  • Reach the escape ledge. CRITICAL: Do NOT jump immediately. Wait here. The timer counts down... at exactly 5 seconds, Shadow leaps over from the rubble and joins you. Jump with him = he's saved. Jump before 5 seconds = Shadow is permanently dead.
  • After jumping: the airship catches the party. The World of Balance ends. The World of Ruin begins.
Shadow (permanent): Wait at the jump ledge until the timer shows 5 seconds. Jump early = permanently gone.
Lv.5 Death Lore: Strago must be conscious when a Parasite casts it in Area 2. Check the Pre-FC Checklist above.
Bit (bestiary): Kill only the Laser Gun in the Air Force fight. The Bit spawns automatically when it breaks — record it before killing it.
🌑

World of Ruin

Kefka has reshaped the world. Everything you knew is ash. But hope isn't dead — and neither are your friends.

16

Solitary Island — Celes Awakens

Solitary Island ▾

One year has passed. You awaken as Celes, alone on a small island with the elderly Cid. This is one of the most emotionally powerful sections of the game.

  • One year after the Floating Continent. You awaken as Celes on a tiny island. Cid is ill and bedridden. There are no other survivors you're aware of.
The Fishing Minigame (Cid's Survival)
  • To keep Cid alive, fish from the dock and bring him food. The fish on the ocean surface have two types:
    — Fast fish (dark color, swim quickly): restore a large amount of Cid's health.
    — Slow fish (light color, move slowly): restore very little and may accelerate his decline.
  • Save before starting to fish if you want to ensure Cid survives. Bring him only fast fish — roughly 6–8 fast fish will keep him alive.
  • If Cid survives: He reveals a hidden raft, gives you a letter about the outside world, and encourages Celes to find the others.
  • If Cid dies: Celes attempts suicide by jumping from a cliff. She's saved by a seagull carrying Locke's bandanna — a sign of hope. Either way the story continues identically from the raft departure. Cid doesn't rejoin either way.
The Island — Hidden Item
  • Before using the raft: climb the island's small cliff path east of Cid's house. At the top is a hidden chest containing an Elixir.
  • The island itself is tiny — there's nothing else to find here.
Leaving the Island
  • Use the raft from the dock. Celes floats northeast and washes up near Albrook on the mainland.
  • The World of Ruin begins properly. Your goal: find all your friends scattered across this broken world.
  • First stop after the island: Head north to Albrook, then follow the road to Tzen.
To keep Cid alive: only bring him the fish that are moving quickly (they appear darker). Slow fish deal more damage to him. Save before fishing if you want to ensure his survival.
17

Tzen — The Collapsing Building & Sabin

Tzen (WoR) ▾
  • Head north from Albrook along the coast road to reach Tzen. A building is collapsing — Sabin is bracing it with his bare hands.
The Collapsing Building — Every Second Counts (But You Have Plenty)
  • The building has a timer (~3 minutes, very generous). You must rescue the trapped child inside and loot the building before it collapses.
  • Floor 1: Enter through the front door. Chests 1–3: X-Potion (left room), Hi-Potion (center room), Tent (right room). Fight or flee the Scorpion enemy (first bestiary entry here).
  • Floor 2: Stairs up. Chests 4–5: Ether (left), Genji Gloves variant (right). Enemy: Zokka (second unique bestiary entry) wanders this floor.
  • Floor 3: Chests 6–7: Elixir (far left), Remedy (far right). Enemy: Nightwalker (third unique bestiary entry) — appears as a random encounter. Make sure to fight one to record it.
  • Child's Room (floor 3, center door): Find the trapped child. Interact to trigger rescue. This starts the "exit sequence."
  • Chest 8 (post-rescue, near the stairs on the way back down): Tincture.
  • Exit the building. Sabin lets it fall. He joins permanently.
8 chests and 3 bestiary-exclusive enemies are inside this building. It is permanently gone after Sabin exits. Take the full 3 minutes — there's no rush if you're systematic.
8 chests and 3 bestiary enemies are inside the building — and it only exists in this one moment. If you leave without looting everything, it's permanently gone.
18

Reuniting with Edgar & Figaro Castle

Nikeah · South Figaro · Figaro Castle ▾
  • Travel to Nikeah. A suspicious merchant in the pub turns out to be Edgar in disguise. Follow him through South Figaro Cave to Figaro Castle.
  • The South Figaro Cave chests you left behind in WoB have now upgraded to their better versions — collect them.
  • Figaro Castle is stuck — its underground engine has been overrun by monsters. Descend into the engine room.
  • Four Tentacle bosses guard the engine — each has a different elemental weakness. Fight them one at a time. Edgar's Tools deal reliable damage to all of them.
  • Collect the Soul Saber from the engine room statue.
  • Move Figaro Castle to Kohlingen for the next story step.
Tentacles: Each arm type has a different weakness — Ice, Fire, Thunder, and Holy. Edgar's Drill works on all of them. Sabin's Blitz (Rising Phoenix) is excellent here.
19

Darill's Tomb & Setzer

Kohlingen · Darill's Tomb ▾
  • After Figaro Castle's engine is cleared, fly/sail to Kohlingen. Setzer is in the pub — haunted by the death of Darill, his rival and love. Another airship, the Falcon, exists — but it's buried in Darill's Tomb.
Darill's Tomb — Navigation & Chests
  • The tomb is southeast of Kohlingen, accessible by foot through the grasslands.
  • Floor 1 (Entrance Hall): Six gravestones with inscriptions. Reading them in the correct order opens the path. The gravestones answer three questions:
    — "What do you want?" → Stone: "Nothing" (interact east wall stone first)
    — "What do you get?" → Stone: "Everything" (center stone)
    — Answer the hidden stone: "How?" → "Death" (northwest stone)
    The correct order reveals the staircase south. Chest 1: Genji Helm (left alcove after the staircase opens).
  • Floor 2 (Gallery): Corridor with coffin alcoves. Chests 2–3: Crystal Mail (east alcove), Regal Gown (west alcove — best female armor at this point).
  • Floor 3 (Lower Tombs): More coffins. Switch on the north wall opens the path to the treasure vault. Chests 4–5: Growth Egg / Exp. Egg (halves EXP on equipped character — wait, it DOUBLES EXP, extremely valuable), Thornlet (useful for specific builds).
  • Save Point: At the bottom of the tomb before the Dullahan room. Use it.
  • Chest 6: Ether (in the room just before Dullahan).
  • Enemy notes: Ghost Train (same as Phantom Train's area, weak to Fire/Phoenix Down), Anemone (status-heavy — Silence and Blind), Specter (heals itself).
Boss: Dullahan
  • HP ~18,000. A headless undead knight who primarily uses magic.
  • Celes's Runic absorbs virtually all his attacks — use Runic every turn as the first action. While it's active he wastes every turn.
  • Have the rest of the party attack physically (Sabin's Bum Rush, Edgar's Chainsaw). He has no particular elemental weakness.
  • If your party can't survive without Runic: keep Celes always casting Runic, two physical attackers, one healer.
The Falcon Airship
  • After Dullahan: the tomb opens to reveal the Falcon airship. Setzer pilots it out and rejoins permanently.
  • The Falcon gives full world exploration — all continents, all islands. This is the point where WoR opens completely.
  • Equip the Growth Egg on whichever character is furthest behind in levels. Switch it around to equalize the party.
Growth Egg (also called Exp. Egg) found here doubles EXP gained. Equip it on characters who need catching up — extremely valuable for grinding.
Dullahan: Celes's Runic is almost a win condition here. Keep using it. When Runic isn't available, use Sabin's Blitz attacks.
20

Mt. Zozo & Cyan

Maranda · Mt. Zozo ▾
  • In Maranda (small town, southern continent), a woman is receiving letters from a soldier at the front — letters postmarked from Zozo. The soldier is Cyan, trapped by grief. Head to Zozo.
Zozo — Buy Rust-Rid First
  • In Zozo's item shop (still full of liars), buy the Rust-Rid item for 1,000 gil. This is the only way to access Mt. Zozo.
  • In the pub building north of the item shop, there's a locked door in the back. Use Rust-Rid on the lock to open it → path leads up to Mt. Zozo.
Mt. Zozo — Navigation & Chests
  • Mt. Zozo is a stormy cliff-face dungeon. Rain hits constantly. Navigate via ladders and rope bridges.
  • Chest 1 (first rope bridge, left alcove): Thunder Shield
    Chest 2 (mid-mountain, cave alcove): Zephyr Cape
    Chest 3 (upper mountain, north cave): Gold Helm
    Chest 4 (near summit, right branch): Aegis Shield
    Chest 5 (locked door room — requires Rust-Rid-opened route): Crystal Mail
  • Key (6th chest): A key is hidden near the summit in a crevice. Pick it up to unlock the locked chest below (backtrack) for a Muscle Belt.
  • Enemies: Punisher (hits hard, weak to Ice), Ralph (fast, use Thunder), Borras (bear, physical). These enemies are tougher than most WoR early enemies — keep HP above 1,000.
  • Optional: Storm Dragon — one of the 8 Dragons guarding the final Eight Dragons challenge. HP ~26,000. Weak to Lightning. Drops Force Armor (best heavy armor). Fight now or return later after collecting all 8 Dragons.
  • Find Cyan at the summit in a small shelter. He's been writing the letters himself, pretending to be Lola's deceased soldier. Emotional scene. Cyan rejoins permanently.
If Cyan is in your active party after joining, you can trigger an optional scene in Maranda involving Lola that adds emotional depth to his story.
21

Gau & the Veldt

Veldt ▾
  • Head to the Veldt in the northeastern part of the world map. Keep one party slot open.
  • During random battles on the Veldt, Gau will appear. Do not attack him — defend or use healing items until the battle ends. He recognizes you and joins.
  • Use Gau's Leap ability to learn all remaining enemy Rages. He should already know many from the WoB, but new WoR enemies are here too.
Gau's best Rages in WoR: Stray Cat (critical physical hit), Magic Urn (free healing), Intangir (powerful damage), Brachosaur (devastatingly powerful late-game).
22

Mobliz & Terra

Mobliz ▾
  • Travel to Mobliz on the southwest continent. Terra is caring for a group of orphaned children in the town's basement.
  • The beast Humbaba terrorizes the area. First encounter: You're meant to lose this fight — let Humbaba defeat the party or fight until Terra intervenes.
  • After the cutscene, form a party and return to fight Humbaba for real. Second fight: Attack aggressively with your best magic and Blitz.
  • After winning, Terra reflects on her purpose and joins your party permanently.
  • Collect the remaining 3 items in the basement hidden room.
Humbaba (second fight): He uses Wind Slash (party damage) and Absolute Zero. Keep HP above 1500. Sabin's Rising Phoenix (fire Blitz) hits his weakness. Terra's Trance + Firaga is devastating.
23

Owzer's Mansion & Relm

Jidoor ▾
  • In Jidoor (northern coast, same town as WoB), find Owzer's Mansion — the large building in the center of town. Owzer is a collector of magical paintings.
Owzer's Mansion — Possesed Paintings
  • Ground floor: The paintings are alive. Examining paintings triggers enemy encounters. These enemies are bestiary-exclusive — fight each painting at least once:
    — Rafflesia (plant, back wall left)
    — Misty (fairy, center wall)
    — Blade Dancer (sword spirit, east wall)
    — Coeurl Cat (right wall)
    — Still Life (living still life, kitchen painting)
  • Upstairs (second floor): Turn on the light switch at the top of the stairs — this reveals shadows in the rooms that hide chests.
    — Chest 1 (east bedroom, shadow near bed): Ether
    — Chest 2 (west study, shadow by bookcase): Rename Card (rare — lets you rename a character)
    — Chest 3 (gallery room, shadow near frame): Memento Ring (auto-undead protection)
    — Chest 4 (attic room, far shadow corner): Behemoth Suit
  • The largest painting at the end of the gallery room — the "Woman in Green" — is the source of the evil. Interact with it to trigger Chadarnook.
Boss: Chadarnook
  • HP ~14,000 (demon form). Chadarnook alternates between two forms:
    — Demon form: Attack this form. Fire weakness — use Firaga, Terra's Trance, Sabin's Aura Bolt. This is the real enemy.
    — Woman form: Do not attack this form. Any attack on the Woman heals the demon. Wait, defend, use items.
  • It alternates forms every 2–3 turns. Attack only during demon form. Heal during woman form.
  • After defeat: Relm was trapped inside the painting. She rejoins permanently.
Chadarnook: Only attack the demon form. If the woman's portrait appears, guard or use items. The demon form has a fire weakness — Firaga and Terra's Trance hit hard.
24

Narshe — Mog, Umaro & Valigarmanda

Narshe (Northern Island) ▾
  • Narshe is now on a far northern island continent. Fly there with the Falcon.
  • Recruit Mog: Find him in the Moogles' Den inside the old mining cave north of Narshe. He joins willingly.
  • Molulu's Charm: Check behind Mog's position in the den to find this accessory — it completely negates random encounters when Mog equips it. Extremely useful for the rest of the game.
  • Head to the Narshe cliffs and teach Mog the Snowman Rondo dance (one of his best).
  • Boss: Valigarmanda (the Frozen Esper) — weak to Fire. Use Firaga and fire Blitz attacks. Obtain the Tritoch Magicite (Mag +3 per level — exceptional).
  • Head deeper into the Yeti's Cave (requires Mog in the party). Fight Tonberry monster-in-a-box for a chance at Minerva Bustier (best female armor).
  • Boss: Umaro — a giant Yeti guarding the Midgardsormr Magicite. Fight him with Mog in the party. After defeating him, Mog talks him into joining.
Equip Molulu's Charm on Mog for the rest of the game whenever you need to traverse old dungeons without random encounters. It's a massive time-saver.
Tritoch (Mag+3) is one of the best Magicite for boosting magic damage. Put it on your main mage immediately.
25

Shadow, Locke & Gogo

Veldt Cave · Coliseum · Triangle Island ▾
Recruiting Shadow
  • Find the Cave on the Veldt — a small cave entrance on the south side of the Veldt. Shadow's dog Interceptor is here, whining. Follow him in.
  • Cave on the Veldt — Chests: The cave is small (2 rooms).
    — Chest 1: Striker (ninja weapon)
    — Chest 2: Ninja Stars
    — Chest 3: Ichigeki (a unique ninja sword — the key to recruiting Shadow)
