  • Shadow's backstory is revealed in flashback dreams here if Shadow is already in your party — revisit with him for lore.
  • Fly to the Dragon's Neck Coliseum (south of Jidoor, same location as WoB). Bet the Ichigeki at the front desk. This triggers a fight in the arena.
  • Arena rules: one character fights alone, controlled by AI. The opponent is Shadow. Your character will fight automatically — equip them with strong armor beforehand. Shadow is fast but manageable at this point.
  • After Shadow is defeated in the arena, he concedes and joins permanently.
Recruiting Locke — Phoenix Cave
  • Phoenix Cave is on the northeast coast of the southern continent — it appears as a cave opening on a volcanic peninsula.
  • This dungeon uses two parties simultaneously. Split your party: Team A and Team B. You switch control between them using a button prompt in certain rooms.
  • Navigation: Team A opens doors/pulls switches that Team B can then pass through, and vice versa. Key coordination points:
    — Team A: pull the left switch to drop the lava bridge for Team B.
    — Team B: open the sealed door to let Team A advance.
    — Both converge at the center chamber where Locke waits.
  • 10 Chests total (5 per team path):
    Team A path: Flame Sabre, Hi-Potion, X-Potion, Elixir, Wing Edge
    Team B path: Fire Knuckle, Phoenix Down, Ether, Crystal Helm, Flame Shield
  • Save Point: Center chamber before the Phoenix encounter.
  • Locke finds the Phoenix Magicite — it's being used to try to revive his lost love Rachel. The scene is devastating.
  • Boss: Guardian (or MagiMaster variant in some versions) — HP ~35,000. Strong magic attacks. Use physical attacks from the stronger team while the other heals.
  • After: Locke takes Phoenix Magicite. He rejoins permanently. Phoenix teaches Raise, Reraise, and Curaga at high rates.
Ragnarok Magicite vs Sword: After Locke joins, fly to Narshe. Only Locke can pick the Narshe weapon shop lock. Inside, a merchant offers Ragnarok as either Esper (teaches Ultima — the most powerful spell) or a sword. Always take the Esper.
Recruiting Gogo — Zone Eater
  • Fly to Triangle Island — a tiny triangular island north of the Veldt in the ocean.
  • Walk around until a Zone Eater appears in random battle. Do NOT flee or kill it. Let it use its Inhale ability on all 4 party members one by one. The whole party gets swallowed.
  • Inside Zone Eater (3-floor stomach dungeon):
    — Floor 1: 3 chests (Relic Ring, Muscle Belt, Heavy Shield). Navigate left/right passages carefully.
    — Floor 2: 3 chests (Genji Armor, Magus Hat, Gale Hairpin). Two false exits — take the center passage down.
    — Floor 3: 3 chests (Mirage Vest, Moogle Suit, Chocobo Suit). Large open room.
    — Collection spots: 6 items gathered from alcoves (Elixir, Tincture ×3, Phoenix Down ×2).
  • Gogo is seated in the last room. Simply talk to him — he joins without a fight. No conditions needed.
  • Exit through the door behind Gogo — it returns you to Triangle Island.
Ragnarok: When the Narshe merchant offers Ragnarok, choose the Esper version (not the sword). It is the only way to learn Ultima — the most powerful spell in the game.
Recruiting Gogo
  • Fly to Triangle Island, a small triangular island north of the Veldt.
  • Encounter Zone Eater in random battles. Allow it to swallow all four party members one by one (do not flee or attack it away).
  • Inside Zone Eater's stomach is a dungeon with 9 chests and a 6-item collection spot.
  • Gogo waits in the final room before the escape. Simply speak to him — he joins without a fight.
26

Strago's Sidequest & Ebot's Rock

Cultists' Tower · Ebot's Rock ▾
  • Find the Cultists' Tower — southeast of the Veldt, along the coast near the Serpent Trench. Strago is inside, brainwashed by Kefka's cult.
  • Bring Relm in your active party. Talk to Strago inside — her voice breaks the cult's hold and he wakes up. He rejoins immediately.
Cultists' Tower (Optional — Worth Doing)
  • The tower has 5 floors of rooms, each containing increasingly powerful magical enemies. The tower is magic-only — physical attacks and items don't work. Only magic can hurt enemies or heal the party.
  • Floor arrangement:
    — Floor 1: Garm (weak), Troll (status magic) → Chest: Ether
    — Floor 2: Living Dead (Holy weakness), Alcyone (wind) → Chest: Elixir
    — Floor 3: Misfit (shadow), Moonform (no weakness) → Chest: Megalixir
    — Floor 4: Magna Roader (thunder), Dark Force (all elements) → Chest: Elixir ×2
    — Floor 5: Boss room
  • Boss: Magic Master — HP ~44,000. An ancient mage casting powerful spells. Weakness: nothing.
    — When killed, he casts Ultima as a final act — massive party damage. Before he dies, ensure one character has Reflect status (from Reflect Ring or the spell) to bounce the Ultima.
    — Or: equip all party with high magic defense and heal immediately after his death.
    — Alternatively: use Death or X-Zone instant kill spells to bypass his Ultima counter.
  • Final chest (top floor): Soul of Thamasa — a relic that lets a character cast magic twice per turn. One of the most powerful relics in the game. Equip on your strongest mage (Terra or Celes).
Ebot's Rock — Getting Grand Delta
  • Ebot's Rock is an island cave southeast of Thamasa. Bring Strago — Grand Delta is a Lore he MUST witness in person.
  • The cave is a maze with randomly shuffled rooms. Each time you enter a room, the next one is different. Navigate patiently.
  • Throughout the cave, examine shining spots on the floor — each gives you a piece of Coral. You need exactly 22 pieces.
  • A large chest in the center of the cave is blocking the path to Hidon. It demands Coral to move. Feed it all 22 pieces (interact and choose to feed it). It opens.
  • Boss: Hidon — Strago's white whale. HP ~19,000. He's accompanied by 4 ElephanToad adds that keep healing him.
    — Kill the adds first with AoE magic (Thundaga, Blizzaga) — they have low HP but heal fast.
    — Then focus Hidon. He uses Grand Delta during the fight — Strago MUST be alive when it fires to learn the Lore.
    — If Strago is KO'd when Grand Delta fires: he cannot learn it. Keep him healed with priority.
Grand Delta (Lore): Strago must be conscious when Hidon casts Grand Delta. There is no other source for this Lore. Keep Strago alive throughout the Hidon fight.
Grand Delta is ONLY learned from Hidon in Ebot's Rock. There is no other source. Strago must be alive and present in the battle when Hidon uses it (or use Anticipate/Reflect methods).
27

Cyan's Dream Sequence

Doma Castle (Dream) ▾
  • Fly to Doma Castle (east side of the WoR continent, near where Doma was in WoB). Enter with Cyan in your active party. Sleep in any of the castle beds — the dream sequence triggers automatically.
Dream Dungeon — Sequence & Items
  • The dream world mirrors real locations from earlier in the game but distorted. You recruit the three other party members (Terra, Celes, and a third) within the dream before the dungeon proper begins.
  • Phantom Train Dream Cars (3 cars, switch puzzles):
    — Car 1: Switch on left wall opens east car door. Chest: Genji Glove (left alcove).
    — Car 2: Switch on right opens passage forward. Chest: Lump of Metal (examine the engine mechanism).
    — Car 3: Two switches must be toggled in order (left then right). Chests: Gauntlet, Assassin's Dagger.
  • Magitek Cave section: Navigating abandoned Magitek armor corridors. 3 chests: Crystal Shield, Crystal Helm, Magus Hat. Several enemy encounters here — strong magic users.
  • Doma Dream Castle interior: Navigate through mirror-image Doma. Find Cyan's wife Elayne and son Owain — they're alive in the dream world. The emotional resolution of Cyan's arc.
  • Save Point: At the entrance to the final Wrexsoul room.
Boss: Wrexsoul
  • Wrexsoul possesses party members and hides inside them. While possessing someone, Wrexsoul is untargetable.
  • Strategy to force Wrexsoul out: Use X-Zone, Doom, or Banish spells on your own KO'd party members. This doesn't kill them (they're already KO'd) but forces Wrexsoul to re-emerge.
  • Alternatively: use Stop status on a possessed character — this freezes Wrexsoul in place, allowing targeting.
  • When Wrexsoul is visible: Blizzaga deals massive damage (he's weak to Ice). Kill him quickly before he re-possesses someone.
  • After Wrexsoul: Cyan makes peace with his grief. He wakes. His Bushido charge times are permanently reduced — techniques now charge in roughly half the time, making him much more practical.
Wrexsoul: Use the X-Zone spell or Doom on your own party members to force Wrexsoul out of hiding. Then blast it with Blizzaga.
After completing Cyan's Dream, his Bushido skills charge much faster — making techniques like Mindblow and Quadra Slam actually practical to use.
28

Late-Game Sidequests & Prep

World of Ruin — Various ▾
Ancient Castle
  • Park Figaro Castle over the desert south of the Kohlingen area. The prison trapdoor inside Figaro's dungeon now connects to the Ancient Castle passage. Enter the dungeon from Figaro's prison cell.
  • The passage has 4 chests: Elixir, Protect Ring, Ether, Full Moon. Navigate the one-way corridors to reach the Ancient Castle proper.
  • Ancient Castle layout: Throne room, west gallery (blue Esper mural), east dungeon (locked cell area), lower vault.
    — Chest 5: Excalibur (throne room, right alcove — the legendary Holy-element sword)
    — Chest 6: Genji Armor (lower vault, south door)
  • Boss: Blue Dragon (Eight Dragons optional fight) — HP ~26,600. Weak to Lightning. Uses Blizzaga and Ice-element breath. Defeat it for Force Robe (one of the best robes in the game).
  • Alexander Magicite: Found in the throne room's statue room — interact with the queen statue to receive it. Teaches Holy.
  • Odin Magicite: Found in the lower vault. Odin himself is petrified — interact with the statue for Odin Magicite.
  • Upgrading Odin to Raiden (teaches Quick): From the throne room, walk south exactly 5 steps from the throne chair, then interact with the floor. A hidden staircase opens revealing a small room with a second queen statue. Examine it — Odin's Magicite transforms into Raiden, who teaches Quick (double turn for one character — one of the most broken spells in the game).
Deathgaze (Airship Boss)
  • Fly the airship over the world map and steer into random air battles. One of these will trigger Deathgaze — an optional flying boss.
  • Deathgaze may flee — keep flying and you'll encounter him again. His HP carries over between encounters.
  • Weak to Fire. Defeating him grants Bahamut Magicite (teaches Flare, HP+50%).
  • Avoid having any party member at a level divisible by 5 — Deathgaze's Lv. 5 Death spell will instant-kill them.
Cursed Shield → Paladin Shield
  • The Cursed Shield can be found in Narshe (WoR). It inflicts every status ailment on the wearer each fight.
  • Equip it and complete 256 battles while wearing it — it transforms into the Paladin Shield, the best shield in the game (absorbs most elements, teaches Ultima at x1 rate).
Training Tip
  • The Dinosaur Forest (north of Doma Castle) has high-level enemies: Tumbleweed, Tyrannosaur, Brachosaur. They give massive EXP and AP. Equip the Growth Egg for double EXP.
  • Target level 50+ for all characters before Kefka's Tower. Focus on building Magic stat via Esper choices.
Before Kefka's Tower: Make sure you have Ultima learned on at least 2–3 casters, Phoenix equipped for auto-revival, and all characters above level 45.
29

Kefka's Tower — The Final Dungeon

Kefka's Tower ▾

The culmination of everything. Kefka's Tower is a massive, multi-team dungeon — the longest and most complex in the game. There is no return once you enter, so be thoroughly prepared.

Before Entering
  • All 14 characters should be recruited. If any are missing, get them now.
  • Equip Phoenix Magicite on key characters — its auto-raise ability triggers on KO.
  • Bring Megalixirs, Ethers, and status-healing items in bulk.
  • Ensure Strago has learned Grand Delta and Force Field (Force Field is only in the tower).
Pre-Entry Checklist
  • Recruit all 14 characters before entering. Miss any and you've locked yourself out — some story encounters (Mog, Umaro) require Narshe; Gogo requires Triangle Island; Shadow requires Veldt Cave + Coliseum.
  • Strago is critical: He must be in Team 2 to learn Force Field Lore (only source in the game) AND he should already know Grand Delta from Ebot's Rock.
  • Equip Phoenix Magicite on one character per team — Phoenix's auto-revival (Reraise) can trigger on KO and save a run.
  • Stock: 20 Megalixirs (if you have them), 20 Ethers per mage, 15 Phoenix Downs per team, Ribbons on your most critical characters.
  • Have Ultima learned on at least 2 characters. It's the most powerful spell in the final boss fights.
  • No return once you enter. Final save is outside Kefka's Tower.
Team Assignment Strategy
  • Split 12 characters into 3 teams of 4. You switch between teams at specific points in the dungeon — all must advance together to unlock the final area.
  • Team 1 (recommended: Celes, Edgar, Sabin + tank): Navigates the lower Magitek corridor area. Less dangerous path but needs a healer and physical damage.
  • Team 2 (REQUIRED: Strago + 3 others): Prison/jail dungeon path. Strago must be here for Force Field Lore. Other recommended: Terra, Locke, Relm.
  • Team 3 (recommended: physical fighters): Catwalk exterior. Faces the Inferno boss and Skull Dragon (8th Dragon). Needs your strongest physical attackers: Shadow, Cyan, Umaro work well.
Team 1 Path — Magitek Corridor
  • 3-floor mechanical corridor. Enemies: Prometheus (mechanical, weak to Water), ProtoArmor (physical tank), Mega Armor (ranged attacks).
  • Chests 1–2: Maximillian (best heavy armor for Edgar/Cecil), Aegis Shield. Located in side alcoves at the end of floors 1 and 2.
  • Pull the central lever at the corridor's end to lower the platform for Team 2's path to clear. Then wait for the team-switch prompt.
Team 2 Path — Prison Wing (Strago Required)
  • 4-section dungeon with cell blocks and magic barriers. Enemies include: Dark Force (cast magic only — physical does nothing), Misfit (shadow), Inferno's minions.
  • Lores for Strago (learn all three here):
    — Quasar: Learned from the Ultima Buster boss at the section's end. Strago must be alive when it fires.
    — Lv.? Holy: Learned from Alluring Rider enemies in the cell block area.
    — Reflect???: Learned from Dark Force enemies. Reflect some magic back at it.
  • Boss: Ultima Buster — HP ~55,000. Extremely powerful. Uses Quasar (party magic damage), Flare Star, and Ultima. Keep your entire team above 2,500 HP at all times. Use Sabin's Phantom Rush or Terra's Trance + Ultima for maximum damage.
  • Chests 3–4 in the prison wing: Crystal Mail, Genji Shield.
Team 3 Path — Catwalk & Factory Exterior
  • Exterior catwalks exposed to magical storms. Enemies: Outsider (magic), Dragon (various elements), Covert (fast, Invisible).
  • Boss: Inferno — HP ~44,000. Three components: Inferno (body), Striker (right arm), Rough (left arm). Kill both arms first — they protect the body and counter attacks. Then destroy the body with everything you have.
  • Skull Dragon (optional, 8th of 8 Dragons) — on the catwalk section. HP ~26,200. Weak to Holy (Alexander summon). Completes the Eight Dragons challenge if you've fought all others.
  • Chests 5–7: Ribbon (possibly most valuable item in the game — prevents all status ailments), Crystal Orb, Holy Lance.
Button Puzzle — Force Field Lore (Missable)
  • All three teams converge in a central room with 3 large buttons. The buttons control which boss encounters are triggered.
  • Press the LEFT button first with Team 2 (the team with Strago). This spawns the Fiend encounter. During this battle, Fiend uses Force Field — Strago observes it and learns the Lore.
  • Force Field raises the party's elemental resistances — extremely useful for the final boss fights. This is the only way to learn it in the entire game.
  • After Fiend: press the middle and right buttons to clear the Guardian and Goddess bosses with the other teams. All three boss battles are straightforward compared to the final boss.
  • Final Chest (Ribbon) — south of the Goddess battle room, in a small alcove. Don't miss it.
Final Boss Gauntlet — Kefka
  • After the three button bosses, a long staircase leads to Kefka. Save at the save point just before the final ascent.
  • Tier 1 — Warring Triad (three entities): Attack all three. Target Lady (center) with physical, Hit (right) with magic, Demon (left) with magic. Exploit their weaknesses with the appropriate element. HP ~30,000 each.
  • Tier 2 — Strange Creatures: A group of smaller forms. Sweep with Ultima or Morph + magic. HP totals ~50,000 combined.
  • Tier 3 — Power / Magic / Wisdom: Three floating entities. Each uses a different attack type. Bring down HP of all three simultaneously — if one falls too far ahead, the others power up. HP ~10,000–18,000 each.
  • Tier 4 — Kefka (True Form): The god of magic in his final form. HP ~62,000.
    — Uses Light of Judgment (massive party damage, ~3,000+), Havoc Wing (party damage), and Delta Attack (petrification).
    — Spam Ultima. Each cast hits for 4,000–9,999. Two casters with Soul of Thamasa (double cast) can deal 20,000+ damage per round.
    — Keep all party members above 3,500 HP before each of his turns. Phoenix auto-revival will trigger on deaths.
    — Mages: Ultima spam. Fighters: Sabin's Phantom Rush, Shadow's Throw, Edgar's Chainsaw.
    — Victory brings one of gaming's most celebrated endings.
Force Field Lore (Strago): Only available from the Fiend boss in Kefka's Tower. Strago MUST be in Team 2 and the left button MUST be pressed. No second chance.
Kefka: All four forms have high HP and use powerful magic. Ultima from multiple casters ends each form quickly. Keep Reraise on key characters. This is the moment the whole game builds to.
After defeating Kefka, enjoy the ending. The final scenes for each character are tailored to their story arc — one of the most celebrated JRPG endings of all time.

— The End —

Final Fantasy VI Pixel Remaster · Complete Walkthrough

Research based on RPG Site, GameFAQs (bover_87 guide), The Gamer, and Screen Rant resources.

Complete Walkthrough · 22 Jobs · Every Missable Spell

Final Fantasy V

✦ ✦ ✦
Pixel Remaster Edition

The definitive job-system RPG. Mix and match 22 jobs across four characters to build any party imaginable. This guide covers all three worlds, the complete job system, every Blue Magic spell, and every missable item — from the Wind Shrine to the Cleft of Dimension.

✦

Introduction & Essential Tips

▾

Final Fantasy V is the definitive expression of JRPG class customization. Four heroes, 22 Jobs unlocked by shattering elemental Crystals, and a villain named Exdeath who wants to return everything to the void. The Pixel Remaster is the first official Western PC release of the original 16-bit version, with redrawn sprites and rerecorded music.

What Makes FF5 Unique
  • The Job System: Every character can equip any job. Mastering a job unlocks its abilities to use on other jobs. This is the entire game — experiment constantly.
  • ABP (Ability Points): Like EXP but for jobs. Every battle earns ABP. Higher-tier abilities cost more ABP to unlock.
  • Freelancer & Mime: Freelancer inherits the best passive stat bonuses of any mastered job. Mime copies the previous character's action for free. Both are game-changing.
  • Blue Magic: One of the most powerful spell sets in the game. Blue Mages learn spells by surviving enemy attacks — Strago's equivalent, but far more impactful.
  • Crystals unlock jobs in stages: There are four Crystal events per world, and each shattering unlocks a new batch of jobs. You can't get every job in World 1.
Essential Tips
  • Switch jobs constantly. Early on: Knight + Monk for offense/defense, White Mage for healing. Once you unlock Mystic Knight and Time Mage, re-evaluate everything.
  • Equip Blue Mage early. Many Blue Magic spells are only catchable in specific areas. Miss the window and they're gone.
  • Galuf is a permanent party member until World 2's emotional midpoint. Do not neglect his ABP — it transfers to Krile when she joins.
  • The Brave Blade and Chicken Knife are mutually exclusive. Choose one. Brave Blade is stronger statically; Chicken Knife scales with runs.
  • Before the Cleft of Dimension, complete Fork Tower, get Leviathan, and prepare for Omega (the hardest fight in the game).
⚔

The Job System — All 22 Jobs

▾

Jobs are unlocked by shattering Crystals throughout the three worlds. Each job has a set of abilities you unlock with ABP — and once learned, those abilities can be equipped as sub-abilities on any other job.

World 1 Jobs — Wind & Water Crystals
Knight
Wind Crystal · W1
Heavy armor, Swords, Cover. Key ability: !Guard (auto-protect). Mastery: Equip Shields on any job.
Monk
Wind Crystal · W1
Highest HP/Str. Fights bare-handed. Key: !Kick (AoE). Mastery: HP+30%.
Thief
Wind Crystal · W1
!Steal, !Flee (escape guarantee). Mastery: Agility+2 on Freelancer.
Blue Mage
Wind Crystal · W1
Learns enemy spells (Blue Magic). Best AoE damage, support, and utility spell list. Learn spells by surviving enemy attacks.
White Mage
Water Crystal · W1
Full heal/status cure line. !White (all white spells). Mastery: Magic+3 on Freelancer.
Black Mage
Water Crystal · W1
Best direct damage magic. !Black. Mastery: Magic+3. Pair with Spellblade for devastating results.
Time Mage
Water Crystal · W1
Haste, Slow, Stop, Meteor, Gravity. Essential for most boss fights. Mastery: Magic+2.
Summoner
Water Crystal · W1
Call powerful Espers (Syldra, Shiva, Ramuh, Golem, Leviathan). Strong with !Summon. Mastery: Magic+2.
Red Mage
Water Crystal · W1
Mixed black/white spells + swords. Key: !Dualcast (cast twice per turn). Mastery: !Dualcast ability.
World 1 Jobs — Fire & Earth Crystals
Berserker
Fire Crystal · W1
Auto-attacks with axes — can't be controlled. High damage, inflicts Berserk. Mastery: Equip Axes on any job.
Mystic Knight
Fire Crystal · W1
!Spellblade: enchants sword with a spell element. Spellblade + Flare on a Ninja with dual wield = one of the strongest builds in the game.
Beastmaster
Fire Crystal · W1
!Catch and !Release monsters. Releasing certain creatures does massive damage. Niche but fun.
Geomancer
Fire Crystal · W1
!Gaia: terrain-based random attack. Passive: walks on damage floors. Low ABP cost, solid early.
Ninja
Earth Crystal · W1
Equip two weapons simultaneously (dual wield!). !Throw (inflicts heavy damage). Top-tier physical damage job in the whole game.
Ranger / Hunter
Earth Crystal · W1
!Rapid Fire: attacks 4 times at half damage each. Excellent with elemental arrows. Mastery: Equip Bows on any job.
Bard
Earth Crystal · W1
!Sing: buffs party with sustained songs (Regeneration, Magic Power). Very powerful late-game support.
Dancer
Earth Crystal · W1
!Dance: randomized dances with strong effects. Ribbon's Dance can deal massive damage. Less reliable but fun.
World 2 Jobs
Samurai
World 2 · Bal
!Zeninage (Gil Toss): destroys enemies with money. Very powerful; bring lots of gold. !Mineuchi: stuns. Mastery: Equip Katanas.
Dragoon
World 2 · Bal
!Jump: invulnerable airborne attack. Excellent with elemental spears. Mastery: Equip Spears on any job.
Chemist
World 2 · Bal
!Mix: combine items for devastating effects. Mix Elixir+Elixir = Hi-Ether. Many combinations. !Drink: temporary stat boosts.
Mime
World 2 · Kelger's
Copies the previous character's action for 0 MP. Synergizes with Summoner, Spellblade Ninja, and Chemist builds. Can't equip other abilities.
Special Jobs (Always Available)
Freelancer
Always unlocked
Default job. Inherits the highest passive bonuses of any mastered job. End-game Freelancers with mastered Knight/Monk/Ninja are terrifying.
Mime
World 2 (see above)
Copies the last party member's action. No ability slots but inherits passive mastered job bonuses like Freelancer.
✦

Blue Magic — Key Spells & Where to Learn Them

▾

Blue Magic is learned when Strago — sorry, when a Blue Mage — survives being hit by an enemy's spell. The character must be in the active battle party and must be alive and conscious when the spell hits them. Here are the essential ones:

Must-Get Spells
  • White Wind — Heals the party for HP equal to the caster's remaining HP. Best healing tool in the game. Learned from Enchanted Fan (Ronka Ruins, W1) or Aevis enemies (W1).
  • Aqua Breath (Aqua Rake) — Heavy water/wind AoE damage. Learned from Hydra (Karnak area, W1) or Exocite. Absolute workhorse spell for most of W1 and W2.
  • Death Claw — Reduces one target to single-digit HP and paralyzes it. Learned from Gargoyle (Ronka Ruins, W1). Sets up any finisher.
  • Level 5 Death — Instantly KOs all enemies whose level is divisible by 5. Learned from Level Checker (Walse Tower, W1). Trivializes enormous stretches of the game.
  • Mighty Guard — Casts Protect + Shell + Float on the entire party for free. Learned from Stingray (Merged World sea, W3) or Siren. One of the best spells in any FF game.
  • Moon Flute — Berserks the entire party (they attack randomly but with massive power). Pair with Level 5 Death or Death Claw for instant wins. Learned from Moon Bear (W2).
  • Aero — Solid wind-element damage. Learned from Drippy (W1 grasslands) or Wind Drakes.
  • ??? (What) — Deals damage equal to (9999 - your current HP). Best used at low HP. Learned from Dhorme Chimera or Page 32.
  • Self-Destruct — The caster sacrifices themselves to deal massive damage. Learned from Bomb-type enemies.
  • Magic Hammer — Drains 25% of target's MP. Useful against magic-heavy bosses. Learned from Mu (W1).
Always keep a Blue Mage in your party during new areas — many Blue Magic spells are location-specific and cannot be obtained later.
💎

World 1 — The Four Crystals

The Wind Crystal has shattered. Four adventurers are drawn together by fate. Unlock jobs, collect Blue Magic, and stop Exdeath's forces from destroying the remaining Crystals.

⚔

Equipment Reference & Boss Guide

▾
Key Weapons to Acquire
Brave Blade
World 3 — exclusive choice
Starts at highest attack in the game (~150 Atk) but loses 1 Atk for every time you flee battle. Never flee if keeping this. Best raw attack if you avoid all running. A high-Strength Knight or Ninja with Brave Blade + Two-Handed deals devastating damage.
Chicken Knife
World 3 — exclusive choice (vs Brave Blade)
Starts weak but gains 1 Atk for every battle you flee from. Maxes at 127 Atk + forces you to flee when attacking normally (unless the Brave Blade mechanic is understood). However: Chicken Knife + Rapid Fire quadruple-attacks ignoring the flee penalty = enormous total damage. The preferred choice for most builds.
Hermes Sandals
Fork Tower reward
Auto-Haste for one character — the single most powerful accessory in the game. Equip on your main attacker (Ninja with Rapid Fire, or the Spellblade user). A Hasted Ninja dealing 4× Rapid Fire attacks per turn is the game's most consistent damage output. Do Fork Tower before the Rift.
Kornago Gourd
Mix ingredient
When a Chemist Mixes Turtle Shell + Dragon Fang → Turtle Soup (Shell + Protect on party). Turtle Shell + Turtle Shell → Dark Ether. Multiple Mix combinations become essential for Omega/Shinryu fights. Stock ingredients before the Rift.
Enhancer
World 3 shop — Mage sword
The Enhancer (also called Rune Blade) significantly boosts Magic power — equip it on a Mystic Knight with Spellblade to combine physical and magic attack in one hit. At endgame, Spellblade Flare on a Ninja with Dual Wield + Rapid Fire is one of the highest single-turn damage combinations in the game.
Magus Rod
World 2 shops
Best rod for Black Mage — boosts magic damage. Equip on whoever is casting Flare or Holy. Magic Lamp (World 2 item) summons Espers in order (Ramuh → Shiva → Ifrit → Titan → Odin → Bahamut → Leviathan → Syldra) — once depleted the magic lamp is spent. Use it on tough early bosses.
Summons (Summoner class)
Syldra
Story — Faris's ship
Wind/Water AoE. Faris's childhood companion. Very powerful early game. Obtained automatically through story. Excellent through World 1.
Carbuncle
Optional — Island Shrine
Casts Reflect on all party members — the entire party becomes immune to single-target magic. Extremely powerful against magic-heavy bosses like Exdeath's final form. Bosses then hit themselves with their own reflected spells.
Golem
Optional — World 2 auction
Erects a physical damage barrier absorbing all physical hits to the party. Invaluable for protecting against physical-heavy bosses. Buy at the Mua auction house. Stacks with Protect for near-invulnerability to physical.
Leviathan
Optional — Sea battle
Tidal Wave — massive Water AoE. Triggered by sailing into the storm near Surgate Castle in World 3. One of the most powerful summons. Fight him to earn it — he's a mid-tier boss at that point.
Bahamut
Optional — North Mountain W3
Mega Flare — the most powerful summon in FF5. Non-elemental, hits all enemies. Required for Neo Exdeath final boss. Found atop North Mountain in World 3. Fight Bahamut (hard fight) to unlock. Essential acquisition before entering the Rift.
Odin
Optional — World 3 castle
Zantetsuken (instant KO all enemies) or a physical AoE. 1-minute time limit to kill Odin before he kills you. Use Hasted fighters with Rapid Fire to beat the timer. Works on trash, fails on bosses. Worth having for dungeon clearing.
Boss Quick Reference
Wingraptor · Wind Shrine
HP: ~650 · Wind weak (grounded)
Opens closed-winged (physical attacks deal no damage to wings) and grounded. Attack body when wings are closed. When it opens wings, hit the wings with magic. First time the game forces you to understand target selection.
Karlabos · Ship
HP: ~700 · Lightning weak
Crustacean boss on the ship. Uses Tail Screw (reduces one character to single-digit HP). Heal immediately when Tail Screw hits. Thundara from Time Mage or Thunder scrolls wrecks him.
Siren · Boat
HP: ~900 · Switches element
Switches between human form (use physical) and undead form (use Fire/Holy, physical heals her). Watch for the form change mid-fight. Keep at least one Fire spell equipped at all times during this fight.
Soul Cannon · Karnak
HP: 10,000+ · Cannons
Surrounded by two Fire Cannons. Destroy the Fire Cannons first — they attack every round. Then focus on the main body. This fight has a time limit (Karnak Castle escape countdown). Move fast.
Atmos · Dungeon
HP: ~20,000 · Comet
Mid-game boss. Uses Comet (random heavy damage to the party). Attacks 3 party members and drags them into the void — party shrinks during the fight. Carbuncle summon reflects his magic back. Rush him down with Rapid Fire.
Exdeath · World 2 Finale
HP: ~32,768 · Varies
Uses Holy (heavy magic), Vacuum Wave (HP-halving), and heavy physical. Golem absorbs his physical hits. Carbuncle reflects his Holy back at him. Bahamut for sustained AoE magic damage. Keep party above 1,500 HP always — Vacuum Wave to physical combo is lethal.
Omega · Cleft of Dimension
HP: ~55,000 · Optional superboss
One of the hardest bosses in Final Fantasy history. Uses Wave Cannon (HP to single digits for all), Encircle (removes one character), and Atomic Ray (massive fire). Strategy: Reflect Rings on all four → Berserk the whole party (prevents Encircle from targeting) → Chemist Mix potions for healing. Omega takes 10–15 minutes to whittle down even optimally. Reward: 1 ABP per kill (modest but the bragging rights are the real reward).
Neo Exdeath · Final
HP: 50,000 (4 parts)
Four-part final boss. Each part has different HP and attacks. The Grand Cross part uses random devastating effects on all characters. The Almagest part (also in FF6) deals 9,999 to all. Strategy: Carbuncle reflects most magic. Focus on the Grand Cross and Almagest parts first — they're the killers. Bahamut + Rapid Fire Ninja = highest DPS. Win in 6–8 rounds.
Shinryu · Cleft of Dimension
HP: ~33,000 · Optional
Optional superboss in a chest in the Cleft. Opens with Tidal Wave (party ~4,000 water AoE) then Blaze (~3,000 fire to all). Equip Coral Rings (lightning absorb) — Shinryu uses Aqua Breath (water+lightning). Dragon Kiss + Ice Lance from Dragoon deals ~9,999. Dragon-type enemy — Dragoon's Dragon Kiss (Dragon's Breath) does full damage. Reward: Ragnarok (strongest weapon in Shinryu's chest, renamed Dragon Seal in some versions).
1

Wind Shrine · The Job System Awakens

Wind Shrine ▾

A meteorite crashes near Tycoon Castle. Bartz, a wandering traveler and his chocobo Boco, meets Princess Lenna and the amnesiac old man Galuf. Together they investigate the Wind Shrine to find Lenna's sister Faris — then the Crystal shatters and the job system begins.

  • Explore the Wind Shrine (a tower dungeon). Enemies are weak — use the time to get comfortable with the battle system.
  • Boss: Magissa + Forza — Magissa attacks first alone; defeat her before Forza joins. If Forza appears, he picks her up and heals her. Focus Magissa down first. Physical attacks work fine.
  • The Wind Crystal shatters, releasing four jobs: Knight, Monk, Thief, Blue Mage. Assign them immediately.
  • Recommended starting setup: Bartz → Knight, Lenna → White Mage (unlock next), Galuf → Monk, Faris → Blue Mage. Adjust once more jobs are available.
Set Faris as Blue Mage immediately — she should stay Blue Mage until you learn Aqua Breath and White Wind. Missing these early spells is one of the most common FF5 mistakes.
2

Torna Canal & Walse Castle

Torna · Walse ▾
  • Pass through the Torna Canal. Boss: Karlabos — a giant crustacean. It uses Tail Screw to drop characters to 1 HP. Cast Slow first, then attack with everything. Finish fast.
  • Visit Carwen (the port town east of the canal) and buy the best equipment available.
  • Cross the sea to reach Walse Castle on the western continent. Explore the castle — there's a hidden room behind the throne with a chest.
  • The Water Crystal is atop Walse Tower (a tall tower north of Walse town). Climb it.
  • Boss: Garula (top of Walse Tower) — A giant rhino charging repeatedly. Use Knight's Guard on the charge turns. Physical attacks, Fira if available.
  • The Water Crystal shatters, unlocking five more jobs: White Mage, Black Mage, Time Mage, Summoner, Red Mage.
  • Side quest: The Walse Tower basement has a hidden chest containing the Brave Blade — one of the two weapons in the Brave/Chicken Knife choice event. Note its location for later.
The Brave Blade or Chicken Knife — you can only get ONE. The Brave Blade starts strong but weakens each time you flee. The Chicken Knife grows stronger with each flee. Decide your playstyle and commit.
3

North Mountain & Karnak

North Mountain · Karnak ▾
  • The party is drawn to the North Mountain after a hiryuu (wind drake) is spotted. Climb the mountain — Blue Magic opportunity: let Faris get hit by Aero from Wing Raptor to learn it.
  • Boss: Magissa + Forza (if not fought before) or Forza alone — Use the same strategy. Defeat Magissa before Forza joins.
  • Rescue the wounded hiryuu and arrive at Karnak. You're immediately arrested by the local garrison — don't panic, it's scripted.
  • The town of Karnak has some of the best equipment in World 1. The Fire Crystal is near Karnak Castle — fight your way through the castle interior.
  • Boss: Iron Claw — Transforms between forms. Use physical attacks on the Iron Claw form; it counters magic. Kill the human form first if he splits.
  • The Fire Crystal shatters: Berserker, Mystic Knight, Beastmaster, Geomancer unlock.
At Karnak: unlock Mystic Knight immediately and start learning Spellblade LV1-LV3. Pairing Spellblade with dual wield later is the most powerful physical setup in the game.
4

Fire Ship & Library of the Ancients

Fire Ship · Library ▾
  • Board the Fire Ship — a massive burning vessel threatening Karnak. You have a time limit. Grab as many chests as possible on your way through.
  • Boss: Liquid Flame — Changes form each turn: humanoid (use ice), tornado (magic only), hand (any). Use Blizzara and Aqua Breath. If you have White Wind, keep HP topped.
  • After the Fire Ship: the Library of the Ancients is a dungeon disguised as a giant library. Wandering enemies here include the Magna Roader (train enemy) — let it hit Faris to learn Level 5 Death.
  • Blue Magic window: Page 32 enemies teach ??? (What) spell. Let Faris take the hit.
  • Boss: Ifrit — Fight the fire summon and win to obtain the Ifrit summoning magicite. Use Blizzara/Aqua Breath. After Ifrit is defeated, he joins as a summon.
  • Boss: Byblos — A bookworm boss that seals abilities. Use physical attacks only (magic will be sealed early). Drain MP with !Magic Hammer if available.
Level 5 Death is one of the strongest Blue Magic spells in the game. If you miss it at the Library (from Magna Roaders or Level Checker at Walse), you may not see it again until late in World 2.
5

Earth Cave & Lonka (Ronka) Ruins

Earth Cave · Ronka Ruins ▾
  • Travel to the Jachol Cave / underground area to reach the southern continent. Standard dungeon — open all chests.
  • Visit Crescent and Jachol towns to buy updated equipment and rest.
  • The Earth Crystal is guarded in the underground Lonka (Ronka) Ruins. Reach them by the hiryuu (wind drake) after it recovers.
  • Blue Magic opportunity: Enchanted Fan enemies in Ronka Ruins use White Wind. This is the BEST heal in the game — must-get. Have Faris survive the hit.
  • Blue Magic: Gargoyle enemies here use Death Claw — get it. It reduces enemies to 1 HP and paralyzes them.
  • Boss: Archeoaevis — Changes elemental weakness each turn. Use !Scan (if you have it) or just alternate element spells. Aqua Breath + Blizzara rotation works.
  • The Earth Crystal shatters, unlocking: Ninja, Ranger, Bard, Dancer, Freelancer, Mime.
  • Immediately after: the Void opens and the party is hurled into World 2.
White Wind from Enchanted Fan in Ronka Ruins is one of the best healing spells in the whole game. Do NOT miss this window. If you can't survive the hit, use a Reflect Ring to bounce the attack off an ally to the Blue Mage.
Archeoaevis: Bring Summoner with Ifrit/Shiva for alternating elements. If he resists a turn, switch element. Aqua Breath for off-element turns. Keep White Wind topped.
🌿

World 2 — Galuf's World

Separated from Lenna, Bartz, and Faris, Galuf returns to his own world to rally resistance against Exdeath. Samurai, Dragoon, and Chemist jobs await — and one of the most emotional moments in all of Final Fantasy.

6

Exdeath's Forest — Galuf Alone

Big Bridge · Exdeath Forest ▾

Galuf arrives in his own world after being captured by Exdeath. He escapes from Exdeath's dungeon and reunites with his granddaughter Krile (Cara). The World 1 party eventually arrives by meteorite to join him.

  • Play as Galuf alone (or with Krile) for a short sequence. He retains all his ABP from World 1 — his jobs and abilities are intact.
  • Reach Castle of Bal (Galuf's kingdom) to link up with the rest of the party.
  • Collect the Samurai, Dragoon, and Chemist jobs from the sealed tablets inside Bal's vault.
  • Visit Kelger's Village — the wolf-people settlement. Kelger fights Bartz in a brief duel and unlocks the Mime job.
Immediately start using Samurai (!Zeninage) — it costs gil, but Gil Toss destroys most of World 2's regular enemies instantly. Farm gil from battles and spend it on damage.
7

Castle of Bal & Big Bridge — Gilgamesh!

Castle of Bal · Big Bridge ▾
  • The party uses a submarine to cross to the mainland where Exdeath's Castle is located. Storm the castle.
  • After pushing through Exdeath's Castle, you chase Exdeath across the iconic Big Bridge — a massive structure spanning the ocean.
  • Boss: Gilgamesh (1st Fight) — The recurring silly samurai rival makes his debut. He has multiple weapons and attacks physically. Use Haste on your party and hit him with Spellblade attacks. He's challenging but survivable.
  • He retreats. The party boards the airship Hiryuu to continue chasing Exdeath.
  • Visit Regole and Mua Forest (the forest town of animal people) — buy new equipment and heal.
  • Gilgamesh fights again before Exdeath's Castle dungeon — same pattern but stronger. Beat him again.
Gilgamesh is a recurring fight that must be triggered by crossing the Big Bridge at the right time. If you somehow skip the bridge sequence, you miss his fights — though this requires deliberate sequence-breaking. Follow the story naturally and you'll face him.
Gilgamesh Fight 2: He uses a variety of weapons and can inflict confuse. Equip Ribbons or accessories with confusion immunity if you have them. Haste + Spellblade Fira/Thundara + Rapid Fire is devastating here.
8

Hiryuu Valley & Ghido's Cave

Hiryuu Valley · Ghido's Isle ▾
  • Travel to Hiryuu Valley — a mountain canyon where the wind drakes roost. Lenna's chocobo father has been cursed here.
  • Boss: Hiryuu — The corrupted wind drake. Use Esuna to remove the poison effect and it calms down. After the fight, Hiryuu evolves into a powerful Dragon and joins as transportation.
  • Fly to Ghido's Island — the tiny island home of the sage turtle Ghido, an ancient wise man who has lived for 700 years.
  • Ghido reveals the location of the Ancient Library and gives key story lore about Exdeath's nature (he is a tree that absorbed evil souls).
  • The party gains access to more of the world map after Ghido's cave. Continue toward Moore Forest.
9

Moore Forest — Galuf's Sacrifice

Moore Forest ▾

Moore Forest is one of Final Fantasy V's most beautiful locations — and home to its most emotional story beat. Do not rush through it.

  • Enter Moore Forest, a magical living forest with the Crystal Tablets inside.
  • Solve the tree-spirit puzzle to navigate deeper into the forest. Open all side chests — there are several hidden on off-path branches.
  • Boss: Exdeath (first full fight) — Exdeath appears in his armored form. He uses powerful magic (Meteor, Flare) and physical attacks. Use Haste + Spellblade Flare + Rapid Fire. White Wind for recovery. This is a tough fight — don't be ashamed to use multiple Elixirs.
  • Exdeath activates a barrier that KOs three party members. Only Galuf is left standing. Play the solo Galuf sequence — he cannot be healed by items or spells, but he cannot die until he chooses to. Keep attacking.
  • After the cutscene: Galuf dies. This is permanent. Krile (Cara) joins, inheriting all of Galuf's jobs, ABP, and equipment.
Galuf's death is story-scripted — it cannot be prevented. However, all his ABP (spent and unspent) transfers to Krile. Grind ABP on Galuf before Moore Forest to give Krile a head start on abilities.
The solo Galuf fight: He auto-revives on every hit — this is scripted invincibility. You can't lose. Just use all your strongest attacks on Exdeath and enjoy the scene. Galuf's max HP is displayed but effectively infinite here.
10

Crystals' Lair — World 2 Endgame

Exdeath's Castle · Lair ▾
  • With Krile in the party, storm Exdeath's Castle for the final time. It's a multi-floor dungeon with strong enemies — bring Elixirs.
  • Navigate to the top of the castle and through the Crystals' Lair — the inner sanctum where the last Crystal tablets are held.
  • Boss: Gilgamesh + Enkidu (3rd Fight) — Gilgamesh now fights with his ally Enkidu. Focus Gilgamesh; Enkidu heals him if Gilgamesh gets low. Kill Enkidu first. Exdeath intervenes and boots Gilgamesh out for good.
  • The final Crystals shatter. Exdeath merges the two worlds into one — the Merged World (World 3) begins. Many towns are destroyed; the world map is dramatically rearranged.
Before the Crystals shatter, make sure you have: all Blue Magic you wanted from World 2 enemies, ABP grinding done for key jobs (especially Chemist's !Mix and Mystic Knight's Spellblade LV4), and full stock of items.
☑

Pre-Rift Checklist — Before Entering the Cleft

▾

Once you enter the Cleft of Dimension (the Rift), you cannot return to the Merged World. Complete all World 3 sidequests before going in.

Critical — Do Before the Rift
  • Fork Tower — Located on the merged world map west of Tycoon. Split your party — physical fighters go up one tower, mages go up the other. Reward: Mirage Vest (auto-reflect) or Hermes Sandals (auto-haste). Hermes Sandals are arguably the best accessory in the game.
  • Leviathan — The legendary sea serpent summon. After Moore events, a storm triggers near the Surgate coast. Sail into the storm to fight him. Boss: Leviathan — Use Thundara and Aqua Breath (it's water-immune but Aqua Breath still does wind damage). Win to get the Leviathan summon.
  • Brave Blade / Chicken Knife — Go to the Merged World's Walse area. An NPC will offer you one of the two legendary weapons. The Brave Blade weakens by 1 ATK each time you flee; Chicken Knife grows by 1 ATK each flee. Choose wisely.
  • Sunken Walse Tower — Walse Tower is now underwater on the world map. Dive in with the submarine. It contains rare equipment and the optional boss Neo Exdeath's prototype. Very challenging — bring your best build.
  • All 22 Jobs mastered (or at minimum all jobs unlocked) — Every character should have their core jobs at high ABP before entering the Rift. Freelancer's power comes from mastered jobs.
Optional But Recommended
  • Omega (optional superboss) — Found in the Cleft of Dimension. An ancient mechanical war machine. You can technically fight it once you enter the Rift. Strategy: Equip all Reflect Rings. Berserk your entire party (so Grand Cross doesn't affect them). Use !Mix to make Hi-Potions and Elixirs. Omega is one of the hardest fights in all of Final Fantasy.
  • Shinryu (optional superboss) — Also in the Cleft. A dragon with Maelstrom (drops HP to critical) and devastating physical attacks. Use Coral Rings (lightning absorb) for his wave attacks. !Dragon Kiss (from Dancer) + Ice Lance on Dragoons works well.
  • Blue Magic: Mighty Guard — From Stingray enemies in the merged world sea. The best support spell in the game (Protect + Shell + Float). Do not miss this.
  • Odin summon — Available in the Merged World. Fight Odin in the castle where he's sealed — you have one minute to kill him before he uses Zantetsuken and kills you. Reward: Odin summon (insta-kill all enemies, can miss bosses).
  • Bahamut summon — Fought at the top of the North Mountain in World 3. Strong party + high level required. Reward: Bahamut, the most powerful summon in the game (Mega Flare).
Once you enter the Cleft of Dimension, the world outside is gone forever. Fork Tower, Omega/Shinryu (fight them inside the Rift), Brave/Chicken Knife — get everything before stepping in.
🌀

World 3 — The Merged World & The Rift

Two worlds collide into one. Exdeath controls the Void. Seek out the legendary weapons, finish your job mastery, and prepare for the Cleft of Dimension — the final dungeon.

11

The Merged World — Reorientation

Merged World ▾

The two worlds have fused into one massive continent. Towns are repositioned or destroyed. New enemies with new Blue Magic populate the world. This is the final exploration phase before the Rift.

  • Visit all new towns for updated equipment. Kuzer and Surgate are key towns with late-game gear.
  • Find the Submarine — needed to access the Sunken Walse Tower and other underwater locations.
  • The world map is dramatically changed — some old towns are islands now, others are merged coastlines. Use the world map to orient yourself.
  • Blue Magic hunt: The Merged World has many new enemies. Key spells: Mighty Guard (Stingray, sea enemies), Dragon Force (Dragon enemies, boosts damage enormously), Refrain (Bard-type enemies, raises Berserk status party), Guardian (rare support spell).
  • Farm ABP here — World 3 enemies give much better ABP than earlier areas. Focus on finishing Mystic Knight, Ninja, Chemist, and Summoner job mastery.
12

Sunken Walse & Fork Tower

Sunken Walse · Fork Tower ▾
  • Sunken Walse Tower: Dive to the old Walse Tower location, now underwater. Use the submarine. Contains some of the best loot in World 3, including rare equipment and a tough optional boss. Bring full Elixir stocks.
  • Fork Tower: Two parallel towers — the Tower of Magic (left) and the Tower of Strength (right). The restriction: physical characters can only go in the Strength tower, magic users only in the Magic tower. Split your party accordingly.
  • Magic Tower boss: Omniscient — Counters all magic with powerful spells. Use physical attacks only. Bring a Knight or Samurai.
  • Strength Tower boss: Minotaurus — Counters all physical attacks. Use magic only. Bring a Black Mage or Summoner.
  • Completing Fork Tower rewards: Mirage Vest (auto-Reflect on wearer, protects from many magic attacks) and Hermes Sandals (auto-Haste every battle — one of the best items in the game).
Hermes Sandals grant Auto-Haste permanently. Equip them on your hardest-hitting character. If you skip Fork Tower before the Rift, these items are gone forever.
13

Pyramid of Moore

Pyramid · Moore ▾
  • The Pyramid of Moore rises from the desert. Inside, Exdeath is trying to recover five legendary sealed items. If he gets them, they'll strengthen him. You must collect them first.
  • Navigate the pyramid, which is a multi-floor dungeon with strong enemies and undead. Bring Elixirs and Phoenix Downs.
  • Collect all five sealed tablets before reaching the top. If Exdeath gets one, it powers him up (but the game continues — it's not a game-over condition, just harder).
  • Boss: Exdeath (Pyramid) — Same Exdeath fight pattern. Use Spellblade + Rapid Fire or Zeninage. White Wind for recovery. He's tough but manageable with Haste.
  • After the pyramid: the story leads directly to the entrance of the Cleft of Dimension.
If Exdeath absorbs a sealed item, he gains a powerful new attack form. Getting all five before him makes the final battle easier. Prioritize the chests over enemies — run from battles if needed.
14

Cleft of Dimension — The Final Dungeon

Cleft of Dimension · The Rift ▾

The Cleft of Dimension (also called the Rift or the Void) is the final dungeon of FF5. It is divided into distinct biomes, each with unique enemies, and ends with the hardest boss in the game: Neo Exdeath.

  • Zone 1 — The Forest: Tree and plant enemies. Bring fire. Blue Magic opportunity: learn any remaining spells from enemies here.
  • Zone 2 — The Library: Page-type book enemies. They can seal abilities temporarily — use !Gaia or physical attacks when sealed.
  • Zone 3 — Waterfall: Water and undead enemies. Heavy use of status effects — equip Ribbons or Coral Rings.
  • Zone 4 — Castle: The most complex zone with branching paths. Contains the strongest regular enemies. The treasure rooms here hold final-dungeon-tier equipment.
  • Omega is found here — an ancient robot. It uses Encircle (instant KO), Mustard Bomb, and various elements. Strategy: Berserk your party, equip Reflect Rings, use Dragon Kiss. Very optional.
  • Shinryu is in a chest in the Rift — opening the chest triggers the fight. He opens with Tidal Wave (massive water damage). Bring Coral Rings. Then use Dragoon jump with Dragon Lances.
  • Final Boss: Exdeath (True Form) — Exdeath merges with the Void itself. He has high HP, multiple status attacks, and Almagest (holy-element party damage).
  • Final Boss: Neo Exdeath — Four separate parts, each needing to be destroyed. The Grand Cross attack inflicts random status effects on the party. Critical: All four parts must be killed — if you leave any alive, they can resurrect the killed parts. Use AoE magic or AoE Spellblade attacks to hit all four simultaneously.
Neo Exdeath Strategy: Give everyone Ribbons (or Protect Rings + Hermes Sandals). Use Quick + Spellblade Holy/Flare on Ninja with dual wield. Summon Bahamut. Lenna with Dualcast + Flare. Faris as Chemist for Mix Heroism (boosts attack). Grand Cross is the key threat — status immunity via Ribbon is essential.
If you have Mighty Guard as a Blue Magic spell, open every boss fight by casting it. Protect + Shell + Float on the entire party for free is invaluable in the Rift.

— The End —

Final Fantasy V Pixel Remaster · Complete Walkthrough

Research based on GameFAQs (peewee or Nemesis guides), FFV Advance documentation, and community wikis.

Complete Walkthrough · 12 Characters · Surface, Underground & Moon

Final Fantasy I V

✦ ✦ ✦
Pixel Remaster Edition

Cecil Harvey's journey from Dark Knight to Paladin spans three worlds: the war-torn surface, the molten underground, and the ancient moon. Twelve characters join your party — most temporarily — in a story built on betrayal, redemption, and the threat of an alien god named Zeromus.

✦

Introduction & Essential Tips

▾

Final Fantasy IV is a story-driven linear RPG — your party members are fixed and change throughout the narrative. Unlike FF5 and FF6 there is no customization; each character has a unique role. The Pixel Remaster uses the original SNES difficulty (not the Easy Type version) with modern QoL features.

Key Rules to Know
  • Save constantly. FF4 has some sudden, brutal difficulty spikes (Golbez's Shadow Dragon, Zeromus in Dark Form).
  • The ATB bar never stops. Enemies attack while you navigate menus — learn to be decisive.
  • Characters leave and return. Don't over-invest in gear for characters who will depart soon (Edward, Tellah, Palom/Porom, Yang).
  • Cecil's job change at Mt. Ordeals is one-time and automatic — you cannot return to Dark Knight.
  • Augments (DS/3D version feature) are NOT in the Pixel Remaster — characters have fixed abilities.
  • Speed toggle is available — use 2× for grinding, switch to 1× for bosses.
Missable Items Overview
The Pixel Remaster removes most of the original's permanent missables. Virtually all items can be found in multiple locations or obtained later. The main things to watch: Rare item drops from unique enemies, and making sure you grab the Adamant Ore from the Mythril area before advancing past the Giant of Bab-il.
✦

Characters & Abilities

▾
Cecil Harvey
Dark Knight → Paladin
Main hero. Starts as a physical attacker who drains his own HP with Darkness. Becomes a Paladin at Mt. Ordeals — full heal-capable tank with Cover and Holy spells.
Kain Highwind
Dragoon
Jump deals 2× damage and makes him untargetable. Leaves and rejoins multiple times due to Golbez's mind control. One of the best physical attackers late-game.
Rosa Farrell
White Mage / Archer
Primary healer. White magic up to Arise and Holy. Aim for a near-guaranteed hit with her bow. Essential for the endgame.
Rydia
Summoner / Black Mage
Rejoins in the underworld grown up. Has all Black Magic + Summon magic. Gets new summons by finding monsters. The most powerful magic user in the game.
Tellah
Sage (temporary)
Joins twice, leaves twice. Has Meteo (uncasted until Golbez fight). Very limited MP — do not rely on him heavily.
Edward Chris
Bard (temporary)
Weakest combatant. Salve doubles item healing and targets all party members. Hide makes him untargetable. Story-important but don't gear him up.
Yang Fang Leiden
Monk (temporary)
Incredible physical power, poor magic. Kick hits all enemies. Leaves after Mt. Hobs, returns briefly, then leaves again permanently (though his wife gives you rewards later).
Palom & Porom
Black/White Mage (temp)
Twin mages. Palom has Bluff (doubles next magic hit). Porom has Cry (lowers enemy defense). Leave permanently after the Antlion fight — they petrify themselves to save you.
Cid Pollendina
Engineer
Lowest magic, decent physical. Analyze reveals enemy stats and weakness. Leaves temporarily when he crashes the Enterprise; returns on the Underworld surface.
Edge Geraldine
Ninja
Dual-wields, fast, can Throw weapons and items for massive damage. Ninjutsu magic (Flood, Blitz, Smoke, etc.) learned automatically. Gets weaker as the game scales up unless you keep his gear current.
FuSoYa
Lunarian (temporary)
Joins on the moon. Has nearly every spell in the game but very limited MP. Leaves after the Giant of Bab-il segment. Use him freely — he won't be there long.
Golbez
Shadow Mage (final act)
Joins for the very end of the game alongside FuSoYa. Extremely powerful but present for only one major fight. Cast Meteor and watch.
☑

Missables Checklist

▾
The Pixel Remaster is very generous — most items can be found again. These are the things still worth watching for.
  • Shuriken & Fuma Shuriken (Edge) — Limited supply found in chests. Once used with Throw they are gone. Hoard them for the hardest bosses.
  • Summons for Rydia — Leviathan (boss fight on the water), Bahamut (Bahamut's Lair on the moon). Both are missable only if you skip their areas entirely, which you can't do in a normal run.
  • Spoon (Adamant Ore quest) — Talk to the dwarf in the Mythril area, give him the rat tail from the Feymarch to get Adamant Ore. Forge it into the Adamant Armor (best armor in the game) at Kokkol's Forge before the endgame.
  • Rare drops — Some enemies in the Lunar Subterrane drop exclusive equipment. If you want 100% gear, check a dedicated item FAQ.
⚔

Equipment Reference, Summons & Boss Guide

▾
Best Weapons (Endgame Party)
Cecil — Paladin
BEST: Ragnarok / Lightbringer
Ragnarok is the strongest sword for Cecil in the Pixel Remaster. Found in the Lunar Subterrane treasure chests. Crystal Sword and Excalibur are strong mid-tier options. The Paladin class can cover (take hits for a KO'd ally) and use White Magic L1–L3 — equip accordingly. Never equip Dark weapons after class change.
Kain — Dragoon
BEST: Longinus / Holy Lance
Kain's Jump deals 2× weapon damage while airborne. Longinus and Holy Lance are both found in the Lunar Subterrane. Equip elemental spears against appropriate enemies — Blizzard Spear against fire-immune bosses. Kain's Jump is safe during boss AOE phases (he's untargetable while airborne).
Rosa — White Mage
BEST: Artemis Bow
Artemis Bow is Rosa's best weapon for its Aim command accuracy. Rosa's primary role is healing — White Magic L8 includes Curaja, Holy, and Arise. Her bow attack is secondary; prioritize her spell casting. Equip Rune Armlet for Magic boost and White Robe for Spirit/defense.
Rydia — Summoner
BEST: Change Rod / Stardust Rod
Rydia's weapon choice is cosmetic — her damage comes entirely from Black Magic and Summons. Stardust Rod boosts magic damage and is the best weapon for her. Equip Protect Ring and Ribbon for status immunity. Rydia has access to all Black Magic levels and all Summons — she's the most powerful character in the game.
Edge — Ninja
BEST: Masamune / Murasame (×2)
Edge dual-wields — equip a strong weapon in BOTH hands. Murasame × 2 (dual Katanas) maximizes physical damage. If Masamune is available (from a chest in the Lunar Subterrane), equip it in the main hand with Murasame off-hand. Edge's Throw command uses Shurikens — hoard them. Ninjutsu spells (Flood, Blitz, Smoke) are learned automatically.
Rydia's Summons — Complete List
Chocobo
Storyline · Chocobo Village
Chocobuckle — inflicts Paralysis. Low damage. Early game only. Replaced quickly by better summons.
Shiva
Optional · Underground Waterway
Diamond Dust — Ice-element AoE. Strong against fire enemies. Effective through most of the game against appropriate targets. Easily obtained in the mid-game.
Ramuh
Optional · Sylvan Cave
Judgment Bolt — Lightning AoE. Good early summon. Replaced later by Indra but still useful for lightning-weak enemies.
Ifrit
Optional · Mt. Ordeals area
Hellfire — Fire-element AoE. Strong against ice enemies. Medium power level mid-game.
Titan
Optional · Underground
Gaia's Wrath — Earth AoE, instant KOs some enemies. Inflicts Earth damage — useless against flying enemies or bosses with immunity. Good against non-boss ground enemies.
Odin
Baron Castle · Story
Zantetsuken — attempts instant KO on all enemies. Works on regular enemies, fails on bosses. Useful for trash clearing. Rydia gets this automatically from story progression in Baron.
Sylph
Optional · Sylph Cave
Whispering Wind — deals damage to all enemies AND heals all party members for the same amount. One of the most useful summons for long dungeons — damage-dealing with built-in party heal. Found in Sylph Cave in the Underworld area.
Asura
Optional · Feymarch
Random effect: Protect+Shell+Haste OR Curaja OR Life on random party member. Useful when you need all-purpose support. The Feymarch is optional but highly recommended — also yields the Rat Tail for the Adamant Armor quest.
Leviathan
Required · Overworld sea
Tidal Wave — massive Water AoE damage. One of the most powerful summons. Rydia is swallowed by Leviathan on the ocean — this triggers in a story event. She returns from the Feymarch later, now grown up, with Leviathan and Asura learned.
Bahamut
Optional · Bahamut's Lair (Moon)
Mega Flare — the most powerful summon in FF4. Non-elemental, hits all enemies for massive damage. Found on the Moon in Bahamut's Lair — fight Bahamut to earn the summon. Essential for the Zeromus final boss fight. Must-get before the endgame.
Mist Dragon
Story · Given to Rydia
Inherited from Cecil's story in Mist Village. One of FF4's most emotionally significant summons. Mist Breath hits all enemies. Moderate power level but the backstory context makes it notable.
Cockatrice / Lich / Plague
Feymarch / Dungeon chests
Status-effect summons. Cockatrice inflicts Petrify, Lich inflicts Doom (countdown KO), Plague inflicts multiple status effects. All situationally useful for bosses vulnerable to status; mostly niche picks outside of specific encounters.
Boss Quick Reference
Mist Dragon · Mist Cave
HP: 1,000 · Ice weak
First boss. Phases in and out of mist form — only attack when solid. Kain's Jump during the mist phase (he's safe airborne). Cecil's physical hits when it solidifies. Shiva deals bonus damage when available.
Antlion · Antlion's Den
HP: 1,000 · No weakness
Uses Needle (heavy single-target damage). Steal from him with Edge later (if revisited) but during the story fight just burst with physical. Palom's Bluff (doubles next magic hit) + Porom's Cry (lowers defense) combo before Tellah casts — surprisingly effective.
Golbez's Shadow Dragon · Story
HP: ~20,000 · Scripted
This fight is scripted — Golbez crushes the party. Rydia appears and summons Mist Dragon to save everyone. It doesn't matter how much damage you deal before the cutscene. Do not use limited resources here.
Cagnazzo · Bahamut's Lair
HP: ~5,000 · Lightning weak
Water Archfiend. Absorbs water, weak to Thunder. He pulls in to charge Tsunami (party AoE water) — attack physically during the charge (magic doesn't interrupt it). Palom + Porom Twincast deals massive damage if they're in your party. Rydia's Ramuh summon wrecks him.
Four Elemental Archfiends · Giant
HP: ~7,000 each
Rubicante (fire), Cagnazzo (water), Barbariccia (wind), Scarmiglione (dark). Each appears in the Giant of Bab-il. Rubicante heals the party before fighting out of honor — use the healing. Barbariccia curls into a tornado; only Jump and physical work during tornado form. Edge's Flood tech destroys Rubicante. Rydia's opposite-element summons handle each.
Zeromus · Final
HP: ~50,000 · Hard mode
The true final boss — Golbez's Crystal reveals Zemus's true form as Zeromus. He's invincible until you use the Crystal item. Uses Big Bang (party AoE ~2,000 to all), Black Hole (removes all buffs), and Flare (single ~1,500). Rydia: Bahamut every round (~3,000 AoE). Rosa: Curaja every round — keep everyone above 4,000 HP before Big Bang. Edge: throw Shurikens. Kain: Jump. Cecil: Cover Rosa during critical HP moments. Big Bang followed by Black Hole removing your buffs is the deadliest combo — re-apply Protect immediately.
1

Baron & the Mist Village

▾
Party: Cecil, Kain
  • Start in Baron Castle. Cecil is stripped of command of the Red Wings after refusing Golbez's orders. He and Kain are sent to deliver a package to the Mist Village.
  • Mist Cave (dungeon between Baron and Mist Village): 2 floors. 4 chests: Potion (×2), Tent, Ether. Enemies: Mist Claws (weak to Fire), Bombs (do not let them Self-Destruct — kill fast).
    — Boss: Mist Dragon — Becomes mist when physical attacks land. When it dissipates, do not attack — wait for it to solidify, then hit it. Use Kain's Jump to deal safe damage during mist phase. HP ~600.
  • Arrive at Mist Village. The Carnelian Signet package triggers an explosion — Bomb Ring destroys the village. Cecil's guilt begins. Rydia's mother (the Mist Dragon) dies from the explosion.
  • Rydia attacks Cecil. She's defeated but KOs Kain in the process. Rydia joins your party (by accident). Kain is separated.
  • Travel south to Kaipo. Rosa is at Kaipo's inn, delirious with Desert Fever — she needs Sand Ruby from the Antlion's Cave to recover.
  • Antlion's Cave is north of Kaipo. Short dungeon (2 floors). 3 chests: Hi-Potion, Maiden's Kiss, Silver Apple (raises max HP permanently — collect these always).
    — Boss: Antlion — Normally docile (doesn't attack), but using physical attacks triggers its counterattack mode. Use magic only (Rydia's Mist summon, Cecil's Darkness skill). HP ~1,500.
  • Return to Kaipo with Sand Ruby. Rosa is cured and joins the party.
Young Rydia can only use summons and Black Magic (which she'll gradually learn). She's fragile — keep her in the back row. Her Mist Dragon summon (Whyt) and early summons like Chocobo/Shiva are effective early-game tools.
2

Kaipo, Waterway & Damcyan

▾
Party: Cecil, Rydia → + Tellah → + Edward
  • Kaipo: Rosa is sick in Kaipo — she has desert fever and needs the Sand Ruby to recover. Cecil promises to find it. The Antlion's Cave in the desert nearby has one.
  • Waterway (underground canal, 3 floors): Enter from the waterfall south of Kaipo. Tellah joins here — he's a Sage searching for his daughter Anna who ran off with "some bard" to Damcyan. He's furious about it. Enemies: Coeurl (Paralysis attack — cure it immediately), Alraune (plant, weak to Fire). Chests: Ether ×2, Hi-Potion ×3, Antidote ×4. Three floors connecting underground to the Antlion desert area.
Antlion's Cave — Sand Ruby
  • Floor 1: Desert cave. Enemies: Antlion Guard (regular enemies, weak to Water). Head east to the boss chamber.
  • Floor 2 (Boss): The Antlion is normally docile and won't attack first. However: if you use any physical attack on it, it retaliates with Poison Sting on the whole party. Use magic only — Rydia's summons (Chocobo, Sylph) or Tellah's Fire spell work perfectly.
Boss: Antlion — ~2,000 HP
Behavior: Passive unless physically attacked; then uses Poison Sting (party AoE poison)
Strategy: Rydia's Chocobo summon or Shiva. Tellah: Fire. Rydia is your best damage dealer here — use her summons freely. One or two summon casts and the Antlion falls without ever retaliating.
Reward: Sand Ruby (cures Rosa's desert fever back in Kaipo).
Damcyan — Story Cutscene
  • Travel to Damcyan Castle (northeast of Kaipo across the desert). The Red Wings bombed it on the way there — the castle is burning and mostly destroyed when you arrive.
  • Edward and Anna are found among the rubble. Anna is Tellah's daughter (the bard she ran off with was Edward, prince of Damcyan). Anna is fatally wounded and dies in Edward's arms — and in front of Tellah. Tellah blames Edward, strikes him, and vows to learn Meteo to destroy Golbez.
  • Edward joins your party — heartbroken, weak, but determined. Use his Salve command (uses one Potion to heal all four characters) — it's extremely efficient for HP conservation early on. His Hide ability makes him untargetable (useful when enemies focus on him since he has low HP).
  • Chests in Damcyan ruins: Lute (Edward's instrument), 600 Gil, Dry Ether.
Fabul Castle — Defend the Crystal
  • Travel northwest to the Fabul martial arts kingdom. Yang (Master Monk) is training here — he joins the defense of the Fabul Crystal.
  • Wave Defense Battle: A sequence of combat encounters against wave after wave of Red Wing soldiers. You must win each round to protect the Crystal. Between waves, use Salve (Edward) and Cure (Tellah) to keep everyone up. Yang's Kick hits all enemies and is excellent against the groups.
  • Final wave — Kain: Under Golbez's mind control, Kain appears as the final wave. He defeats the party in a scripted cutscene — regardless of how well you fight, he takes the Crystal and abducts Rosa. The party is thrown overboard. Ship sinks. Everyone washes up separated on different shores.
Don't over-equip Edward — he will leave soon. When the ship sinks: Rydia is lost (temporarily), Tellah separates, Yang is found washed up on another shore. You wake up in Mysidia as Cecil alone.
3

Mt. Hobs, Mysidia & the Twins

▾
Party: Cecil + Tellah → Cecil, Tellah, Edward → Cecil, Tellah, Yang
  • After Fabul's invasion by the Red Wings, the party escapes by ship to Mysidia. A storm sinks the ship — Rydia and Tellah are separated, Yang is found on a shore.
  • Mt. Hobs (north of Mysidia area): Yang is here, mind-controlled by Golbez, blocking the pass. Rydia surprises everyone by returning — she's grown up, summoned from the Feymarch (time flows differently there). She yells at Yang to snap him out of it. Yang joins.
    — Boss: Mom Bomb — A giant bomb blocking the pass. Don't use Fire (heals it). Physical attacks only. When its HP drops, it explodes into multiple Small Bombs — kill them all quickly or they chain-explode. HP ~3,500.
  • Mysidia: Cecil is despised here — the Red Wings stole the Crystal. The Elder of Mysidia sends Cecil to Mt. Ordeals as atonement. Twin mages Palom (Black Mage) and Porom (White Mage) accompany to spy on him.
  • Mt. Ordeals (the most important dungeon in Cecil's arc): 4 floors of undead enemies — heal spells damage them.
    — Floors 1–3: straightforward. 5 chests: Hi-Potion, Elixir, Dry Ether, Dark Crystal, Ether.
    — Floor 4 (Summit): Cecil faces his dark self — his shadow reflection. Attack it: when it uses Darkness to drain HP, respond with Cure spells. The shadow can only be defeated by Cecil himself (other party members' attacks are less effective).
    — Cecil becomes a Paladin. His Dark Sword becomes the Paladin equipment. He gains the ability to use White Magic and can no longer use Darkness.
    — Tellah remembers Meteo at the summit — but his current MP is too low to cast it. He awaits the right moment.
  • Return to Mysidia. Then travel to Baron Castle.
    — Boss (Baron Gatehouse): The Guards — two strong guards block the gate. Cecil's new Paladin Holy attacks are effective. Beat both simultaneously.
    — After: the walls begin to close. Palom and Porom petrify themselves to stop them. They are turned to stone permanently. Do not over-equip them — their gear cannot be recovered.
Palom and Porom permanently leave the party petrified to save you. Don't equip them with rare items you want to keep — you lose everything they have equipped at this moment.
4

Baron Revisit & Tower of Zot

▾
Party: Cecil, Yang, Tellah → + Cid → + Kain + Rosa
Baron Castle — Cagnazzo Revealed
  • Return to Baron after Cecil's Paladin transformation. The guards who loyally followed Cecil in the opening now recognize his returned honor and step aside.
  • The King of Baron acts strangely hostile — this is because the "King" is not the King. He is Cagnazzo, the Fiend of Water, who killed the real King and took his place to manipulate the Red Wings for Golbez.
  • Chests in Baron Castle: Elixir ×2, Ether ×3, Darkness Sword (Cecil's old sword — you can equip it but it's weaker than Paladin gear). Pick up everything before the fight.
Boss: Cagnazzo (Water Fiend, Fake King) — ~6,500 HP
Weakness: Thunder/Lightning
Mechanic: When Cagnazzo "Absorbs Water" (draws water into his shell), stop all physical attacks — he will counter with Tsunami (massive water AoE). Only attack when his shell is open.
Attacks: Tsunami (party-wide ~800 water damage when triggered), physical strikes
Strategy: Rosa: cast Shell on party first (halves magic damage — critical for Tsunami). Cecil: physical when shell is open. Yang: Kick (hits all). Tellah: Thundara (ignore the shell restriction for magic — Thunder directly damages him). The fight is easy if you watch the Absorb Water cue.
  • After Cagnazzo: Cid (the head engineer of Baron) breaks in with a group of rebel engineers. He's furious that his airship fleet was used for evil. He joins and upgrades the Enterprise airship with a Magnet Hook — allowing you to fly up and latch onto the Tower of Zot (Golbez's floating fortress where Rosa is held).
Tower of Zot — Rescue Rosa
  • A 5-floor floating tower. Enemies: Magus Sisters appear as regular enemies early in the tower (the same trio you'll fight as a boss), Searcher (robotic, physical). Keep everyone's HP high throughout.
  • Floor 1–3: Standard tower corridors. Chests: Power Armlet (boosts Strength — equip on Cecil or Kain when he returns), Blizzara tome, Crystal Gloves. Head upward via the central stairway.
  • Floor 4 — Boss: Magus Sisters (Cindy, Sandy, Mindy):
Boss: Magus Sisters — Cindy ~3,500 HP, Sandy ~4,000 HP, Mindy ~3,000 HP
Mechanic: They coordinate — Mindy charges Sandy who charges Cindy for a combo Tri-Disaster attack (3-element AoE). Disrupting one breaks the chain.
Strategy: Kill Mindy first (smallest, lowest HP — she's the charger). Then Sandy. Cindy alone is manageable. Cecil physical, Tellah Thunder/Fire on Mindy, Cid attack. Don't let them chain their combo attack — it deals 600+ to the whole party.
  • Floor 5 — Golbez, Tellah's Sacrifice, Barbariccia: Golbez appears. Tellah challenges him alone — he unleashes Meteo (which normally costs 99 MP but Tellah only has ~90 max). He powers the spell with his own life force. Meteo deals massive damage and breaks Golbez's hold on Kain. Tellah collapses and dies. Golbez retreats. Kain rejoins, ashamed and freed.
Boss: Barbariccia (Wind Fiend) — ~6,500 HP
Weakness: Physical attacks at the right time; Lightning when exposed
Mechanic: She surrounds herself with a Maelstrom tornado barrier — physical attacks are reduced while it's active. Kain's Jump breaks through the tornado (dealing double damage and landing when she's exposed). Use Kain's Jump every turn.
Attacks: Maelstrom (reduces party HP to single digits), Breath Wing (AoE wind), physical
Strategy: After Maelstrom, Rosa must Curaga the party immediately — everyone is near death. Kain: Jump every turn. Cecil: physical when tornado is down. Rosa: Curaga every turn after Maelstrom hits. The fight is long but survivable with constant healing.
Rosa rejoins after Barbariccia. Your endgame party is forming: Cecil, Kain, Rosa, and soon Edge and Rydia. Before the Underworld: buy the best equipment available in surface towns. Stock 20 Elixirs and upgrade Rosa's White Magic gear.
5

Underworld — Dwarves & Dark Crystals

▾
Party: Cecil, Kain, Rosa + Cid → Cecil, Kain, Rosa, Rydia, Edge (final surface party)
Descending to the Underworld
  • Cid modifies the Enterprise to dive through the magma barrier separating the surface and underworld. The ship plunges down — then Cid must stay behind to repair the barrier hole or the lava seals them in. Cid temporarily leaves the party. He returns on the Underworld surface later.
  • The underground world has its own continents, towns, and the Dwarven kingdom of Tomra. The Dwarves are fighting a losing battle against Golbez's Machines.
Dwarven Kingdom — Golbez's Machines
  • In Tomra: stock up heavily. The Underworld shops carry much better equipment than what you had on the surface. Priority: upgrade Cecil's armor, Rosa's robes, and Kain's spear.
  • Boss: Luca's Golems (Lugae's Machines / Calcabrina) — Golbez sends doll-monsters controlled by the mad doctor Lugae to steal the Dwarven Dark Crystal. The dolls merge into Calcabrina when damaged.
    Calcabrina (~6,000 HP): deals AoE magic damage. Use Cecil and Kain's physical attacks. Rosa Curaga. Kill the individual dolls before they can merge if possible — once merged, Calcabrina is stronger.
  • Rydia returns! In the middle of the underground battle, Rydia appears fully grown. Time in the Feymarch passes differently — she has been there for years. She has all her Black Magic AND summons. She replaces the gap left by the departed Tellah and Palom. She joins the party permanently.
Eblan Castle & Edge
  • Eblan Castle (underground, to the east) is under attack. Edge (Prince of Eblan, Ninja) has been fighting alone. He's brash, arrogant, and devastated — Rubicante the Fire Fiend has transformed his parents (King and Queen of Eblan) into monsters.
  • Fight alongside Edge to his parents' location in the cave. His parents beg Edge to kill them and end their suffering — he does. Edge joins permanently, angry and hurt.
  • Edge's abilities: Throw (throw weapons for massive damage — save Shurikens), Ninjutsu (Flood, Blitz, Smoke — learned automatically), Steal (rarely useful but try on bosses). He's fast and dual-wields automatically.
Boss: Rubicante (Fire Fiend) — ~31,000 HP
Mechanic: Open cloak = weak to Ice. Closed cloak = physical attacks deal more damage but magic is absorbed. Watch the cloak state.
Ritual: Before the fight, Rubicante fully restores your party's HP and MP out of respect for honorable combat. He then fights seriously.
Strategy: Rydia: Blizzaga when cloak is open (high damage). Cecil: physical when cloak is closed. Edge: Flood (water ninjutsu — also effective when open). Rosa: Shell + Curaga. Kain: Jump (always deals solid damage regardless of cloak). Long fight but manageable with cloak awareness.
Sealed Cave — Final Dark Crystal
  • The Sealed Cave is the last of the Dark Crystals. Luca gives you the key to enter. It's a 10-floor cave with deadly random encounters — Waning Moon enemies use instant KO abilities. Stock 15 Elixirs before entering.
  • Floors 1–5: Cave passages with Waning Moon, Dark Elf variant enemies, and Golems. The encounter rate is high. Rosa: keep party healed constantly. Rydia: Blizzaga or Meteor for crowd control. Edge: Throw Shurikens on anything that seems dangerous.
  • Floors 6–10: Stronger enemies, narrower corridors. Chests: Elixir ×3, Murasame (powerful katana for Edge — very useful), Protect Ring. At the bottom: the Dark Crystal chest. Pick it up.
  • Kain's second betrayal: At the exit, Golbez's influence recaptures Kain's mind. He takes the Dark Crystal and hands it over. The party falls through a trap door into the underground river. They wash up near the Land of Summoned Monsters (Feymarch).
Kain takes the Dark Crystal. This is scripted — you cannot prevent it. Do not panic. He will return to your party permanently later. The current party without Kain is: Cecil, Rosa, Rydia, Edge.
6

Land of Summoned Monsters & the Feymarch

▾
Feymarch — Land of Summoned Monsters
  • The Feymarch is both a story location (where Rydia grew up) and an optional dungeon. You don't need to fight either boss to complete the game — but Asura and Leviatan are two of the most powerful summons in FF4.
  • The Feymarch has its own shops — buy Shurikens (×99 for Edge), upgrade any remaining armor. Stock Dry Ethers — Rosa will need them later in the Lunar Subterrane.
Boss: Asura (Queen of the Feymarch) — ~23,000 HP
Mechanic: Asura randomly uses one of three abilities each turn: Cure (heals herself ~3,000 HP), Reflect (reflects all magic back at you), Berserk (increases her attack power). The randomness makes strategy tricky.
Strategy: If she reflects, your Rydia summons will hit your own party — stop summoning and use physical attacks. Cecil, Edge, Kain (when rejoined): attack every turn. Rosa: Curaga when your party is low. The fight is winnable even with bad Asura RNG — just be persistent. Reward: Rydia learns Asura summon.
Boss: Leviatan (King of the Feymarch) — ~29,000 HP
Weakness: Fire (weak when wet)
Attacks: Tidal Wave (party AoE water damage ~1,500 — the most dangerous attack), physical hits
