  • Floor 1 (B1): Enemies: White Dragon (ice-elemental, hits very hard — use Fire spells), Wolf (fast, pack attacks), Eye (casts Petrify — the most dangerous status here). Bring Gold Needles — at least 8. If you lack Gold Needles, Esuna cures Petrify (White Mage/Red Mage). Head north to the stairs.
  • Floor 2 (B2): Teleporter traps — stepping on glowing floor tiles warps you to random spots on the floor, potentially back to B1. Walk carefully along the walls to avoid most traps. Enemies same as B1 with more Eyes appearing. Stairs are in the northeast corner.
  • Floor 3 (B3 — Lowest): The key floor. Chests: Floater (key item — the main objective), Ribbon (Pixel Remaster — best armor in the game, protects against all status effects), Ice Shield (if not already obtained), Ice Sword (lightning-element in some versions). Zombie Dragon patrols here — not mandatory but very dangerous: ~1,200 HP, weak to Fire and Dia/Diara. Run if unprepared.
  • After grabbing the Floater, use Warp/Teleport to exit. Return to the airship site in Ryukahn Desert (south of Crescent Lake). Examine the sand to use the Floater → Airship rises!
Airship — New Accessibility
  • The Airship lets you fly anywhere. Visit Onrac (north continent) — they mention the Sea Shrine. Visit Gaia (northwestern island) — a fairy in the spring gives you Oxyale (you'll need this for the Sea Shrine later).
  • Visit Lufenia (far east on airship) — the locals speak a foreign language you can't understand yet. Note the location — you'll need the Rosetta Stone later.
  • Buy new spells in Onrac and other towns accessible only by air. Prioritize: Haste (speed up warriors), Curaga, Holy (Dia3) for undead.
Citadel of Trials — Rat Tail
  • Located on a small peninsula in the south (fly there with the Airship). A 3-floor teleporter maze.
  • Floor 1: Teleporter tiles send you to Floor 2. Step on the correct teleporter (trial and error — the safe path goes counterclockwise from the entrance). Enemies: Mindflayer (paralyze/confuse), Blue Dragon.
  • Floor 2: Same teleporter puzzle mechanic. Correct path leads to Floor 3 staircase. Mindflayer are very dangerous — equip Ribbons if available, or have Esuna ready.
  • Floor 3: Chest with Rat Tail — the key item. Red Dragon may spawn here (extremely powerful, ~1,600 HP) — run from it unless you're very high level. Use Warp to exit after grabbing the Rat Tail.
Class Change — Bahamut's Cave
  • Fly the Airship to the small island in the southwest sea. The cave entrance leads to King Bahamut — the same Bahamut who is summonable in later FF games.
  • Walk to Bahamut's throne. Present the Rat Tail. He promotes all four Warriors to their advanced classes instantly.
Class Change Upgrades:
Warrior → Knight (all armor/weapons, White Magic levels 1–3 usable)
Thief → Ninja (dual wield, Black Magic levels 1–4 usable — buy them spell tomes!)
Monk → Master (higher base stats, barehand damage)
Red Mage → Red Wizard (all magic levels except L8 spells)
White Mage → White Wizard (top-tier white magic: Curaga, Holy, etc.)
Black Mage → Black Wizard (top-tier black magic: Flare, Meteo equivalent)
After class change, immediately return to Cornelia, Elfheim, Crescent Lake, and Onrac to re-equip. Knights can now wear Dragon Mail and Ribbon. Ninjas who chose the Black Mage spell list — buy all available spell scrolls right away. This is the single biggest power spike in the game.
6

Sea Shrine — Water Orb

▾
Prerequisites — Getting Oxyale
  • Fly to the town of Onrac (northern continent). A submarine is moored at the dock, but you need Oxyale (magical air for underwater travel).
  • Fly to Gaia (small northwestern island). In the center of town there's a spring — a trapped fairy is inside a bottle in the spring. Examine the spring to free the fairy. She gives you Oxyale in thanks.
  • Return to Onrac. Board the submarine using the Oxyale → descend to the Sunken Shrine.
Sea Shrine (Sunken Shrine) — Floor by Floor
  • Pre-entry stock: At least 15 Antidotes, 10 Gold Needles, 10 Cottages or 5 Elixirs, 99 Potions. This is the longest dungeon in FF1 — do not enter underprovisioned.
  • Floor 1 (B1): Underwater entry room. Enemies: Sahagin (water, weak to Lightning), Mermaid (can confuse), Ocho (tentacle attacks). Head north to the main shrine structure.
  • Floors 2–4: Teleporter maze. Many tiles warp you to other floors — map cautiously. Mermaids are found in small alcoves on these floors — talk to them to fully restore HP and MP for free. These are your rest points. Seek them out before each difficult floor.
  • Floors 5–6: Harder enemies appear: Sea Snake (poison on hit — keep Antidotes ready), Shark (fast, high physical damage). More Mermaid alcoves for healing. Chests include Thor's Hammer (Black Wizard can equip this for lightning damage — very useful), White Robe (powerful white mage armor), Healing Helm.
  • Floor 7: Warmech zone begins. Warmech is a random encounter (~1.5% chance per step) on the bridges near the top. Warmech has ~2,000 HP, uses Nuclear (massive party AoE), and counters frequently. Run if you see one unless you're level 40+ and fully healed. He's technically optional and very deadly.
  • Floor 8 (Boss): Use a Cottage before entering Kraken's chamber. Chests on this floor: Ribbon (if not obtained in Ice Cave — do not miss this), Light Axe (Holy-element axe, crushes undead).
Boss: Kraken (Water Fiend) — ~2,000 HP
Weakness: Lightning (Thundara/Thundaga)
Attacks: Ink (inflicts Blind on target — immediately use Eye Drops or Esuna), Tentacle (physical hit), CometTail (party AoE ice)
Strategy: Black Wizard/Black Wizard: Thundaga every round — Kraken has no lightning resistance. White Mage: Curaga when party drops below 200 HP, or remove Blind status immediately (Blind halves physical accuracy — your Warriors become near useless while blinded). Knight with Light Axe deals strong physical damage. Haste on your fastest attacker.
Reward: Water Orb lit.
After Kraken, use Warp/Teleport to exit the Sunken Shrine. You only need two Orbs left: Wind (Flying Fortress) and a brief return to the Earth shrine. Next stop: Mirage Tower.
7

Mirage Tower & Flying Fortress

▾
Prerequisites — Lufenia & the Chime
  • Before the Flying Fortress, visit Onrac — a merchant there sells you the Bottle (empty bottle). Take it to the spring in Gaia to free the fairy and get Oxyale (if you haven't already for the Sea Shrine).
  • Fly to Lufenia (far eastern island). The inhabitants speak an incomprehensible language. To understand them, find the Rosetta Stone — it's a chest inside the Waterfall cave near Onrac (a short cave north of Onrac, accessible on foot from the town). Bring the Rosetta Stone back, and the Lufenians give you the Chime — required to enter the Mirage Tower's warp gate.
Mirage Tower — Floor by Floor
  • The Mirage Tower is visible as a pyramid in the desert (near Lufenia). Fly there, enter, and use the Chime to open the magical barrier on the entrance.
  • Floor 1: Enemies: Mummy (undead, weak to Fire/Dia), Cockatrice (can inflict Petrify). Keep Gold Needles ready. Head north to the stairs.
  • Floor 2: Enemies: Sphinx (strong physical, no weakness), Wyvern (fast, high HP). More Cockatrice appear. Chests: Sun Sword (powerful sword with no elemental type — great for Knight/Ninja), Saber. Exit is north.
  • Floor 3 (Top): A single warp pad at the top. Step on it → transported to the Flying Fortress in the sky. No turning back until you Warp/Teleport out.
Flying Fortress — Floor by Floor
  • Enemy theme: All enemies are robotic/mechanical — universally weak to Lightning. Thundaga destroys everything here. Enemies: Aerial Killer (fast), Gunpowder (can self-destruct for massive damage to one character — kill it fast), Robotech, Piscodemon (status effects: Paralysis).
  • Floor 1: Entry. Head north-northeast to the stairs. Chests: Platinum Armor equivalent (heavy armor for Knight), Healing Staff (White Mage can attack with it to heal for ~50 HP).
  • Floor 2: Branching corridors. Chests: Protect Cloak, 10,000 Gil. Piscodemon appear — they can Paralyze your party members. Esuna or Heal status immediately.
  • Floor 3: Chests: Winged Sword (wind element — very powerful here as enemies aren't resistant to it), Megalixir (fully restores one party member — save for Tiamat). Gunpowder encounters peak here — target them first every fight.
  • Floor 4: Pre-boss. Chests: Genji Helmet (best headgear for physical classes), Genji Armor (best heavy armor). Use a Cottage here. There is a small alcove before Tiamat's chamber — rest completely.
  • Floor 5 (Boss): Long corridor leads to Tiamat's chamber. No last-minute healing — use it on Floor 4.
Boss: Tiamat (Wind Fiend, Five-Headed Dragon) — ~2,000 HP
Weakness: Ice (Blizzaga)
Attacks: Blaze (fire breath hitting ALL characters for 200–300 damage), physical claws (single target ~200), Poison (inflicts Poison status), multiple attacks per round
Strategy: This is the hardest of the four Fiends. Open with Haste on your Knight. Black Wizard: Blizzaga every round. White Mage: Curaga after every Blaze — Blaze to the whole party at low HP is a wipe condition. Keep party above 350 HP at all times. Ninja: throw Shurikens or use Blizzaga scrolls. If anyone gets poisoned, Antidote immediately or they'll drop fast during the next Blaze.
Reward: Wind Orb lit. All four Orbs are restored. Warp out and return to the Temple of Fiends (Chaos Shrine) — the Orbs have opened a path into the past.
8

Temple of Fiends — Past & Chaos

▾
There is no save point inside the Temple of Fiends (Past). You will fight 4 boss rematches + Chaos with no rest between them. Prepare thoroughly before entering.
Pre-Entry Checklist
  • Level recommendation: 35–40 minimum. Level 45+ for comfort. Grind the area outside the Temple if needed — enemies here drop decent Gil for equipment upgrades.
  • Consumables: 15+ Elixirs, 10 Cottages (use inside the dungeon between floors), 20 Gold Needles, 20 Antidotes, 30 Eye Drops, full Phoenix Down stock.
  • Equipment check: All party members in best available gear. Knight with Genji Armor + Genji Helmet. White Wizard with Ribbon (all status immunity). Black Wizard with best Robe + high level spells stocked.
  • Spell loadout: Ensure Flare (Pixel Remaster's Nuke equivalent), Thundaga, Blizzaga, Curaga, Arise, and Haste are all acquired.
Entering the Past
  • Return to the Temple of Fiends (Chaos Shrine) in the present — the same location where the game began. The four Orbs have created a portal. Walk through the glowing door → transported 2,000 years into the past.
  • In the past, the shrine is intact and fully operational. The four Fiends are here in their original forms — but stronger than before.
Floor by Floor — Four Fiend Rematches
  • Floor 1 — Lich Rematch: Enemies: Zombie (undead, weak to Fire/Dia), Ghoul (Paralysis). Lich awaits at the end. Use Dia3/Holy and Fire spells. He has higher HP than before (~2,400) and opens with Quake more aggressively. Same strategy: Holy, Diara, Flare. Use a Cottage in the corridor after defeating him.
  • Floor 2 — Marilith Rematch: Enemies: Fire Lizard, Agama (same as Gurgu Volcano). Marilith (~2,400 HP) now uses Fire3 more frequently. Same strategy: Blizzaga spam. Cottage after victory.
  • Floor 3 — Kraken Rematch: Enemies: Sahagin, Sea Snake. Kraken (~2,400 HP) uses Ink more aggressively (Blind on multiple targets). Same strategy: Thundaga. Immediately cure Blind when it lands. Cottage after victory.
  • Floor 4 — Tiamat Rematch: The hardest rematch. Tiamat (~2,400 HP) uses Blaze nearly every turn now. Party must enter with full HP and MP. Keep Curaga ready every round after she attacks. Blizzaga from Black Wizard. Cottage after victory — critical before Chaos.
  • Floor 5 / Basement — Chaos: Final staircase. Enter fully healed from the Cottage used after Tiamat.
Final Boss: Chaos — ~20,000 HP (the true original Chaos from 2,000 years past)
No elemental weakness — he resists or absorbs most elements
Attacks: Flare (massive non-elemental damage to one character), Curaja (heals himself for 9,999 HP — the biggest threat in the fight), elemental breath attacks, physical hits
Strategy: Speed is everything — Chaos's Curaja can undo entire rounds of damage. Apply Haste to both physical attackers immediately. Use Temper (Str Up) on your Knight for maximum damage per hit. Black Wizard: Flare or non-elemental attacks every round — Fire, Ice, and Lightning are all absorbed or resisted. White Wizard: Curaga every round — when Chaos casts Flare on your frontliner they'll drop to near-zero. Ninja: throw the best weapons you've saved (Masamune scroll etc.) for unresisted damage. Focus purely on offense — you must outdamage his healing.
Victory: The time loop collapses. Chaos dies. Garland never went back in time. The Warriors of Light return home — to a world with no memory of them ever fighting. Credits roll.
The twist: Chaos sent Garland 2,000 years into the past to become Chaos — creating a time loop where he could never truly die. The four Warriors of Light breaking this loop is the first time paradox in Final Fantasy history. For a 1987 NES game, the implication is remarkably sophisticated.
+

Soul of Chaos — Bonus Dungeons

▾

The Soul of Chaos dungeons are optional bonus content from the GBA release, included in the Pixel Remaster. They unlock progressively as you restore each Orb and contain guest bosses from later Final Fantasy games.

Soul of Chaos bosses are significantly harder than Chaos himself. The final bonus boss (Shinryu) rivals post-game FF5 content. Do not attempt these at story-appropriate levels.
Earthgift Shrine — Unlocks after Earth Orb (Lich)
  • Located in a cave near Melmond. 4 floors with monsters that feel from the FF3 era. Enemies include Cerberus (three-headed dog, fast) and Echidna (wide spell variety).
  • Floor Layout: Each floor has a random layout — the dungeon rearranges itself on each visit. Boss encounters trigger at fixed room spots.
  • Bosses (any 4 floors, random order): Cerberus (Slow all enemies, then beat down), Ahriman (Eye enemy variant — Petrify and instant KO spells), Echidna (status spread — Ribbon essential), Scarmiglione (undead boss from FF4 — use Holy/Dia3). Defeating all 4 bosses rewards a Megalixir.
  • Chests: Rune Blade, Rune Staff, Mirage Vest, various high-tier accessories. Best early-game bonus dungeon rewards. Recommended level: 25+.
Hellfire Chasm — Unlocks after Fire Orb (Marilith)
  • Located in a mountainous area northeast of Crescent Lake. 4 floors with fire-themed enemies and intense difficulty.
  • Bosses: Scarmiglione (FF4), Cagnazzo (FF4 Water Archfiend — Thunder weakness), Barbariccia (FF4 Wind Archfiend — use physical attacks when she curls up into tornado form, use lightning otherwise), Rubicante (FF4 Fire Archfiend — Ice weakness; he heals you before the fight out of honor — a nice callback). Defeating all 4 rewards a rare accessory.
  • Notable reward: Masamune (the legendary sword from FF history — strongest weapon in FF1, no class restriction). Well worth the effort. Recommended level: 35+.
Lifespring Grotto — Unlocks after Water Orb (Kraken)
  • Located near Onrac on the northern continent. 4 floors with water and nature-themed enemies.
  • Bosses: Guest bosses from FF2 — the Emperor (powerful magic casts), Borghen, Leon (physical), and Gottos. Their spells are more aggressive than anything you've faced in FF1.
  • Notable rewards: Protect Ring (permanent Protect effect — excellent for your tank), Megalixir. Recommended level: 40+.
Whisperwind Cove — Unlocks from start (or after Wind Orb)
  • The longest and hardest Soul of Chaos dungeon: 10 floors. Guest bosses from FF5.
  • Bosses include: Gilgamesh (show up and try to impress him — multiple encounters across floors), Atmos (instant KO attempts), Necrophobe (the hardest non-Shinryu boss — uses Barrier Change cycling between elemental absorptions).
  • Shinryu (optional, found in a chest at the end) — Opens with Tidal Wave (massive water damage). Bring multiple Coral Rings and hit with the strongest non-water attacks available. He's the hardest fight in the game.
  • Notable rewards: Ribbon (absolute best armor — all status immunity), Crystal equipment set (strongest armor tier in FF1 Pixel Remaster). Recommended level: 50 (max).
The recommended order: clear Earthgift Shrine right after Lich (level 25+), skip Hellfire Chasm until you've done the class change (~level 35), tackle Lifespring and Whisperwind post-game after defeating Chaos. Masamune from Hellfire Chasm trivializes the Chaos fight if you get it early enough.
✦

▾

Research based on GameFAQs (Split Infinity, dark_neo_cloud guides), FF1 wiki, and Pixel Remaster community documentation.

Complete Walkthrough · All Characters · Every Missable

Final Fantasy V I I

✦ ✦ ✦
Classic / Remake Guide

From Reactor 1 to the Northern Cave — floor-by-floor dungeon navigation, every chest, Materia locations, missable characters, and boss strategies for the most iconic RPG ever made.

✦

Introduction, Materia System & Tips

▾
How Materia Works
  • Materia are crystallized Mako energy slotted into weapons and armor. Each piece of equipment has linked and unlinked slots — linked slots allow Support Materia to modify Command Materia.
  • Key links: HP Absorb + Any magic = heals on cast. MP Absorb + Any magic = restores MP. All + Any magic = hits all enemies. Added Effect + a status Materia = auto-inflicts status.
  • Materia grows AP after each battle. At maximum AP it masters and produces a free copy at Level 1. Master All your core magic Materia before the final dungeon.
  • Enemy Skill Materia is blue (Command type) and learns skills from enemies. There are 4 in the game — pick up all 4 for a full set.
Core Tips
  • Save at every save point. The game has no auto-save.
  • Limit Breaks fill from taking damage. Each character has 4 levels, 2 limits per level. To unlock Level 2: use Level 1 limits X times. Level 3: use Level 2 limits X times. Level 4 (ultimate): unique item per character.
  • Gil is easy to earn — spend it on Materia and Potions early. Don't hoard.
  • Items sold only in one town may not reappear — buy extra when you see them.
Yuffie and Vincent are both optional characters with unique missable recruitment sequences. See their individual sections for exact conditions.
✦

Characters & Limit Breaks

▾
Cloud
SOLDIER 1st Class
Limit: Braver → Cross-Slash → Meteorain → Omnislash

Mandatory. Ultimate Limit: Omnislash — must win at Gold Saucer Battle Square with 64,000 BP (Disc 1) or purchase for 51,200 after (Disc 2+).

Barret
AVALANCHE Leader
Limit: Big Shot → Mindblow → Satellite Beam → Catastrophe

Mandatory. Ultimate Limit scroll: Fort Condor final battle reward (before the Condor dies).

Tifa
Martial Artist
Limit: Beat Rush → Waterkick → Dolphin Blow → Final Heaven

Mandatory. Final Heaven manual: Tifa's Piano in Nibelheim (revisit Disc 2 after Cloud recovers).

Aerith
Ancient
Limit: Healing Wind → Seal Evil → Planet Protector → Great Gospel

Dies in City of the Ancients. Great Gospel: finish before Disc 2. Scroll found via Mythril trade with man in house north of Junon after Midgar escape.

Red XIII
Ancient Beast
Limit: Sled Fang → Lunatic High → Blood Fang → Cosmo Memory

Joins automatically at Shinra HQ. Cosmo Memory: reward from Lost Number boss in Nibelheim Mansion.

Yuffie
Ninja / Materia Hunter
Limit: Greased Lightning → Clear Tranquil → Landscaper → All Creation

Optional. Recruit via random battles in forests. Never flee — pick the right dialogue options. Ultimate limit scroll found in Wutai pagoda (must complete Wutai sidequest).

Cait Sith
Fortune Teller Robot
Limit: Dice → Slot

Joins at Gold Saucer. Slot limit is random and extremely powerful if Triple 7s or Bar/Bar/Bar land.

Cid
Pilot / Engineer
Limit: Boost Jump → Dynamite → Dragon → Highwind

Joins in Rocket Town. Highwind limit scroll: inside Gelnika submarine wreck (Disc 2 optional dungeon).

Vincent
Turk / Experiment
Limit: Galian Beast → Death Gigas → Hellmasker → Chaos

Optional. Found in Nibelheim Mansion basement. Chaos scroll from Lucrecia's Waterfall Cave (Disc 2+, after Diamond Weapon falls).

Materia, Equipment & Boss Reference

▾
Best Materia — Priority Acquisitions
Knights of the Round (KOTR)
Round Island (NE corner, requires Gold Chocobo)
The most powerful Summon in the game — 13 hits of non-elemental damage. Pair with HP Absorb and MP Absorb for sustainable use. Breed a Gold Chocobo (Wonderful + Wonderful with Zeio Nut) to reach Round Island. Mastered KOTR can be sold for 500,000 gil or duplicated via W-Summon + Mime.
Mime
Wutai Area (after Corneo sidequest, in the pagoda chest)
Repeats the last action performed by any party member at no MP cost. Combine with KOTR + HP Absorb for infinite free summons. One of the most powerful Materia in the game for boss fights.
W-Summon / W-Magic / W-Item
W-Summon: Disc 3 crater (Midgar Sunken Highway area) · W-Magic: Disc 2 Junon area steal · W-Item: Disc 2 Midgar underground
W-Item allows infinite item duplication mid-battle (use one item, cancel, repeat). W-Summon casts two summons per turn. W-Magic doubles spell output. These three Materia are core to any endgame optimized setup.
HP↔MP
Disc 1: Sleeping Man near Junon (after 64+ random battles)
Swaps HP and MP values. Equip on a character with naturally high HP to gain enormous MP pools. Combine with MP Turbo for devastating spell damage. The Sleeping Man requires an even number of battles fought.
Quadra Magic
Disc 2: Cave of the Gi (accessible after Cosmo Canyon)
Casts the linked Materia 4 times for the MP cost of one. Pair with Ultima or Comet2 for massive damage output. Cannot be paired with Summon or W-Materia. Limited to 5 uses per battle.
Counter Attack / Counter
Disc 1: Cosmo Canyon (Counter) · Disc 2: Mt. Nibel area
Counter automatically attacks/casts when the character is hit. Pair Counter with a damage spell for automatic magical counter-attacks. Extremely powerful for high-agility characters like Yuffie or Cloud.
Master Magic / Master Summon / Master Command
Mideel (Disc 2 onward) — created by mastering all Materia of each type in a single copy
Master Materia condenses all spells/summons/commands into one slot. Only one exists per type (unless duplicated). Mastering all Magic Materia requires AP grinding — equip on characters who fight often. Final reward from the Materia Keeper chain.
Enemy Skill Materia — Complete List
There are 4 Enemy Skill Materia in the game. Collect all 4 as early as possible so you can learn skills on multiple copies simultaneously. All 24 skills can be learned on a single materia — you just need one, but having multiple lets multiple characters use them.
Beta (Fire damage, all enemies)
Learn from: Midgar Zolom (Grasslands marsh)
One of the strongest Enemy Skills. Midgar Zolom uses Beta when your party HP drops below ~768. The strategy: let it swallow one party member (they survive), then the others learn Beta. Requires Level 20+. Deals ~3,000 damage at mid-game.
Big Guard (Barrier + MBarrier + Haste, all allies)
Learn from: Beach Plug (Corel area beaches)
Arguably the most useful Enemy Skill — applies Barrier, MBarrier, and Haste to entire party at once. Beach Plugs are found on the beaches near the Corel area. Essential for all major boss fights.
Aqualung (Water damage, all enemies)
Learn from: Jenova·LIFE (mandatory boss fight)
Also learnable from Harpy (Gold Saucer desert area) and Serpent (Underwater area). Jenova·LIFE teaches it automatically during the story — just have Enemy Skill Materia equipped on an alive party member.
Trine (Lightning damage, all enemies)
Learn from: Godo (Wutai Pagoda boss, Disc 2) or Dragons
Learnable from Materia Keeper (Cosmo Canyon) on Disc 1 if you have the Skill Materia equipped. Strong non-elemental-ish lightning damage. Also from CMD.Grand Horn in the Northern Crater.
Laser (Single target, ignores defense)
Learn from: Dark Dragon (Northern Crater) or Keeper (Gongaga)
Reduces one target to single-digit HP. Useful for killing off near-dead enemies instantly. Works on most non-boss enemies.
Pandora's Box (Non-elemental, all enemies)
Learn from: Dragon Zombie (Northern Crater, Disc 3 only)
The Dragon Zombie only appears once per visit to that crater section. The move deals massive non-elemental damage to all enemies. Extremely rare — requires the Enemy Skill Materia equipped when Dragon Zombie uses it. One of the most powerful Enemy Skills.
Goblin Punch (Non-elemental, same-level enemies)
Learn from: Goblin (Cactus Island, southeast of Mideel)
Deals massive damage when the user is the same level as the target. Use Manipulate to force Goblin to use it. At high levels against low-defense enemies it can one-shot. Useful for the Yuffie sidequest leveling strategy.
Death Force (Immune to Instant Death)
Learn from: Adamantaimai (Wutai beaches) via Manipulate
Grants immunity to all instant-death attacks for one battle. Use Manipulate Materia on Adamantaimai and select Death Force. Critical for safer Northern Crater runs against death-inflicting enemies.
Best Weapons by Character
Cloud — Ultima Weapon
Defeat Ultimate Weapon (flying boss, Disc 2 onward, appears after Diamond Weapon dies)
8 linked slots, all growth. Damage scales with Cloud's current HP — the higher his HP vs max HP, the more damage it deals. Keep Cloud at or near full HP for maximum output. Stat: Attack 100, Magic 51.
Barret — Missing Score
Disc 2: Huge Materia rocket side-quest (Corel area) — board the rocket before it launches
Damage scales with total AP in all equipped Materia. Load Barret with high-AP Materia (mastered spells, KOTR in progress) for astronomical damage. 6 linked slots, double growth. Arguably his best weapon by endgame.
Tifa — Premium Heart
Disc 2: Junon — visit the weapon shop after the Meteor summon event
Damage scales with Limit gauge fill. Keep Limit gauge full for maximum damage on each Limit Break. 4 linked slots, double growth. Pairs perfectly with Limit Materia.
Aerith — Princess Guard
Temple of the Ancients (must retrieve before Aerith dies — permanently missable)
Damage scales with number of KO'd party members. As a support character she won't often use physical attacks, but keep it equipped for the stat bonuses. 4 linked slots, triple growth — level Materia on it. Missable — get it at the Temple of the Ancients before the Black Materia event.
Red XIII — Limited Moon
Disc 2: Bugenhagen's observatory in Cosmo Canyon (Disc 2, after Bugenhagen's death)
Damage scales inversely with MP — the more MP remaining, the higher the damage. Keep Red XIII's MP high. 6 linked slots, double growth.
Cid — Venus Gospel
Disc 2: Lucrecia's Waterfall (with Vincent in party, after Diamond Weapon dies)
Restores MP to all allies when Cid uses a Limit Break. Pairs excellently with 4x Cut and high MP usage setups. 6 linked slots, double growth.
Yuffie — Conformer
Disc 2: Sunken Gelnika (underwater area, accessible via submarine)
Damage scales with enemy level — extremely powerful against high-level enemies in the Northern Crater. Also does not trigger the 9,999 cap on Throw damage. 6 unlinked slots, no growth. Best for Yuffie's Throw/Frog Throw strategies.
Vincent — Death Penalty
Disc 2: Lucrecia's Waterfall (with Vincent in party, after Diamond Weapon cutscene)
Damage scales with number of enemies Vincent has killed. Grind 60,000+ kills with Vincent for absurd damage output. 6 linked slots, double growth. The ultimate weapon for a dedicated kill-farmer.
Key Armor & Accessories
Mystile (Armor)
Disc 3: Northern Crater (treasure chest) and Midgar Raid shops
Highest Evasion armor in the game (55 Evade, 20 Magic Evade). 4 linked slots, double growth. Best armor for physical-evasion builds. Combine with Cover Materia for a near-untouchable cover tank.
Aegis Armlet (Armor)
Disc 2: Gaea's Cliff chest
High magic evasion (48 Magic Evade). 4 linked slots. Good mid-game armor when magic-heavy bosses need countering.
Ribbon (Accessory)
Disc 2: Temple of the Ancients chest + Disc 3: Northern Crater
Prevents all status ailments. Only 2–3 available per playthrough. Prioritize for characters who lack natural status resistance. Essential for the Safer·Sephiroth fight (Slow, Silence, Stop all disabled).
Sprint Shoes (Accessory)
Disc 1: Gold Saucer — purchase in the Wonder Square for GP
Permanently applies Haste at battle start. Frees up a Materia slot that would otherwise be used for Haste spell. Excellent quality-of-life accessory for any character.
Hero Drink / Hyper / Tranquilizer
Purchasable from various shops throughout the game
Hero Drink temporarily raises all stats. Hyper triggers Fury status (faster Limit gauge fill, -10% accuracy). Tranquilizer counters Fury. Stockpile for Emerald/Ruby WEAPON fights.
Superboss Strategies
Emerald WEAPON — 1,000,000 HP
Disc 2+: Underwater (requires Submarine) · Weakness: None · Time Limit: 20 minutes
Strategy: Equip underwater Materia (removes time limit) or work within 20 min. Use Big Guard first. KOTR + HP Absorb + W-Summon deals ~130,000 per round. Keep party HP above 7,777 (Aire Tam Storm hits that exact amount to every party member). Equip Underwater Materia (from Kalm traveler after Ultimate Weapon dies) to remove the timer. Each of Emerald's eyes killed reduces its attacks — knock out the Emerald Laser eye clusters first.
Ruby WEAPON — 800,000 HP
Disc 2+: Desert south of Gold Saucer · Weakness: None · Appears after Ultimate Weapon dies
Strategy: Ruby starts battle by removing two party members. Enter with only Cloud alive — Ruby's tentacles won't emerge if only one character is alive, preventing its "Whirlsand" attack. Then revive partners with Phoenix Summon. Use KOTR repeatedly. Alternatively: Dazers (paralyze) + W-Item trick for infinite items. Reward: Desert Rose (trade for Gold Chocobo from Kalm traveler).
Boss Quick Reference
Guard Scorpion
Disc 1: Reactor 1 · HP: 800 · Weakness: Lightning
Do NOT attack when its tail is raised — it counters with Tail Laser. Use Thunder and physical attacks between tail cycles. Cloud + Barret can solo it easily.
Airbuster
Disc 1: Shinra Building · HP: 1,200 · Weakness: Lightning
Position Cloud behind, Barret + Tifa in front. Prioritize the MG Turrets (HP: 300 each) to prevent machine gun attacks. Thunder spells deal double damage.
Jenova·BIRTH
Disc 1: Cargo Ship · HP: 4,000 · Weakness: Fire, Lightning
Attacks with Tail Laser (reduce HP), Seed Cannon (random target), and Invisible Touch (Silence). Keep party HP above 200, use Ice spells (Aerith). First Jenova fight — straightforward.
Gi Nattak
Disc 1: Cave of the Gi · HP: 4,000 · Weakness: Fire (absorbs HP from Revive items)
Use Phoenix Down or X-Potion directly on Gi Nattak — undead enemies take damage from healing items. Three Phoenix Downs kill it instantly without combat.
Demon's Gate
Disc 1: Temple of the Ancients · HP: 8,000 · Weakness: None
Uses Demon Rush (Petrify, high priority), Punch (800+ damage), and Stone Gaze. Equip Ribbon or Fairy Ring for Petrify immunity. Kill fast with Limits + Ultima.
Jenova·LIFE
Disc 1: City of the Ancients · HP: 35,000 · Weakness: None
First multi-part fight. Tentacles can Poison the party. Cut them off first. Main body uses Aqualung (teachable via Enemy Skill). Note: Aerith's death is triggered by story, not this fight.
Diamond WEAPON
Disc 2: Outside Midgar · HP: 30,000 · Weakness: None
Charges Diamond Flash (hits all, 1,000+ damage) periodically. When charging, it's vulnerable — attack the eye cluster to interrupt if possible. Countdown visible on screen. Kill before it reaches 0 or ensure party HP > 1,200.
Safer·Sephiroth (Final Form)
Disc 3: Northern Crater · HP: 80,000 (Bizarro) + 80,000 (Safer) · Weakness: None
Bizarro·Sephiroth: Attack core last; kill outer cells first. Safer·Sephiroth uses Heartless Angel (reduces party to 1 HP), Wall (Barrier+MBarrier), and Super Nova (reduces party to ~1/32 max HP). Counters with Shadow Flare. Use Big Guard, KOTR, and keep HP topped off constantly. Supernova does not kill — always leave at least 1 HP.
🏙️

Disc 1 — Midgar & the World

Six reactors, a city of five million, and a corporation playing god with the Planet's life force.

1

Reactor 1 — The Bombing Mission

Midgar — Sector 1▾
  • Cloud drops off the train with AVALANCHE. Follow Barret into the reactor. This is a linear tutorial — fight every enemy to build Limit gauges and earn AP.
  • Chest 1 (B3, first chest room): Potion. Chest 2 (B4, catwalk): Phoenix Down. Chest 3 (B5, near core): Potion. Chest 4 (B5, east alcove): Ether.
  • Set the bomb at the reactor core. Return up the same path — there is an elevator shortcut at the top of B4.
Boss: Guard Scorpion
  • HP ~800. Uses Search Scope (locks on). Do NOT attack when it raises its tail — it counterattacks with Tail Laser (heavy party damage). Wait for the tail to lower, then attack. Lightning Materia destroys it quickly.
  • After victory: the reactor countdown begins. You have 10 minutes — more than enough. Escape via the path to the right of the boss fight area back to the streets.
Guard Scorpion: Attack freely until it raises its tail. Stop all attacks when the tail is up — wait for it to lower, then resume. Lightning spells deal double damage throughout.
2

Sector 7 Slums, Train Graveyard & Meeting Aerith

Midgar — Sectors 5–7▾
  • After the escape: Cloud falls into the Sector 5 Slums and meets Aerith selling flowers. She joins your party temporarily.
  • Talk to everyone in Sector 5 — the item shop sells Materia unavailable later. Buy Restore Materia if you don't already have one.
  • Return to Sector 7 Slums via the Sector 6 park (Wall Market shortcut becomes available later). AVALANCHE's base is the 7th Heaven bar.
Train Graveyard
  • Optional area accessible from Sector 7 — puzzle dungeon using train car levers. 5 chests: Ether, Potion ×2, Sedative, Hi-Potion. Complete it before the plate drops (it's permanently sealed after).
  • Enemies here include Ghost (immune to physical, use magic) and Ghoul — bring a Fire Materia.
  • A save point is at the exit near the Sector 7 understreet.
Sector 7 Plate Drop (Story Event)
  • Shinra drops the plate on Sector 7. Aerith is captured. Tifa falls. Cloud, Barret, and Tifa re-form as a team.
  • Before leaving for Wall Market (Sector 6), talk to all NPCs in Sector 7 for hidden items: Ether (old man near pillar), Tent (kid by fence).
Train Graveyard is permanently sealed after Sector 7's plate drops. Loot all 5 chests before advancing the plate-drop story scene.
3

Reactor 5, Wall Market & Shinra Headquarters

Midgar — Sectors 5–6, Plate Top▾
Wall Market (Cloud's Disguise)
  • To infiltrate Don Corneo's mansion and rescue Tifa, Cloud must dress as a woman. Collect:
    — Dress: Tailor (choose "Something Shiny" or "A Little Mature" or "Sporty" for different dress qualities)
    — Wig: Win the squat competition at the gym (or buy from the vending machine)
    — Tiara: Win the darts game in the bar with a high score
    — Cologne: Get the best cologne from the item shop via the pharmacy quest chain
  • Higher-quality items unlock a better Materia reward from Aerith after Corneo's mansion.
Shinra Headquarters — Floors 59–70
  • Two approaches: fight through 59 floors of enemies (more EXP/Materia) or sneak up the stairs (faster, no fights). The stairs route takes you through floors 60–70 with multiple chests.
  • Floor 63: Chest — Enemy Skill Materia #1 (one of four in the game). Equip it immediately — enemies on these floors can teach you Beta (one of the strongest skills).
  • Floor 67: Hojo's lab. Three containers in the Specimen Room — examine all three for Materia and key items including Elemental Materia.
  • Floor 68: Jenova BIRTH boss. Floor 70: Rufus boss.
Jenova BIRTH: HP ~10,000. Attack physically — she's weaker to physical than magic. Uses Stop (Barret is immune, keep him healing). After: escape to roof for Rufus fight.
Rufus + Dark Nation: Kill Dark Nation first (it casts Barrier on Rufus, blocking spells). Then focus Rufus. He deals heavy physical damage — keep HP above 300.
Enemy Skill Materia #1 is on Floor 63 of Shinra HQ. Pick it up and equip it — enemies on surrounding floors can teach you Matra Magic and other skills you cannot get easily later.
4

Kalm & the Nibelheim Flashback

Kalm · Nibelheim (Memory)▾
  • Escape Midgar on the highway — motorcycle chase minigame. Protect the truck with Cloud's bike by ramming enemies off the road. Dodge the Motorball boss afterward.
  • Travel to Kalm east of Midgar. Cloud recounts the story of Nibelheim — the flashback is mandatory and establishes the game's central mystery.
  • During the Nibelheim flashback, you control Cloud but cannot deviate from the story — just follow Sephiroth and watch the cutscenes.
  • After Kalm: The world opens. First stop: Chocobo Farm southeast (required to cross Midgar Swamp — the Midgar Zolom guards the marshland).
Sleeping Man — Critical Side Stop
  • Northwest of Junon in the hills: a man sleeping in a cave. He tracks your total battle count (the exact number matters). Return here repeatedly — when your battles end in a number matching his, he gives you Mythril. Mythril unlocks Aerith's Great Gospel limit break via a man in a house near Junon.
The Sleeping Man / Mythril chain for Aerith's Great Gospel must be completed on Disc 1 before reaching the City of the Ancients. Aerith cannot use it after she dies.
5

Chocobo Farm, Mythril Mines & Junon

Chocobo Farm · Mythril Mines · Junon▾
  • Buy a Chocobo Lure Materia from the Chocobo Farm for 2,000 gil. Equip it, go to the farm's chocobo tracks, and catch a chocobo — ride it through the Midgar Swamp to avoid the Midgar Zolom (a mandatory field enemy that will wipe you if encountered before late-game).
  • Mythril Mines: 3-floor dungeon connecting the eastern continent to Junon area.
    — Chest 1 (B1, right fork): Ether. Chest 2 (B1, left fork): Hi-Potion. Chest 3 (B2): Tent. Chest 4 (B2, east): Long Range Materia (lets back-row characters deal full damage — equip on Barret or Cait Sith).
  • After the mines: Priscilla has been hurt by a Shinra military exercise. Save her, do CPR minigame, receive the HP Plus Materia.
Junon — Shinra Military Parade
  • Infiltrate Junon by following Shinra troops. Cloud must participate in a military drill — the quality of your performance determines how many Potions and Hi-Potions you receive.
  • Inside Junon: shop sells new Materia including Shiva Materia (buy it). Also buy a Time Materia (Haste/Slow/Stop) if you can afford it — invaluable in boss fights.
  • Enemy Skill Materia #2: given to you by an NPC in the Junon underground passage. Don't miss it.
Enemy Skill Materia #2 is given by a Shinra MP in Junon's underground passages. It's easy to miss by running past him.
6

Costa del Sol, Mt. Corel & Gold Saucer

Costa del Sol · Corel · Gold Saucer▾
  • Cargo ship crossing: Boss — Jenova BIRTH variant. Same strategy as HQ: physical focus, kill adds first.
  • Costa del Sol: buy the Ifrit Materia from the item shop (4,000 gil). Buy it — Ifrit is one of the best summons for mid-game.
  • Mt. Corel: mountain railway dungeon. 7 chests: Ethers, Tent, Poison Materia, Turbo Ether. Bridges collapse — cross quickly and don't backtrack unnecessarily.
Gold Saucer — First Visit
  • Gold Saucer is mandatory story destination and also the best optional content hub: Battle Square (Limit Breaks/BP rewards), Chocobo Square (race for GP), Wonder Square (mini-games for GP).
  • Cloud's Omnislash limit: purchasable at Battle Square for 64,000 BP on Disc 1 (easier than Disc 2's price). Use BP to buy it if possible.
  • After the Dyne incident: Barret's backstory. Boss: Dyne — HP ~1,200. He uses attacks that hit all. Physical focus — he falls quickly.
  • After prison sequence with Cait Sith (who joins here): escape the Corel Desert and take the ropeway back to the Gold Saucer.
Dyne: HP ~1,200. He counterattacks with S-Mine (party damage) when hit. Bring Cloud's strongest physical attacks. Limit Breaks end the fight in 1–2 turns. Barret's backstory is revealed after — emotional scene.
7

Cosmo Canyon & the Gi Nattak Cave

Cosmo Canyon · Cave of the Gi▾
  • Cosmo Canyon is Red XIII's home — Bugenhagen, his grandfather, explains the Planet's life force (Lifestream). Important lore for understanding the story.
  • Buy all Materia from the Canyon shop — they carry unique combat Materia: Gravity (Demi — deals ¼ of max HP as damage, ignores Defense), Comet, Contain.
  • Cave of the Gi: 3-level cavern dungeon. 5 chests: Ether, Hi-Ether, Elixir, Platinum Fist (Red XIII weapon), X-Potion.
Boss: Gi Nattak
  • HP ~6,000. Gi Nattak and his Soul Fires are undead — healing items like Phoenix Down and Potions deal massive damage to undead. Throw Phoenix Down at Nattak for a potential instant kill, or use Hi-Potions to deal heavy damage. Fire attacks also work well.
Gi Nattak: Undead boss — throw Phoenix Downs directly at him for 9,999 damage (instant kill or near-instant). His Soul Fire adds are also undead; Fire spells clear them quickly.
8

Nibelheim Revisited, Rocket Town & Cid

Nibelheim · Rocket Town · Wutai▾
Nibelheim — Shinra Mansion
  • The mansion is a puzzle dungeon. To access the basement where Vincent sleeps:
    1. Find the Safe combination: clues are hidden on notes around the mansion (Right 36, Left 10, Right 59, Right 97).
    2. Open the safe — Boss: Lost Number inside. Kill him for the Cosmo Memory (Red XIII's level 4 limit scroll) and the Basement Key.
    3. Use the Basement Key to access the lower library. Read the files in the right order. Then talk to Vincent in his coffin.
  • Vincent dialogue: Choose "Who are you?" → "Hojo" → he agrees to join if you mention Lucrecia. Don't accept "Leave me alone" — wake him again.
  • Materia Shop in Nibelheim: buy any Materia you've missed. Good selection including HP Plus and MP Plus.
Rocket Town & Cid
  • Rocket Town houses Cid Highwind — mandatory party member, joins automatically after the failed launch incident. He brings the Tiny Bronco plane (damaged — becomes a water-skimmer).
  • Before leaving Rocket Town: buy the Venus Gospel spear from the man near the rocket (trade a Materia for it — he's the one looking up at the rocket). This is Cid's ultimate weapon.
  • In the house north of the rocket: trade a Materia to get the Backpack — your item carrying capacity doubles.
Vincent: you must actively recruit him in the Shinra Mansion basement. He will NOT join automatically. Safe combination: Right 36, Left 10, Right 59, Right 97. Then basement key, files, then his coffin.
9

Wutai — The Missable Sidequest

Wutai Village · Da-chao Mountains▾
  • Wutai is accessible via the Tiny Bronco (water-skim to the western continent's northern peninsula). This sidequest closes permanently once you get the Highwind airship.
  • Upon arrival: if Yuffie is in your party, she steals all of your Materia and flees into Wutai. You must recover it — follow the story to retrieve it and defeat Don Corneo again.
  • Wutai Pagoda Challenge: After resolving the Materia theft storyline, fight all 5 floors of the Pagoda (Shake, Chekov, Staniv, Gorky, Godo). Beating Godo unlocks Yuffie's Level 4 Limit Break — All Creation. Also earns 3 all-element Elemental Materia.
Wutai is permanently inaccessible as a sidequest after obtaining the Highwind. Complete it with the Tiny Bronco on Disc 1–2. Yuffie must be recruited first for the Materia storyline to trigger.
10

Temple of the Ancients

Temple of the Ancients▾
  • The Temple is a time-loop dungeon — corridors reset around a central clock mechanism. Save at the save point near the entrance before going deep.
  • Clock Puzzle Room: the clock hands point to numbered rooms. Navigate them in sequence:
    — Room 2: Chest (Rocket Punch armor). Room 4: Chest (Megalixir). Room 5: Enemy Skill room — Morph enemy teaches Magic Hammer. Room 8: Chest (Ribbon — the best accessory in the game, nullifies all status).
    Don't miss the Ribbon in Room 8.
  • After the clock puzzle: descend deeper via a sliding rock puzzle. Save again before Demon's Gate.
Boss: Demon's Gate
  • HP ~10,000. Uses Demon Rush (heavy damage) and Paralysis Gas. He charges an attack called Debris — deal heavy damage before it fires. Petrify status can stop him temporarily. Gravity Materia (Demi) hits for ~2,500 per cast without worrying about Defense.
Demon's Gate: Use Gravity (Demi) repeatedly — deals ¼ of remaining HP each cast, very efficient. Keep party HP above 1,500 at all times. His Debris attack deals ~2,000 party damage when it connects.
The Ribbon accessory (nullifies ALL status effects) is in Room 8 of the Temple's clock puzzle. There are only 2 Ribbons easily obtainable in the game — this one and one from Disc 2. Do not miss it.
11

City of the Ancients — Aerith's Fate

Forgotten Capital · Cetra City▾
Point of No Return — Aerith Dies Here. Before entering the City of the Ancients: transfer all of Aerith's Materia to other party members. Equip her best accessory on someone else. Get her Great Gospel limit break first (Mythril trade).
  • Enemy Skill Materia #3: in a chest on the upper level of the Forgotten Capital's shell house. Pick it up before descending into the city proper.
  • The shell city has three areas: three shell-shaped houses. The center house contains a spiral staircase down to the underground level where Aerith prays.
Aerith's Fate (Story Cutscene)
  • Sephiroth descends. Aerith is killed. The party cannot prevent it. She is gone permanently from this point forward.
  • After the scene: Boss — Jenova LIFE immediately follows.
Boss: Jenova·LIFE
  • HP ~10,000. Ice weakness — Blizzard/Blizzara deals double damage. She uses Aqualung (one of the strongest Blue Magic spells) — if an Enemy Skill Materia is equipped here, it learns Aqualung automatically when she casts it.
  • After Jenova LIFE: the party grieves. Aerith is buried in the underwater lake.
Jenova LIFE: Ice attacks deal double damage. Keep her frozen with Blizzara/Blizzaga. Enemy Skill Materia equipped here will learn Aqualung when she casts it on your party — an excellent Blue Magic skill.
🌍

Discs 2–3 — The Planet Fights Back

The WEAPONs awake. Sephiroth descends into the Planet's core. The party must stop him before Meteor falls.

12

Great Glacier & Gaea's Cliff

Icicle Inn · Great Glacier · Gaea's Cliff▾
  • Icicle Inn: take the snowboard off the wall in the Inn (free). The snowboard minigame takes Cloud down the mountain — steer carefully to avoid trees, collect items on the slopes. Best run: center path for the Megalixir.
  • Great Glacier: large open snowfield, easy to get lost. Navigation tip: move east twice from the base, north twice, then east to the hot spring pool. Warming up at the hot spring is required — your body temperature meter fills from cold; if it reaches 0 you collapse and lose progress.
  • Key items in the Glacier: Ice Crystal (weapon upgrade material), Contain Materia (chest, south-central area), Alexander Summon Materia (examine the frozen statue woman in the northeast region of the glacier).
Gaea's Cliff — Navigation
  • 5-level ice cliff. Each level: find the handhold grips to climb. Your party must warm up at campfires on Levels 2 and 4 or they freeze and collapse.
  • Chests per level: Level 1: Ether. Level 2: Fire Armlet. Level 3: Elixir. Level 4: Javelin (Cid weapon). Level 5: Save Point + Megalixir.
  • Enemies: Jumping (Blue Dragon variant, teach Big Guard with Enemy Skill — highly recommended to learn here). Malboro — status-heavy, have Ribbons or Fairy Ring accessories equipped.
Big Guard is one of the best Enemy Skill spells — it casts Barrier, MBarrier, and Haste on the entire party simultaneously. Learn it from the Jumping enemy on Gaea's Cliff. Enemy Skill Materia must be equipped.
13

Northern Crater & the Highwind

Whirlwind Maze · Northern Crater · Highwind▾
  • Whirlwind Maze: straight path with several Sephiroth encounters (non-combat). Each encounter triggers story content — follow the path. No chests; don't worry about exploration here.
  • At the summit: the party confronts Sephiroth. Cloud's mind breaks — he hands the Black Materia to Sephiroth. The Weapons awake. Disc 1 ends.
  • Disc 2 opens: the party wakes in Junon. Cloud is missing. Take control of Tifa.
  • Execute Tifa/Barret escape from Junon Cannon: timed sequence, very forgiving. Don't worry about perfect execution.
  • After escape: regroup at Mideel → Cloud is there but catatonic. Cid takes command as party leader (mandatory until Cloud returns).
  • The party gains the Highwind airship — full world access opens.
Once you have the Highwind, the entire world is open. Priority list: complete Wutai (if not done), Nibelheim Mansion for Vincent, Fort Condor battles, Sleeping Man Mythril chain — all before advancing the story further.
14

Mideel & Cloud's Recovery

Mideel · Lifestream▾
  • Mideel is a small southern island town. Cloud is in the clinic there — catatonic, whispering. Tifa stays behind to care for him. Return here after completing some Highwind-era sidequests.
  • Ultimate Weapon (WEAPON boss) attacks Mideel. During the chaos, Cloud and Tifa fall into the Lifestream.
The Lifestream Sequence
  • Inside the Lifestream, Tifa pieces together Cloud's real memories. This is one of the most important story sequences — the truth about Nibelheim and Cloud's identity is revealed.
  • No combat — just cutscenes and dialogue choices. All choices are story; none affect gameplay.
  • Cloud recovers. He rejoins as party leader. The party's resolve is renewed.
  • After recovery: Tifa's Final Heaven limit break scroll is available from her Piano in Nibelheim (visit with Cloud in the party — he remembers the melody).
Final Heaven (Tifa's Ultimate Limit): visit her piano in Nibelheim with Cloud in the party after his Lifestream recovery. He plays the song, and the manual appears under the lid.
15

Fort Condor & Junon Revisited

Fort Condor · Junon · Diamond Weapon▾
Fort Condor — Final Battle
  • Fort Condor hosts a series of tower defense battles throughout the game. The final battle (defending the Condor's egg) must be completed before advancing the Junon Cannon story sequence.
  • Win the final battle to receive Barret's Catastrophe limit break scroll and a Huge Materia.
  • If the Condor dies (you fail the final battle or neglect the side quest), Barret's Catastrophe limit is lost permanently.
Diamond Weapon Assault on Midgar
  • Story event: Diamond Weapon rises from the ocean and attacks Midgar. The Junon Mako Cannon fires at it. Diamond Weapon fires back at Midgar.
  • This is a story battle on the Highwind deck — not a dungeon, just scripted. Diamond Weapon has ~40,000 HP and is fought in air. It opens its chest cavity to fire — attack during that window for full damage.
  • After the fight: Rufus is seemingly killed. The Sister Ray cannon is moved to Midgar. Midgar is the next story destination.
Barret's Catastrophe limit scroll: Fort Condor's final battle. The Condor bird must survive this battle. If you've been neglecting Fort Condor throughout, backtrack and win all prior battles to keep the quest active.
16

Sunken Gelnika — Optional Best Equipment

Gelnika (Sunken Shinra Plane)▾
  • The Gelnika is a crashed Shinra transport plane on the ocean floor, accessible by submarine (obtained in Disc 2 during the battle sequence near Junon). Park the Highwind, board the submarine, and dive.
  • Enemies here are the hardest regular encounters in the game (Sample:H0512, Schizo, Unknown types) — bring your best party or flee from anything that overwhelms you.
  • Key chests (8 total):
    — Conformer (Yuffie's ultimate weapon — morphs enemies into items)
    — Highwind (Cid's level 4 limit break scroll)
    — Escort Guard (best armor for Barret)
    — Outsider, Spirit Lance, Megalixir ×2, Source stat-up items
The Conformer (Yuffie's ultimate weapon from Gelnika) has a unique mechanic: its damage scales with the enemy's level. Against high-level enemies, it can deal 9,999 damage without Materia. Cid's Highwind limit scroll is here too — don't miss either.
17

Chocobo Breeding & Knights of the Round

Gold Saucer Stables · Icicle Area▾
  • Breed chocobos to reach the round island where Knights of the Round Materia is found — the most powerful summon in the game (13 separate attacks per cast).
  • Breeding steps:
    1. Catch two Good chocobos (near Gold Saucer) and two Great chocobos (Mideel area). Feed them Sylkis Greens (bought from Choco Billy's house for 5,000 each). Race them to S rank.
    2. Mate a Good (male) + Great (female) = Blue or Green chocobo (can cross mountains or rivers).
    3. Catch a Wonderful chocobo (Icicle area). Mate Wonderful + Blue/Green = Black chocobo (crosses mountains AND rivers).
    4. Catch a Gold chocobo naturally OR mate Black + Wonderful again to produce a Gold chocobo (crosses everything, including ocean).
  • Ride the Gold chocobo to the northeast round island (north of the icicle continent, surrounded by shallow water) to find Knights of the Round on the ground.
  • Also accessible on the round island: the Mime Materia on a different island (northwest area, ocean surrounded).
W-Summon Materia + Knights of the Round = 26 separate hits in one turn. With Master Summon and MP Turbo linked to KOTR, you can one-shot nearly any enemy including Emerald Weapon.
18

Ultimate WEAPONs & Final Preparations

World Map · Emerald/Ruby WEAPON▾
Ultimate WEAPON (Mandatory)
  • Ultimate WEAPON circles the world map. Ram the Highwind into it to initiate combat. It escapes after a few rounds — ram it again and again across different locations until it settles near Cosmo Canyon. Final battle there defeats it.
  • After defeating Ultimate WEAPON: it crashes into Cosmo Canyon, revealing the Ancient Forest dungeon (puzzle area). Inside: Apocalypse sword (Cloud's penultimate weapon), Master Command Materia, Slash-All Materia, Superball.
  • Cloud's Ultima Weapon (his best weapon) drops from this fight automatically.
Emerald WEAPON (Optional — Hardest in Game)
  • Emerald WEAPON swims the ocean floor — submarine can initiate the fight. HP ~1,000,000. It has 8 different deadly attacks including Aire Tam Storm (9,999 × number of Materia equipped to a character).
  • Strategy: use W-Summon + Knights of the Round twice per turn. Mime Materia copies the Summon for free. The HP Absorb Materia linked to KOTR lets you sustain. Bring Underwater Materia (from the old man in Kalm who trades for Odin) to remove the 20-minute timer.
  • Reward: Earth Harp → trade to Kalm traveler for Master Summon, Master Magic, Master Command Materia (fully mastered copies of all Materia in each category).
Ruby WEAPON (Optional — Second Hardest)
  • Ruby WEAPON is buried in the desert south of Gold Saucer. It appears after Meteor is summoned. HP ~800,000. Its trick: it buries its tentacles when any party member is alive other than Cloud — you must bring 2 dead party members to the fight for it to expose its claws.
  • Strategy: open with 2 dead party members. Use Cloud's W-Summon + KOTR combo. Reward: Desert Rose → trade to Kalm traveler for a Gold chocobo (skips breeding entirely).
19

Northern Cave — Final Dungeon

Northern Crater — Core▾
Final save point is outside the Northern Crater entrance. No return after descending. Ensure all sidequests, ultimate weapons, and Materia setups are complete.
  • The Northern Cave is a 5-layer descent to the Planet's core. Split-party mechanic for the middle sections (similar to FF9/FF6's multi-team dungeons).
  • Layer 1: Forked path. Both paths converge below. Left path: 5 chests (Speed Source, Guard Source, Elixir, Megalixir, Power Source). Right path: 4 chests (Magic Source, Mind Source, Lucky Source, Elixir).
  • Layer 2: Split into two groups of 3. Left team takes the lava path; right team takes the swamp path. Both reach a central area. 9 total chests across both paths — clear both before descending.
  • Layer 3 (Lower Cave): enemies are extremely strong (levels 50–65). Ultima, Reflect, and status immunity is critical. Enemies include Magic Pot (feed them Elixirs for massive AP) and Master Tonberry.
  • Layer 4 (Core): Save point. Final preparation. Below this: Jenova·SYNTHESIS then Safer Sephiroth.
Magic Pots appear in the Northern Cave and demand Elixirs. Give them — each one gives 8,000 AP (enough to nearly master multiple Materia). Bring 20+ Elixirs down the cave.
20

Safer Sephiroth — Final Battle

Planet's Core▾
  • Jenova·SYNTHESIS: HP ~60,000. Uses Ultima, Flare, Stop. Equip MBarrier (Mental Barrier) and Reflect. Hits hard but falls in 3–4 turns with KOTR. Uses parts of Aerith's theme music — one of the most emotional moments in the game.
  • Bizarro Sephiroth: HP ~100,000+ (split across segments). Keep all three party teams alive. Attack each body part: head (core), right/left arms. When the core HP depletes, the phase ends.
  • Safer Sephiroth: HP ~80,000. His signature attack — Super Nova — takes 3 minutes to animate and deals approximately 93% of each character's current HP (can never kill you in one hit from above 1 HP). Equip Ribbons, cast Big Guard, keep Haste up.
  • When Safer Sephiroth reaches ~20,000 HP: use Cloud's Omnislash limit break if available (9,999 × 15 hits = 149,985 damage).
One-Winged Angel — Final Form (Story)
  • After Safer Sephiroth falls: a solo scene. Cloud faces Sephiroth's true form alone. Only Omnislash is available — execute it to end the game.
  • If you never purchased Omnislash: Cloud's available limit breaks still work, just less efficiently. The fight is not hard mechanically.
Safer Sephiroth: Do NOT use Reflect (his Pale Horse hits allies). Cast Big Guard at the start (Haste + Barrier + MBarrier). Use W-Summon + KOTR or Omnislash Limit. Super Nova cannot kill — always leaves party at 1+ HP.
Complete Walkthrough · All GFs · Triple Triad · Every Missable

Final Fantasy V I I I

✦ ✦ ✦
Remastered Edition

From the SeeD exam on the beaches of Dollet to Ultimecia's castle outside time — every GF location, key Triple Triad cards, missable draw points, and Rinoa's wings.

✦

Introduction & the Junction System

▾
How Junction Works
  • Guardian Forces (GFs) are summoned creatures that you equip to characters. Each GF provides the character with commands (Magic, Draw, Item, GF) and junction slots for boosting stats.
  • Junctioning magic to stats: stock 100 copies of a spell for the maximum stat boost. Blizzaga ×100 junctioned to HP = +3,000 HP. Meltdown ×100 junctioned to Status Attack = 100% Slow/Meltdown on attacks.
  • Draw magic from enemies and draw points — draw until you have 100 of each spell you need. Key early spells to stock: Fire/Blizzard/Thunder (100 each), Scan (junction to HP), Sleep (junction to Magic or Strength).
  • Refine abilities: GFs like Quezacotl have Card Mod (turn cards into items) and T Mag-RF (turn items into spells). This is how you get powerful spells early without being high level.
  • Level scaling warning: enemies in FF8 scale with your party's average level. Do not grind — use Card ability to end battles without gaining EXP. Power comes from junctions, not levels.
Core junction strategy: stock Blizzaga/Firaga on HP, Meltdown on Str, Death on Status Attack, and Reflect on Mag. GF abilities like Med Data (doubles item effectiveness) and SumMag+ (boosts GF damage) are critical to unlock early.
✦
