⚔

GFs, Junctions, Draw Points & Boss Reference

▾
Junction Optimization — Priority Spells
The most efficient early-game strategy: win the Ifrit card from the Fire Cavern, refine it (Card Mod) to get 3× Flare, then use Diablos' Card Mod ability on enemy cards to accelerate spell accumulation. Draw 100× of each priority spell before moving on — you cannot go back to most draw points.
Ultima → HP Junction
Draw from: Ultima Weapon · Refine: GFAbl Mag RF (100 Ultima from 1 Ultima Stone)
Junctioning 100× Ultima to HP gives approximately +2,900 HP per character — far exceeding any other option. Draw from Ultima Weapon in the Deep Sea Research Center or refine from Ultima Stones via Diablos' Time Mag-RF. Priority #1 for late-game optimization.
Triple → Speed Junction
Draw from: Trauma (Disc 3), Galbadia Garden bosses · Draw Point: Trabia Garden
100× Triple junctioned to Speed gives the highest Speed bonus. Also crucial as a combat spell — triples the number of actions per character per turn. Draw as many as possible from each boss that has it. Rare until Disc 3.
Death → ST-Atk Junction
Draw from: various enemies in Tomb of the Unknown King area
Junctioning Death to ST-Atk makes every physical attack inflict instant death on most enemies — essentially a one-hit-kill for all regular encounters. Farm 100× Death as early as Disc 1 for this effect.
Full-Life → HP or Vit Junction
Draw from: Ruby Dragon (Centra ruins) · Refine: Life Magic RF (Monk's Code × 100)
High HP junction alternative to Ultima. Also invaluable as a combat spell. Draw from Ruby Dragon in Centra Ruins when accessible. Refining Monk's Codes (from Galbadian soldiers) gives a supply.
Meltdown → Str or Vit Junction
Draw from: Behemoth (Esthar area) · Refine: Forbid Med-RF
When cast in battle, reduces target's Vit to 0 — making all physical attacks deal massive damage regardless of defense. Stack Meltdown + Limit Breaks for reliable boss damage. Junction to Vit for substantial defense stats.
GF Acquisition & Ability Priorities
Ifrit
Disc 1: Fire Cavern (mandatory, timed battle)
First GF. Learn Card ability immediately (enables Card Mod chain). Str-J, Vit-J, and Elem-Atk-J are his key junctions. His card refines into Flare spells for early Str junctions.
Diablos
Disc 1: Use the Magic Lamp item (given by Headmaster Cid before Dollet mission)
Learn Time Mag-RF, Card Mod, and Encounter-Half/None abilities first. Time Mag-RF converts items into time magic spells. Card Mod converts cards to items and spells — the cornerstone of FF8's item economy. Encounter-None is essential for Northern Crater-style grinding avoidance.
Brothers (Sacred + Minotaur)
Disc 1: Tomb of the Unknown King (south of Deling City)
Requires solving the tomb's navigation puzzle: take the right path at every fork. Learn HP-J first — Brothers has the highest HP junction bonus. Vit-J and Eva-J are also valuable. Defeat Sacred, then Minotaur, then both together.
Carbuncle
Disc 1: Draw from Iguion bosses (Deling City parade)
Learn Mag-J and Spr-J first. Carbuncle's Reflect status cast on the whole party can bounce enemy spells back at them. Useful for the Sorceress boss fights where she spams high-tier magic.
Cerberus
Disc 2: Galbadia Garden — draw during the battle (or fight and draw before killing)
Grants Triple status to all party members — the most powerful buff in FF8. Learn Spd-J, Eva-J, and Hit-J first. ST-Mag-RF converts status-inflicting spells. Essential for late-game optimization.
Alexander
Disc 2: Draw from Edea boss fight (Galbadia Garden finale)
Holy-elemental summon, useful against undead and dark enemies. Learn Med Data first (doubles the effectiveness of healing items). Revive ability allows Phoenix Pinion-equivalent revival.
Doomtrain
Disc 3: Use Solomon Ring (collect 6 Steel Pipes, 6 Remedy+, 6 Malboro Tentacles)
Hard to obtain but powerful. When summoned, inflicts multiple status effects simultaneously. Learn Str+60% and Mag+60% from its ability list — the highest stat boost percentages in the game. Items are farmed from Malboro (Esthar area) for tentacles.
Bahamut
Disc 3: Deep Sea Research Center (requires defeating a series of bosses)
Learn Str+60%, Mag+60%, and Spd+40% first — top-tier stat junction abilities. Defeating him unlocks access to Ultima Weapon's chamber below. The Research Center is only accessible if you have the submarine or Ragnarok airship.
Eden
Disc 3: Draw from Ultima Weapon (Deep Sea Research Center)
Strongest summon in FF8, hits for 9,999 per hit up to 4 times (Str scaling). Learn Spd+40%, Eva+30%, and Luck+50% abilities. Also learn Devour ability — eating enemies can permanently raise stats. Devour Ruby Dragons for HP+10, Behemoths for Str+1.
Pandemona
Disc 2: Draw from Fujin boss (Balamb Town)
Spd-J is Pandemona's defining ability — the highest Speed junction bonus available from any GF. Learn Spd-J first. Also teaches Spd+20% and Spd+40% for passive speed bonuses.
Card Mod & Refine Priority — Key Conversions
Ifrit Card → 3× Flare
Win Ifrit Card from the Fire Cavern (after defeating Ifrit)
Use Card Mod (Diablos ability) to convert. Flare junctioned to Str gives a strong early-game attack stat bonus. Only do this if you have a second Ifrit Card — or draw the GF first and then use the card.
Laguna Card → 100× Megalixir
Win Laguna Card from the CC Group (Balamb Garden Disc 2)
100 Megalixirs from one card. Megalixirs fully restore HP/MP for all party members. Stock before Disc 3 endgame for failsafe healing during Ultimecia's Castle.
Bahamut Card → 100× Megalixir
Win from Bahumut card player (card clubs)
Alternative Megalixir source. Refine via GF-Med-RF (Diablos ability). Can also be refined to 100× Ultima by using higher-tier refine chains.
Three Stars → Spd/Triple stock
Refine from: Rare items, end-game drops · Also purchased in Esthar shops (Disc 3+)
Three Stars remove casting time from all spells (Double → Double, Triple → Triple instant). Makes Triple+Eden or Triple+Ultima fully instantaneous — critical for time-pressure boss fights.
Boss Quick Reference
NORG
Disc 2: Balamb Garden basement · HP: ~20,000 · Weakness: Fire
Pod opens when you break the left/right orbs down to same color (both green or both red). Attack pod only when open. Has Slow-Petrify attack. Draw Leviathan from him if you want it early — only other source is in Disc 3.
Edea (Disc 2)
Disc 2: Galbadia Garden parade · HP: ~20,000 · Weakness: Fire
Draw Alexander from her — this is the only opportunity. She casts Haste on herself and uses Ice Strike (all party). Use Limit Breaks and Quistis's Micro Missiles or Shockwave Pulsar for fast kills. Don't forget to DRAW first.
Trauma
Disc 3: Lunatic Pandora · HP: ~10,000 · Draw: Triple
Draw Triple from Trauma — one of the earliest sources. Destroys the Propagator sub-bosses to prevent Trauma from regenerating. Use physical attacks as Trauma is magic-resistant.
Adel
Disc 3: Lunatic Pandora · HP: ~60,000 · Draw: Ultima
Rinoa is held hostage — AOE magic will hit her. Use only single-target spells or physical attacks. Draw Ultima from Adel. Adel absorbs magic cast on Rinoa to heal herself. Keep Rinoa's HP above 1,000.
Ultimecia (Final Form)
Disc 4: Ultimecia's Castle · HP: ~60,000 per form (4 forms total) · Weakness: None
Four-phase battle. Each phase absorbs one GF ability junction. Bring Holy War (Angel Wing status) or the maximum-stat party. Cast Meltdown, then Limit Break spam. Ultimecia drains one GF from your roster each phase. Draw Apocalypse and Flare from later forms. Time your Limits — she resets party actions when shifting phases.
🎓

Discs 1–3 — SeeD and the World's Fate

Squall reluctantly leads. A sorceress from the future rewrites time. Garden against Garden, mercenary against memory.

1

Balamb Garden & the SeeD Field Exam

Balamb Garden · Dollet▾
  • Before the exam: Access the computer in Squall's classroom (second floor, left terminal) to receive Quezacotl and Shiva GFs. Don't skip this — they're not given otherwise.
  • Visit the library and talk to the girl studying — she's looking for a magazine. Come back several times for Triple Triad card rewards.
  • Fire Cavern: mandatory pre-exam dungeon. Boss: Ifrit — Draw Fire and Blizzard from him during battle. He's weak to Ice. Time limit is generous at 10 minutes.
Dollet — The SeeD Mission
  • Land on Dollet beach with Squall, Zell, Seifer. Advance to the Communication Tower — linear path, fight through Galbadia soldiers.
  • Communication Tower boss: Elvoret. This is the ONLY opportunity to draw Siren GF. Draw from Elvoret before killing him — she will not be available anywhere else in story battles.
  • After Elvoret: a dog (X-ATM092) chases the team down the tower and across Dollet. You must outrun it — fight it occasionally to slow it down, but don't try to kill it here (it will rebuild itself). Full escape triggers the cutscene.
Elvoret: Draw Siren GF first — this takes 2–3 Draw actions. Once you have Siren, kill Elvoret normally. Siren's key ability (L Mag-RF) lets you refine spells from items, which is invaluable early game.
Siren GF: Draw her from Elvoret during the Dollet Communication Tower battle. This is the ONLY guaranteed opportunity. Missing her forces a long workaround via rare card conversion later.
2

Timber & the Forest Owls

Timber · Galbadia▾
  • First mission as SeeDs: escort Rinoa and the Forest Owls resistance group. Board the train in Balamb and head to Timber — the occupied city of Galbadia.
  • Timber train mission: switch the cargo train cars by operating the coupling switches in sequence. Easy puzzle — follow the diagram on the wall of the train car.
  • The plan fails. Squall, Rinoa, and the team are now outlaws in Galbadia. Travel overland to Galbadia Garden for new orders.
  • Along the road north to Deling City: Chocobo Forest — rent a Chocobo for faster travel. The forests contain hidden Chicobo puzzles; whistling summons them, then use the net at the right time. Solve all 6 forests for the Chicobo Card (rare).
Galbadia Garden — Mission Briefing
  • Galbadia Garden assigns the team: assassinate the Sorceress Edea at the Deling City parade.
  • Irvine joins here as a new party member. He uses a gun — his limit break is Shot, which uses different ammunition types for different effects.
  • Draw points throughout Galbadia Garden: Double, Haste, Esuna. Stock 100 of each from these draw points if you can.
3

Deling City — The Sorceress Parade

Deling City · Presidential Residence▾
  • Deling City: split the party. Team A (Squall's group) infiltrates via the sewer system. Team B (Rinoa + Irvine) rides a float in the parade — Irvine tries to snipe Edea.
  • Sewer dungeon: 3 floors, solve the valve puzzles to raise and lower water levels. Navigate to the Presidential Residence to set up the Sniper spot. Chests: Zombie/Slow/Esuna items.
  • Irvine's snipe fails — Edea is too powerful. She counterattacks: party falls into the parade arena.
Boss: Seifer (again) + Boss: Edea
  • Seifer: HP ~3,000. Draw Firaga from him. Use junctioned physical attacks.
  • Edea: HP ~4,000. Draw Carbuncle GF from the Iguion statues before fighting her (or draw Carbuncle from Edea directly). Edea uses Blizzaga and Ice Strike. Draw Cure/Cura from her. At low HP she uses Maelstrom — it reduces the party to single-digit HP. Have a healer ready or use Regen junction.
Edea: Draw Carbuncle from the two Iguion statues before the Edea fight (or draw it from Edea herself). Carbuncle casts Reflect on the party — most of Edea's attacks bounce back at her. After her Maelstrom hits, Cure immediately.
4

Tomb of the Unknown King

Tomb — East of Deling▾
  • Squall needs a code name to present at Galbadia Garden. The code is found in the Tomb of the Unknown King east of Deling City — a circular maze dungeon.
  • Tomb navigation: the tomb is a looping circular corridor with 6 side rooms. Draw the map as you go. The key rooms:
    — Obelisk Room (north): examine the obelisk for a clue number (part of the code).
    — Sacred's Room (east): fight Sacred (minotaur). Draw Regen, Leviathan (do NOT miss drawing Leviathan here — available again from NORG but easier now), then defeat him.
    — Minotaur's Room (northwest): fight Minotaur. Together they summon the Brothers GF.
  • The code for Galbadia Garden is formed from the 3 numbers found in the three obelisk rooms.
Brothers (Sacred + Minotaur): Both are Earth/Physical types — Holy attacks deal bonus damage. Draw Leviathan from Sacred before killing him. The Brothers GF teaches High Mag-RF and Med Data (doubles item healing) — level it up to unlock these first.
Disc 1 Triple Triad — Key Cards to Win
  • Ifrit card: win from the Fire Cavern NPC before the SeeD exam.
  • Quistis card: win from the Triple Triad player in the Balamb Garden lobby, 2F.
  • Seifer card: win during the party in Balamb Garden the night before the exam.
  • Zell card: win from the girl in the library. Talk to her multiple times.
  • Angelo card: win from Watts on the Forest Owls' train after Timber.
  • Card Mod (Quezacotl ability): refine rare cards into items. Seifer card → 3 Diamond Armors → 3 Protect +100. Excellent stat boost for Disc 1.
5

Galbadia Garden & Trabia Garden

Missile Base · Trabia · Balamb▾
  • Split into two teams: Team Squall (infiltrate the Missile Base) and Team Selphie (return to warn Balamb Garden).
  • Missile Base: Squall's team wears Galbadian uniforms. Don't run — walk past guards. Wrong answers during conversations trigger battles. Navigate to the launch control room and sabotage the missiles.
  • Team Selphie fights inside Balamb Garden as it mobilizes — Garden fights Garden for the first time in the game's history.
  • After reuniting: Balamb Garden reaches FH (Fishermans Horizon). NORG is discovered in the basement — mandatory boss.
Boss: NORG
  • HP ~4,000. NORG is protected by two Pods (left/right). Kill both pods first to make NORG vulnerable. Draw Leviathan GF from NORG directly if you missed it from Sacred.
  • Draw Reflect from NORG's pods. NORG switches between yellow mode (weak to magic) and purple mode (weak to physical) — match your attacks to his current mode color.
NORG: Kill the left and right Pods first. Draw Leviathan from NORG directly. Attack based on color — yellow = use magic, purple = use physical. Don't waste Limit Breaks on the pods.
6

Battle of the Gardens

Balamb Garden vs Galbadia Garden▾
  • The two Gardens collide. Balamb Garden students fight Galbadia Garden students in a full-scale war. You have free movement during the battle — help students fight, advance the story, or both.
  • Inside Galbadia Garden: find Cerberus in the center hall. Walk up to him and initiate the conversation — he challenges you to fight. Win to receive him as a GF. He grants Triple and Speed junction abilities.
  • After Cerberus: boss gauntlet ends with Edea again.
Boss: Seifer + Boss: Edea (Final)
  • Seifer again — same strategy. Draw Aura from him if available.
  • Edea: Draw Alexander GF from her during this fight. She uses Maelstrom again (single-digit HP) — have Selphie's Limit Ready for Full-Cure or keep Hi-Potions available. After this fight Edea is freed from the sorceress's possession.
Edea (Disc 2 final): Draw Alexander GF before killing her — last chance for this GF in a story fight. After the fight, Edea joins temporarily and explains the truth about the sorceress chain and the mission to travel to Esthar.
7

FH · Balamb Occupation · Trabia · Esthar

Fishermans Horizon · Balamb · Trabia · Winhill · Esthar▾
Fishermans Horizon (FH)
  • FH is a peaceful town built on an old offshore oil rig. The mayor, Dobe, is a pacifist — he distrusts Squall's military attitude. Follow the story and talk to all NPCs for lore.
  • Galbadian attack on FH: Galbadian soldiers arrive and take hostages. Squall's team fights through 3 waves to reach the mayor's crane. Boss: BGH251F2 (mobile tank) + two soldiers.
  • After the fight: concert scene — Selphie organizes an impromptu concert on the FH stage. This is a critical junction: you must play the right song. Choose the wrong one and the scene is short; choose "Eyes on Me" or keep trying until Selphie is satisfied for the full version with a hidden Odine Bangle reward.
  • FH shop: Draw Curaga from the draw point near the shoreline. Stock 100.
Balamb Town Occupation (Disc 2)
  • Balamb has been occupied by Galbadia — specifically, Fujin and Raijin are searching for a "Rinoa." Search the town to find out what happened.
  • Talk to everyone in town — the girl's father by the hotel, the captain by the shore — to trigger the proper sequence. Ultimately, Fujin and Raijin challenge Squall for the last time in Disc 2.
  • Draw points in Balamb town: Ultima draw point near the train station (fixed, not random). Draw 10 per visit until you have 100.
Fujin + Raijin (Balamb): Fujin uses Wind attacks (immune to wind). Raijin uses Thunder and physical. Focus Fujin first — she uses Sai (removes party member from battle). After she's down, Raijin surrenders. Draw Aero from Fujin for the wind junction.
Trabia Garden
  • Selphie's home Garden was bombed by Galbadia. Explore the ruins for items: Hero (Holy War precursor) ×2, Remedy ×3, Hi-Potion ×6.
  • Key story scene: the party sits in the rubble and realizes they all grew up in the same orphanage under Edea's care. GFs suppress personal memory — they had all known each other as children and forgotten.
  • Irvine reveals he remembers because he was never given a GF. This leads to Edea explaining the mission's true context.
Winhill — Laguna Flashback
  • The party experiences a Laguna dream sequence in Winhill — a small town where Laguna spent years caring for a young girl named Raine. The girl he's raising is significant to the story's final revelation.
  • Winhill side fight: Laguna (in dream) with Kiros and Ward hunts monsters on the cliff path — tutorial-level difficulty, just survive.
  • After the dream: the party understands more of Laguna's past. His relationship to Squall is the game's largest unspoken reveal.
Esthar City
  • Esthar is a massive futuristic city hidden under a cloaking field on the eastern continent. The city is navigated via a series of walkway panels — follow the glowing arrows to reach different districts.
  • Key stops in Esthar: Presidential Palace (meet Laguna — he was elected president after defeating the sorceress Adel 17 years ago), Odine's Laboratory (the scientist who studied GFs and created the junction system), Sorceress Memorial (a stasis facility designed to imprison sorceresses).
  • Esthar shops: The best shops in the game open here. Buy 60× Megalixirs, Holy Wars (available from Esthar Pet Shop for Gysahl Greens), and the Renew item. Stock up heavily — Disc 4 has no shops at all.
  • Draw points in Esthar: Meteor (east district), Flare (palace approach). Stock both to 100.
  • Rinoa falls into a coma in Esthar. Squall carries her to the Sorceress Memorial while the party watches.
Disc 4 prep — stock list: Before the Lunar Base sequence begins in earnest, ensure you have: Aura ×100 (junction or drawn from mobile draw points), Full-Life ×100 (draw from Forbidden/Behemoth), Ultima ×100 (draw point in Esthar), Megalixir ×20+, Holy War ×6+, Elixir ×20+. Also draw points reset on world travel — revisit them.
8

Lunar Base & Escape from Space

Lunar Gate · Lunar Base · Ragnarok▾
  • Squall and Rinoa travel by Lunar Gate elevator to the Lunar Base — a space station near the moon. The moon's surface is covered in dormant monsters from the Lunar Cry.
  • Rinoa is possessed by Ultimecia's spirit and releases the Sorceress Adel from her orbital prison — triggering a Lunar Cry. The Lunar Cry rains monsters on Esthar below.
  • Squall drifts in space, reaches Rinoa's floating body, and in zero-gravity finds the Ragnarok airship. Piloting it through monster hordes to safety is one of the most visually spectacular sequences in the game.
Ragnarok Airship — Escape
  • Navigate the Ragnarok through its monster-infested corridors. The monsters here (Propagators — come in color pairs) must all be killed: when you kill one of a pair, the other becomes angry and aggressive. Kill both of a pair at the same time, or kill the aggressive one fast.
  • 8 Propagator pairs on 3 floors. Clear all pairs to proceed to the bridge. Use magic to stun a pair, then kill them quickly in sequence.
  • After clearing the ship: Ragnarok is your permanent airship for Disc 3 and 4.
Disc 4 has no shops. Before the Lunatic Pandora sequence ends and Disc 4 begins, spend time in Disc 3 stocking Aura, Full-Life, Ultima, and consumables. Buy Gysahl Greens for Chocobo summoning, Holy Wars for invincibility, and Megalixirs.
9

Disc 3: Lunatic Pandora

Esthar · Lunatic Pandora▾
  • The Lunatic Pandora — a massive crystalline structure — moves toward Esthar to trigger a second Lunar Cry intentionally. Squall's team infiltrates it.
  • The Pandora has 4 zones: enter through the side hatch (time your approach with the Ragnarok — it moves). Navigate upward through 3 floors of high-level enemies.
  • Key enemies: Behemoth (Draw Meteor), Tri-Face (Draw Curse — junction to Status Attack for Sleep/Slow/Poison on hit), Malboros (status-heavy — preemptive kills recommended).
Boss Sequence: Raijin + Fujin → Seifer → Adel
  • Raijin + Fujin: Draw Pandemona GF from Fujin during this fight. Physical attacks on both. Raijin paralysis-counters — use ranged attacks or magic.
  • Seifer (third fight): Draw Aura from him. He's much stronger now — limit breaks recommended.
  • Adel (final Disc 3 boss): She holds Rinoa hostage — Rinoa absorbs some damage from attacks that miss Adel. Use Draw on Adel (draws from Rinoa's HP) rather than attacking directly. Junction Life or Full-Life to Rinoa preemptively. Draw Meteor from Adel. Kill her without hitting Rinoa too hard.
Adel: Never use AoE attacks — Rinoa takes splash damage. Use Draw on Adel to drain her HP while transferring her spells. Junction Full-Life to Status Defense for Rinoa. When Adel's HP is low, use a strong single-target Limit to finish her safely.
⏳

Disc 4 — Time Compression

Ultimecia compresses all of time into a single moment. The party fights through dissolving reality to reach her castle outside of time.

10

Ultimecia's Castle

Ultimecia's Castle (Time Compressed)▾
No shops on Disc 4. All preparation must be done before entering Ultimecia's Castle. Stock Aura, Full-Life, Megalixirs, Holy Wars. Ensure all GFs have their essential abilities unlocked.
  • The castle seals all GF commands, magic, items, and limit breaks at the start. You must defeat 8 bosses scattered throughout the castle — each boss defeated restores one sealed ability.
  • Priority abilities to restore: Magic first, then GF, then Items, then Limit Breaks. Choose which bosses to fight in which order based on which abilities you want back first.
  • Castle layout: 5 main areas connected by a central courtyard. Each area has a boss at its culmination:
    — Art Gallery (Krysta — restores Magic)
    — Chapel (Tri-Point — restores GF)
    — Treasure Room (Gargantua — restores Draw)
    — Master Room (Red Giant — restores Items)
    — Armory (Catoblepas — restores Command Abilities)
    — Underground (Trauma — restores Limit Breaks)
    — Clock Tower (Sphinxaur/Sphinxara — restores Magic)
    — Wine Cellar (Cerberus doppelganger — restores GF summons)
  • Save point is in the central courtyard. Use it between each boss.
Krysta drops a Star Fragment (refines to Spd-J Scroll). Tri-Point is weak to the elements it's not using — watch which element it charges and exploit the opposite. Red Giant is immune to magic; use physical attacks only.
11

Final Bosses — Ultimecia

Ultimecia's Throne Room▾
  • After all 8 castle bosses: ascend to the throne room. Ultimecia possesses Rinoa briefly (gut-punch moment), then the true final sequence begins.
  • The party cycles — only 3 characters fight at a time, and when one falls they're replaced by a reserve character. Plan your party order so your strongest 3 go first.
Ultimecia → Griever → Ultimecia+Griever → Ultimecia Final
  • Phase 1 — Ultimecia: HP ~40,000. She casts Maelstrom (reduces party to low single-digit HP) and Apocalypse (near-instant kill). Use Aura items for Limit Breaks. Have a healer active at all times.
  • Phase 2 — Griever: HP ~100,000. Griever is Squall's imaginary ultimate beast made manifest. Randolph (his limit) dispels your junctions. Keep GF summoning — the GF HP pool absorbs damage while the summoning animation plays.
  • Phase 3 — Ultimecia+Griever: HP ~100,000. She uses Shockwave Pulsar (massive party damage). Triple + Aura + Limit Breaks are the fastest way through.
  • Phase 4 — Ultimecia Final: HP ~60,000. Hell's Judgement reduces everyone to 1 HP. Keep Full-Life (or Angel Wing limit from Rinoa) ready. This is the last phase — go all out.
Ultimecia Final: Her Hell's Judgement sets all party HP to 1. Pre-junction Full-Life, have Holy War items for invincibility, and keep Aura status on for constant Limit Breaks. Squall's Renzokuken with Lion Heart hit can deal 100,000+ damage per limit activation.
12

Sidequests & Completion

World Map · Various▾
Deep Sea Research Center (Bahamut + Eden)
  • Southwest corner of the world map — a platform rising from the ocean. Accessible on Disc 2+ by landing the Ragnarok nearby and entering on foot.
  • Puzzle: a steam vent room. To proceed without fighting extra battles: choose NOT to inject steam. Each wrong choice triggers a battle (these battles are winnable and give AP — but the puzzle shortcut skips them).
  • Boss sequence: Bahamut (Draw Flare and Tornado from him) then fight through to Ultima Weapon. Draw Eden GF from Ultima Weapon — the most powerful GF, deals ~60,000–70,000 damage at max level.
Centra Ruins (Odin + Tonberry)
  • 20-minute timer for Odin. Navigate the 4-puzzle tower fast — the order is: floor 1 statue puzzle → floor 2 stone tablet → floor 3 eye lens → floor 4 Odin's room. With practice, completable in 8–10 minutes.
  • After Odin: fight 20 Tonberry enemies anywhere in the ruins. The 21st encounter triggers Tonberry King. Win to get the Tonberry GF — his abilities (LV Down, LV Up, Initiative) are extremely valuable.
Triple Triad — CC Group & Key Cards
  • CC Group quest: aboard the Ragnarok on Disc 3, beat 6 CC Group members in sequence to eventually challenge Card Master King. Rewards include the Gilgamesh card (refines to 3 Holy Wars — invincibility items), the Laguna card, and the Squall card (refines to Three Stars → Ultima ×100).
  • Rare card refinements via Card Mod (Quezacotl ability):
    — Rinoa card → Healing Ring → Curaga ×100
    — Squall card → Three Stars → Ultima ×100
    — Laguna card → Hero ×100 (single-use invincibility)
    — Gilgamesh card → 3 Holy Wars (party invincibility)
  • Card Club Queen is in Balamb Garden's 2nd floor hall. Beat her to get the Queen of Cards quest — she travels to different towns and her matches unlock rare cards through a chain of losses to her.
Shumi Village
  • Located north of Esthar on the western continent. The Shumi people are building a statue of Laguna. Help them gather materials (Iron Giant drop, Malboro tentacle, Cactuar needle) for the sculptor. Reward: Monk's Code item (teaches Counter ability to GF).
  • Also accessible: the Shumi elder gives Squall a Luck+50 stat boost if you complete the statue quest on Disc 3.
Chocobo World & Chocobo Forests
  • 6 Chocobo Forests are scattered across the world map. Use the Chicobo whistle, then net a Chicobo after it appears. Solve all 6 forests to receive the Chicobo card (refines to 100 Gysahl Greens → Chocobo Feather → Initiative ability junction).
  • Boko the chocobo (from Chocobo World on PC/remaster) can be sent out during gameplay to gather random items. Over time he brings back stat-boosting items including Speed Up, Luck Up, and various GF items.
Omega Weapon (PC/Remaster exclusive)
  • Omega Weapon is in the right wing of Ultimecia's Castle, after lighting 4 specific torches in the correct order. HP: 1,000,000. He uses Megido Flame (reduces all HP to 1) and Gravija (cuts HP by 75%).
  • Strategy: equip Rinoa's Angel Wing (permanent Magic status) with Full-Life, stock Aura status, and use Lion Heart limit. One player keeps the party alive with Hero (invincibility items) while others deal damage. Eden GF + Boost at max = ~250,000 damage.

Final Fantasy I X

✦ ✦ ✦
PC / Console Edition

From the theatre ship Primo Vista to the Crystal World — every synthesis item, friendly monster encounter, Stellazzio coin, and Tetra Master card. A love letter to the series.

✦

Introduction & Ability System

▾
How Abilities Work
  • Characters learn abilities from equipped equipment. Each piece of gear has 1–3 abilities attached. Equip the item, earn AP in battles, and the ability unlocks permanently — then you can equip it even without the item.
  • Each character has a limited number of Magic Stones (ability slots). Balance your equipped abilities to fit within your stone budget.
  • Auto-Abilities (Killer, Auto-Regen, Auto-Haste, etc.) are passive and active automatically. Prioritize learning Auto-Haste (adds Haste permanently) and Auto-Regen (constant HP regeneration) early.
  • Synthesis: combine two items at a Synthesis shop to create new equipment. Some of the best weapons and armor in the game are synthesis-only. Keep old equipment instead of selling it — many synthesis recipes require items you'd otherwise discard.
Steal Strategy
  • Zidane (and later Amarant) can Steal from enemies. Every enemy has up to 4 steal slots (Common, Uncommon, Rare, Very Rare). The odds improve when the enemy's HP is lower — weaken before stealing.
  • Bosses always have rare steals worth getting. Equip Bandit/Master Thief abilities to increase steal rate. Some steals are the only way to get certain equipment.
Never sell old equipment — synthesis recipes require previously-worn gear. Keep every piece of armor and weapon in your inventory throughout the game.
!

Missables Checklist

▾
🔴
Excalibur II (Best Sword)In Memoria (final dungeon, Disc 4). Requires reaching it in under 12 hours of total play time. If time is over 12 hours, this item is permanently missable. Plan a focused playthrough if you want it.
🔴
Friendly Monster side questVarious monsters across the world ask for items (Ore, Phoenix Down, Ether, etc.). Give them what they ask for free AP and experience. All 9 must be encountered and appeased before the final dungeon.
🔴
Quina recruitment (both times)Qu's Marsh — Disc 1 near Lindblum, then again in Disc 2 near Conde Petie. Must visit both times. If Quina is not recruited before the Black Mage Village, she joins automatically but with less story content.
🔴
Stellazzio Coins (12 total)Hidden throughout the world, collected for Queen Stella in Treno. Don't sell them. Final reward (13th coin) is a Hammer — refines to 15 Ore.
🔴
Jump Rope mini-game (Alexandria)Get 1,000 jumps in a row for the Faerie Earrings. Get 20 for the first card reward. Available in early Disc 1 and early Disc 3 (Dagger solo section). Very hard.
🔴
Chocograph treasuresPlay Chocobo Hot & Cold at Chocobo's Forest, Air Garden, and Lagoon to find Chocographs. Each leads to a buried treasure on the world map. Several contain key items (Dead Pepper, Ozma access).
🔴
Beatrix steals (3 fights)You fight Beatrix 3 times — she always survives. Each fight: steal her gear (Thunder Gloves, Ice Brand, Mythril Sword). These are the only sources of these items early in the game.
⚔

Steal List, Synthesis, Abilities & Boss Reference

▾
Boss Steal List — Complete (Steal Before Killing)
Every entry below represents a permanently missable steal if you kill the boss without stealing. Always exhaust all steal attempts on each boss, especially Rare/Uncommon items. Zidane's Master Thief ability (from Thief Gloves) dramatically improves rare steal rates.
Baku
Disc 1: Prima Vista · Rare: Wrist · Common: Leather Hat
Tutorial boss. The Wrist is a rare steal — useful for early Dagger/Vivi stat boosts. Steal before finishing the fight.
Steiner (Battle 1 & 2)
Disc 1: Alexandria · Rare: Iron Sword · Common: Potion
Two separate fights with Steiner. The Iron Sword from the Rare steal position is an early weapon upgrade for the Steiner sections of the game. Steiner rejoins the party so the weapon would be equipped to him.
Prison Cage
Disc 1: Evil Forest · Rare: Mythril Dagger · Common: Potion
Mythril Dagger is Zidane's second weapon tier. Grab it here — you won't find another copy easily until much later. This is the only Mythril Dagger steal opportunity before synthesis becomes available.
Plant Brain
Disc 1: Evil Forest · Rare: Ore · Common: Potion
Strike with Fire and physical attacks. Steal the Ore for early synthesis ingredients. Plant Brain attacks by calling Plant Spiders — kill the spiders to prevent their Sleep/Silence attacks.
Black Waltz No. 1
Disc 1: Ice Cavern · Rare: Remedy · Common: Mage Masher
Remedy is rare — grab it. Black Waltz 1 uses Blizzara. He has low HP; steal quickly before the fight ends. Mage Masher is useful for Zidane if you didn't steal the Mythril Dagger from Prison Cage.
Black Waltz No. 2
Disc 1: Dali Mill · Rare: Mythril Dagger · Common: Ether
Another Mythril Dagger opportunity. If you missed the Prison Cage steal, do not miss this one. Black Waltz 2 can summon Blizzara storms — prioritize stealing over healing.
Black Waltz No. 3
Disc 1: Cargo Ship · Rare: Linen Cuirass · Common: Ether
He flees and reappears at Pinnacle Rocks (Disc 1). Try to steal from both encounters. Linen Cuirass is good mid-Disc 1 armor. He's the strongest early boss — use physical attacks and Fire from Vivi.
Sealion
Disc 1: Burmecia Gate · Rare: Mythril Gloves · Common: Ether
Mythril Gloves are great for Freya or Steiner. Sealion uses Blizzara + Tsunami — both deal heavy damage to the full party. Bring Fire and healing.
Gizamaluke
Disc 1: Gizamaluke's Grotto · Rare: Mythril Gloves · Common: Magician Shoes
Another Mythril Gloves opportunity. Requires 4 Kupo Nuts (collected in the dungeon) to open the inner door. Gizamaluke's Silence Bell move silences your entire party — equip Protect Rings or stockpile Echo Screens.
Beatrix (All Encounters)
Disc 1: Burmecia · Disc 2: Cleyra / Alexandria · Rare: Thunder Gloves, Ice Brand, Save the Queen
Three story battles. Each Beatrix fight has different rare steals: Burmecia — Thunder Gloves; Cleyra — Ice Brand (Steiner's sword); Alexandria — Save the Queen (Beatrix's own weapon). All three fights are unwinnable (she casts Stock Break when HP falls low). Steal fast — you have ~3 turns before she resets.
Ralvuimago
Disc 2: Outer Continent · Rare: Mythril Sword · Common: Ether
Mythril Sword upgrades Steiner. First boss on the Outer Continent — stock up on Potions before this area. Uses Venom to Poison the party.
Lani
Disc 2: Madain Sari area · Rare: Ether · Common: Survival Vest
Survival Vest is good armor for Zidane. Lani switches targets mid-fight — she'll focus on Dagger if Zidane deals too much damage. Use Freya's Jump to stay out of range and cycle targets.
Fossil Roo Troll / Friendly Yan
Disc 2: Fossil Roo area · Rare: Ether · Common: Hi-Potion
Fossil Roo has multiple trolls who are optional — but the steals are worth it. Friendly monsters throughout the game (Yan, Lani etc.) give rewards if given specific items — track the Friendly Monster chain for a Pumice Piece at the end.
Antlion
Disc 2: Fossil Roo · Rare: Mythril Vest · Common: Ether
Mythril Vest for good armor upgrade. Antlion uses Sandstorm (party damage) and counterattacks with Sand Storm when hit by magic. Stick to physical attacks and steal first.
Hilgigars
Disc 2: Conde Petie Mountain Path · Rare: Lamia's Tiara · Common: Ether
Lamia's Tiara teaches Zidane Annoy and Freya several abilities. Uses Stomping Stomp (massive single-target damage). Keep party HP above 500. Steal priority: High.
Scarecrow / Hades
Disc 3: Ipsen's Castle · Rare: Running Shoes · Common: Battle Boots
Ipsen's Castle has inverted weapon damage — weaker weapons deal more damage. Equip your worst equipment. Running Shoes are among the best accessories — they grant Haste permanently. Priority steal.
Nova Dragon
Disc 3: Gaia (outer world) · Rare: Elixir · Common: Hi-Potion
One of the hardest random encounters — Nova Dragon appears on the world map in Disc 3+. Drops excellent EXP and AP. Uses Twister (wind-elemental party hit) and Flash Flame. Steal for Elixirs if farming.
Kuja (All Forms)
Disc 3–4: Pandemonium / Crystal World · Rare: Black Robe · Common: Ether
Kuja's Trance form (second fight) is the penultimate boss. Steal Black Robe in the first Pandemonium fight — it teaches Vivi key abilities. Kuja uses Flare Star (non-elemental full-party damage scaling with character levels) and Holy.
Lich / Maliris / Tiamat / Kraken (Crystal Guardians)
Disc 4: Crystal World · Rare: Circlet/Dark Matter/Ninja Gear/Octagon Rod
Four elemental guardians guard the Crystal World. Each has unique rare steals. Lich — Circlet (great helm); Maliris — Ninja Gear (Zidane's best early endgame armor); Tiamat — Dark Matter; Kraken — Octagon Rod. All permanent — steal before attacking.
Necron (Final Boss)
Disc 4: Crystal World · Rare: Elixir · Common: Remedy
Necron appears with no warning after Kuja's death — no save point before him. Ensure the party has full HP/MP and all Limit Break gauges ready before Kuja's final phase. He uses Grand Cross (random status effects on all characters) and Neutron Ring (party near-death). Keep Auto-Regen and Life equipped.
Synthesis Shop Guide — Key Items
Butterfly Sword (Zidane)
Synthesize: Dagger + Mage Masher (3,500 gil) · Lindblum or Alexandria
Zidane's first synthesis weapon. Teaches Flee-Gil and What's That!? abilities. Better than either component — always synthesize this early.
The Ogre (Zidane)
Synthesize: 2× Mage Masher (7,000 gil) · Lindblum
Teaches Sacrifice and Annoy. Strong Disc 1 weapon upgrade. Requires two Mage Mashers — buy or steal both. Ogre becomes available after the Festival of the Hunt.
Exploda (Zidane)
Synthesize: Mage Masher + Mythril Dagger (10,000 gil) · Treno
Teaches Annoy and Sacrifice. Solid Disc 2 dagger — synthesize this at Treno's shop on the Outer Continent visit.
Angel Earrings (Dagger)
Synthesize: Magician Shoes + Silk Robe (3,000 gil) · Lindblum/Treno
Teaches Curaga and Life. Dagger's most important healing spells come from accessories and armor — prioritize synth shops whenever you visit a town. Angel Earrings give her full white magic access earlier than equipment drops.
Pumice (Dagger — Ark Summon)
Synthesize: 2× Pumice Piece · Hades (secret boss) unlocks advanced synth
Pumice Pieces are acquired from Ozma (one) and the Friendly Monster chain (one). Synthesize 2 Pumice Pieces at Hades's forge (Disc 3) to get Pumice — Dagger's ultimate eidolon Ark. The Friendly Monster chain: give each monster their required item (Ore, Ether, Tent, etc.) in sequence.
Tin Armor (Steiner — Trick Sparrow)
Synthesize: Hammer + Mythril Armor + Mythril Helm (50,000 gil) · Treno
Tin Armor is required for Steiner's Darkside and certain Sword Art combos. The Hammer is extremely rare — check treasure rooms in Ipsen's Castle. Not worth the gil investment unless you specifically want Darkside.
Thief Gloves (Zidane)
Synthesize: 2× Mythril Gloves (15,000 gil) · Daguerreo (Disc 3)
Teaches Master Thief ability — dramatically increases rare steal rate. Essential for the Ozma and endgame boss steals. Synthesize as soon as you reach Daguerreo. With Master Thief, rare steals become common steals in terms of frequency.
Protect Ring
Synthesize: Dark Matter + Pumice Piece (30,000 gil) · Hades
Teaches Auto-Protect and Protect. Auto-Protect running at all times is a significant defense boost for late Disc 4. Requires Hades to be defeated first (Disc 3).
Ability Learning Priority by Character
Zidane — Priority Abilities
Equipment: Thief Gloves, Running Shoes, Ultima Weapon (endgame)
Master Thief (Thief Gloves) · Flee-Gil (Butterfly Sword) · High Tide (Kaiser Knuckles) · Protect Girls (defensive passive) · Counter (Mage Masher chain) · Thievery (Disc 4 — scales with total steals). Ultima Weapon comes from Hades synthesis: 2× Orihalcon + 2× Pumice.
Vivi — Priority Abilities
Equipment: Black Robe, Mace of Zeus (endgame), Protect Ring
Reflect × 2 doubles reflected magic — stack reflectors on Vivi for 9,999 white magic attacks. MP Attack (Mage Staff) makes physical attacks drain MP from enemies. Auto-Haste early for faster spell cycling. Black Robe (steal from Kuja) teaches Doomsday.
Steiner — Priority Abilities
Equipment: Ultima Sword (Disc 4), Shield Armor, Grand Helm
Sword Art skills (from swords): Iai Strike (instant death), Minus Strike (reduces to 1 HP). Combine with Vivi's magic for Sword Magic abilities — free Flare/Holy/Meteor at Steiner's physical attack speed. This combo is one of the game's most powerful DPS options.
Freya — Priority Abilities
Equipment: Holy Lance, Dragon Mail/Dragon Helm
Dragon Crest (scales with dragons killed — up to 9,999 with 100 kills) · Jump (avoids all ground AoE during boss fights) · Six Dragons (multiple-target jump) · Dragon Breath (HP-scaling damage). Dragon Crest from Holy Lance is her best Disc 4 attack. Holy Lance: available from Hades synthesis or random drops.
Quina — Priority Abilities (Blue Magic)
Equipment: Gastro Fork (endgame fork), Glutton's Robe
Quina's Blue Magic via Eat/Cook command. Key spells: Frog Drop (scales with frogs caught — catch 99 Qu's Marsh frogs for 9,999 damage), Mighty Guard (eat Nymph in Outer Continent), White Wind (eat Zuu near Lindblum), LV5 Death (eat Dracozombie). Gastro Fork from Qu's Marsh endgame frog quest.
Eiko — Priority Abilities
Equipment: Angel Flute (endgame), Ribbon, Barette
Carbuncle, Fenrir, Phoenix (from Phoenix Pinion items) are her most useful eidolons. Holy is her strongest damage spell. Auto-Regen (Fairy Earrings) keeps party sustained. Full-Life (Gold Hairpin) handles emergencies. Eiko's White Magic via equipment — always check synthesis shops for her accessories.
Amarant — Priority Abilities
Equipment: Rune Claws, Ritual Hat, Genji Armor
Counter (automatic counterattack on being hit) · Chakra (restores party HP/MP based on Amarant's level) · Aura (grants Trance mode to another character) · No Mercy (Disc 4 — massive physical damage). Aura is extremely rare — cast it on Zidane or Steiner for instant Trance+Limit Break access.
Dagger — Priority Abilities
Equipment: Whale Whisker (endgame), Madain's Ring, Pumice (Ark)
Ark (from Pumice synthesis) deals 9,999 non-elemental to all enemies — her strongest summon by far. Leviathan and Bahamut for boss damage. Curaga for healing. Focus on equipment that teaches Curaga, Life, Full-Life before combat summons. Note: Dagger suffers from ability restriction in Disc 2 while dealing with Alexandria events — plan around this.
Boss Quick Reference
Ozma
Disc 3: Chocobo's Paradise (optional) · HP: 55,535 · Absorbs: Fire, Ice, Lightning, Holy · Weakness: None
Optional superboss and hardest boss in the game. Ozma is immune to most damage types — use Shadow- and non-elemental attacks only. Doomtrain status effects work (Osmose, Curse, etc.). Complete the Stellazzio coin quest (12 coins to Queen Stella in Treno) for the 13th coin Virgo, which gives a reward that makes the fight survivable. Friendly Monster chain completion reduces Ozma's stats significantly. Grants Pumice Piece — needed for the Pumice synthesis (Ark eidolon for Dagger).
Hades (Secret Boss)
Disc 3: Memoria area · HP: 65,535 · Weakness: None
Hades is a required fight to unlock the advanced synthesis shop (the best in the game). He inflicts all status conditions and uses Abyss (massive non-elemental party damage). Equip Ribbons or auto-status-clear abilities. After defeat he opens a forge shop with the strongest synthesis recipes.
Trance Kuja
Disc 4: Pandemonium · HP: 58,442 · Weakness: None
Uses Flare Star repeatedly — damage scales with party average level, so lower-level parties take less damage. High-level parties (70+) take 3,000–4,500 per Flare Star hit to each character. Bring Elixirs. He also uses Holy and Meteor. Steal Black Robe (rare) from his pre-Trance form.
Necron
Disc 4: Crystal World · HP: 55,535 · Weakness: None
Appears immediately after Trance Kuja with no save point. Grand Cross inflicts random status effects (Petrify, Stop, Zombie, Confuse, etc.) — equip Auto-Regen, Ribbon, or Chemist to mitigate. Neutron Ring reduces all party to near-death. Keep Eiko casting Curaga and Dagger casting Ark. This fight is survivable with careful preparation.
🎭

Discs 1–2 — Across Gaia

Zidane steals a princess. A kingdom burns. A world held together by four crystals slowly comes apart.

1

Alexandria & the Theatre Play

Alexandria · Primo Vista▾
  • The game opens with the Tantalus Theatre Troupe's performance of "I Want to Be Your Canary." Zidane performs — his role in the play is timed. The performance score affects item rewards, but nothing is permanently missed regardless of quality.
  • Alexandria Streets (before boarding): talk to every NPC in Alexandria for items and Tetra Master cards. Key finds: Phoenix Down ×3 from the knight near the castle gate, Potion ×3 from the old woman near the fountain. Buy all Potions and Antidotes from the item shop.
  • Board the Prima Vista (theatre ship). Explore all rooms — there's a card game in the Engine Room. Find the Silk Shirt synthesis material in the cargo hold.
Boss: Baku
  • HP ~619. Tutorial fight. You're supposed to lose — but if you win (difficult at this point), you get a bonus Elixir. Lose gracefully or try hard for the bonus.
Alexandria Castle Escape
  • After the Prima Vista crashes in Evil Forest: Garnet (Princess Dagger) joins. Team splits. Vivi was arrested — rescue him from the castle guard cells.
  • Before leaving Alexandria via the overworld: visit the rooftop area of the Prima Vista wreck — Chest: Phoenix Down. This chest cannot be reached after Evil Forest seals off.
Steal from every boss — starting with Masked Man (Blank) in Alexandria who carries a Mage Masher dagger. These early-game steals give you equipment you won't find in shops for several hours.
2

Evil Forest & Ice Cavern

Evil Forest · Ice Cavern · Dali Village▾
  • Evil Forest: linear story dungeon. Enemies: Plant Spiders (Steal: Eye Drops), Goblin (Steal: Potion). Steal from every type before moving on.
  • Boss: Prison Cage (×2) — the first real boss fights. Steiner joins here. Steal Ether from the second Prison Cage. These bosses use Absorb — heal whoever is grabbed immediately.
  • After Evil Forest: the forest petrifies permanently. Return via airship later for optional area (none available early — just move on).
  • Ice Cavern: first dungeon with a gimmick — Mist knocks party members asleep. Walk carefully — stepping into the Mist stream puts a character to sleep instantly. Boss: Black Waltz 0 (tutorial battle).
  • Chest route in Ice Cavern: Ether (first chest room), Tent (second), Phoenix Down (before the second Mist stream), Elixir (upper path, easy to miss — take the north branch at the upper junction).
  • After Ice Cavern: arrive at Dali Village. Explore thoroughly — there's a windmill puzzle that reveals a hidden underground passage with chests. Buy all synthesis materials from the Dali shop: Iron Helm, Leather Plate (keep these for synthesis later).
Prison Cage: Physical attacks only — magic is absorbed. Attack the vine holding the captive first to free Garnet/Vivi, then focus the cage. Steal Ether from each cage before killing them.
3

Lindblum & the Festival of the Hunt

Lindblum · Festival of the Hunt▾
  • Lindblum is the largest city in the game — explore all three districts thoroughly: Business District, Theatre District, Industrial District. Each has unique shops, synthesis materials, and Tetra Master opponents.
  • Synthesis shop in the Theatre District: synthesize the Silk Shirt and Bronze Gloves from materials collected so far. These are strong early-game armor pieces.
  • Talk to every NPC in all three districts for items and card games. There are 5 Stellazzio coins hidden in Lindblum — check all statues and fountains.
Festival of the Hunt
  • Timed event (12 minutes) — hunt monsters in Lindblum streets for points. Competition between Zidane, Vivi, and Freya.
  • Prize strategy: If Zidane wins: Coral Ring. If Freya wins: Dagger (weapon for Garnet). If Vivi wins: Magic Armlet. The most useful prize is usually Freya winning for the Dagger, or Zidane for the Ring.
  • Boss: Zaghnol (100+ points). Avoid all small enemies and focus on the Zaghnol in the south part of the city for maximum points.
Buy Wrist (bracelet item) and Bone Wrist from Lindblum's shops — these are synthesis components for mid-game armor. Also pick up several Hi-Potions and Ethers here; Lindblum has the best selection before leaving for Burmecia.
4

Burmecia — The Raining City

Qu's Marsh · Gizamaluke's Grotto · Burmecia▾
  • Qu's Marsh: recruit Quina here. Visit the marsh east of Lindblum — Quina is trying to catch frogs. Let the scene play out, and she joins (she's optional but story-important). Start the Frog Catching mini-game — catch 2 frogs minimum for Quina's basic skill, or go for the frog count milestones (9, 15, 23, 30, 45, 99 frogs for rewards including Bistro Fork ultimate weapon at 99).
  • Gizamaluke's Grotto: bell-key puzzle dungeon. Each locked door requires a bell — find them in the caves and from enemies. Steal Holy Bell from Gizamaluke (boss) — it's his rare steal and the only way to get one early.
  • Boss: Gizamaluke — steal the Mitre (hat) and Magician's Robe from him. Use Vivi's magic and Freya's Dragon Crest attack.
Burmecia — Fallen City
  • Burmecia is a rat-person city under attack by Kuja's armies. Navigate through the partially-collapsed buildings — linear but with several hidden chests off the main path.
  • Chests: Hi-Potion (behind first pile of rubble, east alley), Bronze Helm (first courtyard, north side), Mythril Spear (Freya weapon — northeast of the central plaza), Lightning Staff (Vivi weapon — inside the palace south wing), 1000 gil (west palace wing).
  • Boss: Beatrix (first fight). HP ~3,828 before she uses Stock Break. Steal Thunder Gloves from her — this is the ONLY time you can get this item easily. She defeats you after a set HP threshold — this is scripted. Focus on stealing first, then deal damage.
Steal from Beatrix (all 3 fights): Fight 1 = Thunder Gloves. Fight 2 = Ice Brand. Fight 3 = Mythril Sword. These are the only sources of these items. She always defeats you — focus on stealing before the scripted loss triggers.
5

Cleyra's Trunk & Settlement

Cleyra Trunk · Cleyra Settlement▾
  • Cleyra is a rat-person city built in the branches of a giant sandstorm-generating tree. The trunk is the dungeon entrance — a spiral climb with enemies and puzzles.
  • Trunk chests: Potion, Eye Drops, Tent, Ether, Hi-Potion, Phoenix Down — all along the spiral path. Don't miss the side branches (each branch junction has a chest on the non-obvious path).
  • Trunk boss: Antlion. HP ~3,938. Freya's Jump attack deals major damage. Physical attacks bounce off its shell — use magic or Jump. Steal: Needle Fork (Quina weapon) and the Coral Ring.
Cleyra Settlement
  • The settlement has an inn, item shops, and a hidden synthesis shop. Synthesis materials: buy all available. The Orichalcon is sold here — keep it for later synthesis.
  • A ceremony ritual is performed to maintain the sandstorm. Help the priest with the harp — examine the harp in the correct rhythm (follow the NPC's counts).
  • Boss: Beatrix (second fight). Steal Ice Brand sword. Same strategy — steal first, then fight until scripted loss.
  • After Beatrix: Cleyra falls to Kuja's forces. Escape on the airship Red Rose. During the escape: boss — Black Waltz 3 (again, stronger). Steal the Steepled Hat from it.
6

Pinnacle Rocks & the Iifa Tree (Disc 1 End)

Pinnacle Rocks · Alexandria · Iifa Tree▾
  • Pinnacle Rocks: Garnet learns to summon Ramuh here by collecting his story fragments — 5 purple mushroom spirits scattered in the rocky seaside area. Talk to each, then speak to the main Ramuh. Reward: Ramuh Eidolon.
  • Return to Alexandria — the city is under assault by Kuja. Battle on the rooftops with Garnet and Steiner — a gauntlet of soldiers, no save point. Then Marcus escorts them to the boat.
  • Boss: Beatrix (third time). Steal Mythril Sword. Same scripted loss pattern.
Iifa Tree — Disc 1 Finale
  • The Iifa Tree is a giant organism that processes souls. 3-floor descent to the roots. Enemies: Dragonfly (Draw: Float), Stroper (tentacle attacks).
  • Chests: Hi-Potion, Elixir, Ether, Tent. The chest on level 2's east branch is easy to miss.
  • Boss: Soulcage. HP ~18,192. He's undead — Phoenix Down for heavy damage. Also weak to Fire. Steal Gaia Gear from him (Quina armor). He switches between physical and magic defense modes — use Phoenix Down for consistent damage regardless of mode.
  • After Iifa Tree: Disc 1 ends. Kuja and Queen Brahne clash. The Black Mages are revealed to be mass-produced golems. Garnet's eidolons are extracted. Disc 2 begins.
Soulcage: Phoenix Down deals ~3,000 to this undead boss. Stock 20+ Phoenix Downs and spam them — far easier than dealing with his defense mode switching. Steal Gaia Gear first.
7

Disc 2 — Treno & the Card Tournament

Treno · Card Stadium · Synthesis▾
  • Treno is a nocturnal city of aristocrats and thieves. The main activities here:
    — Synthesis Shop: the best mid-game synthesis shop. Craft: N-Kai Armlet, Mythril Gloves, Thunder Gloves (if you missed Beatrix), Fairy Earrings.
    — Auction House: bid on Stellazzio coins and rare items that rotate. Buy all Stellazzio coins you see.
    — Card Stadium: enters Tetra Master tournament. Win for rare cards and items.
  • Queen Stella's house: bring Stellazzio coins found so far for gil rewards and eventually the Hammer item.
  • Tetra Master tournament: optional but the prize (reward after beating several rounds) includes the Mini-Prima Vista card — one of the rarest. Participate if you care about card collection.
  • After the tournament: story events lead to a short sequence inside Garnet's home — then the Moogles send the team to rescue Garnet's mother.
8

Fossil Roo, Conde Petie & Black Mage Village

Fossil Roo · Outer Continent · BMV▾
  • Fossil Roo: underground tunnel connecting the Mist and Outer Continents. Minecart puzzle — bribe the mole-like excavators (Kupo nuts from a nearby Moogle) to dig alternate routes. Bring 5 Kupo nuts total.
  • Chests in Fossil Roo: Hi-Potion, Ether, Tent, Fairy Earrings (east track route — don't miss), Phoenix Down, Chimera Armlet.
  • Conde Petie: dwarf-like mountain village. Buy the items available here — particularly the Mythril Armlet and Mythril Helm if you don't already have them. Quina recruitment (second and final time if she wasn't recruited at Qu's Marsh on Disc 1).
  • Qu's Marsh (Outer Continent): recruit Quina here if she wasn't recruited before. She automatically joins if this is skipped — but the formal recruitment gives better story context.
Black Mage Village
  • The Black Mage Village is a hidden settlement of sentient Black Mage golems. Buy all available weapons and armor from the synthesis shop here — unique items only sold here.
  • Optional ATE (Active Time Events) show the black mages' daily lives — view all of them for story content. They don't affect gameplay but enrich the world.
  • Boss: Hilgigars (near Madain Sari). HP ~13,488. Weak to Ice. Physical attacks work well. Steal: Mythril Fork (Quina weapon), Rubber Suit.
9

Madain Sari & the Iifa Tree Return

Madain Sari · Eiko's Home · Iifa Tree▾
  • Madain Sari is a ruined Summoner village — Eiko's home. She joins the party here permanently. Explore the village: Mog's gift (interact with the Moogle Mog after story events) gives you the Ribbon accessory (nullifies all status effects — one of the best accessories in the game).
  • Eidolon Wall: murals in Madain Sari tell the history of Summoners. Examine all panels for ATEs that flesh out the lore.
  • Eiko's Moogle Letter chain: throughout the game, Moogles carry letters to other Moogles. Follow the letter chain between Mogki, Mogryo, Mois, and other Moogles for an eventual reward (Kupo Nut → premium items from the Moogle that holds the final letter).
Iifa Tree Return
  • Return to the Iifa Tree (same structure as Disc 1, but accessible from the Outer Continent side). New chests in previously unreachable areas: Elixir, Ether, Phoenix Down.
  • Boss: Silver Dragon (random field encounter at the tree base). Weak to Ice. Steal: Mythril Armlet, Dragon Mail. Dragon Mail is the best heavy armor for Steiner at this point.
  • Boss: Scarecrow (inside Iifa deeper level). HP ~20,000. Thunder weakness. Eiko's Fenrir summon deals heavy damage.
🌌

Discs 3–4 — Terra & Beyond

Kuja's plan unfolds. The truth of Zidane's origin surfaces. A second planet merges with Gaia — and beneath it all, an ancient soul waits.

10

Esto Gaza & Oeilvert

Esto Gaza · Oeilvert · Forgotten Continent▾
  • Esto Gaza: remote mountain town on the Forgotten Continent. One of the best mid-game shops in the game — buy all Magnets, Power Belts, and Venetia Shields from the equipment shop. These are rare elsewhere.
  • Mount Gulug: dungeon accessed from Esto Gaza. Fire-themed area with pull-rope puzzles. 5 chests including the Dragon's Claws (Amarant weapon) and Topaz. Boss: Red Dragon (Fire element — use Ice). Steal: Ruby.
  • Kuja's request: he holds hostages and demands the party split into two groups — one goes to Oeilvert (magic-free zone), one stays in Desert Palace.
  • Oeilvert: all magic is sealed inside — physical attacks only. Bring Zidane, Steiner, Amarant, Freya (physical party) with good armor. The dungeon has a hologram room showing the history of Terran civilization. 5 chests: Elixir, Ether ×2, Aquamarine, Strange Potion.
Epitaph boss in Oeilvert: Magic is sealed, so use only physical attacks. Freya's Jump, Steiner's Sword Magic (still works as command even with magic sealed in area), and Zidane's Dyne moves are all effective. Steal Dark Matter from Epitaph.
11

Desert Palace & Hades

Desert Palace · Cleyra Trunk (revisit)▾
  • The Desert Palace is a trap — Kuja's hidden palace under a desert. The team sent here (Garnet, Vivi, Quina, Eiko) navigates the palace while the Oeilvert team finds their objective.
  • Hourglass puzzle: limited time to collect 4 mirror shards before the hourglass runs out. Each shard is in a different room connected by switches. The correct route: north first, then east, then west alcove, then the center shard. If the hourglass empties before all 4 are collected, the sand resets.
  • 9 chests in the palace: Remedy, Hi-Potion, Ether ×2, Elixir, Lapis Lazuli, Rosetta Ring, Shield Armor (best heavy chest armor for Steiner at this point), Feather Boots.
  • Boss: Garland (Kuja's servant / creator). HP ~16,000. Steal: Battle Boots (Zidane), Reflect Ring. He uses Lv5 Death — keep party levels at non-multiples of 5.
  • Hades (optional boss, post-game accessible): found behind the Desert Palace synthesis shop secret door. HP ~55,535. Defeating Hades unlocks the best synthesis shop in the game — exclusive items including Ultima Sword, Robe of Lords, and more. Worth pursuing before the final dungeon.
Hades (optional): HP ~55,535. He randomly casts powerful spells and status effects — equip Ribbons and Auto-Regen. Use Dagger with Bahamut and Ark summons, Steiner's Flare Sword, Zidane's Grand Lethal Dyne. Victory opens the best synthesis shop in the game.
12

Ipsen's Castle & the Four Shrines

Ipsen's Castle · Shrines of Earth/Water/Fire/Wind▾
  • Ipsen's Castle: a dungeon where weapon strength is inverted — the weaker the weapon's attack value, the more damage it deals. Equip your worst weapons. Use Dagger (lowest attack) for maximum physical damage. Boomerang, Mage's Staff, and other low-attack weapons are strongest here.
  • Chests: Ancient Aroma (key item), Elixir ×3, Ether, Hi-Potion. The Ancient Aroma opens the 4 elemental shrine portals.
  • Boss: Taharka. HP ~22,472. Inverted weapon rule applies — weaker weapons hit harder. Physical attacks outperform magic here. Steal: Ice Brand, Gladius.
The Four Shrines
  • Split the party into 4 teams of 2 (all characters are used). Each shrine must be completed simultaneously in-game (you switch between teams). Each shrine is linear with one boss:
  • Earth Shrine: Zidane + 1. Boss: Lich (Wind weakness).
  • Water Shrine: Eiko + 1. Boss: Maliris (Ice weakness).
  • Fire Shrine: Freya + 1. Boss: Tiamat (Ice/Wind weakness).
  • Wind Shrine: Amarant + 1. Boss: Kraken (Thunder weakness).
  • Each shrine boss drops a Dark Matter — save these for Ozma (the optional superboss).
Ipsen's Castle weapon inversion rule: equip your lowest-attack weapons for maximum damage. The Dagger (1 attack), Mage's Staff, and Javelin are often the best choices. Steiner deals most damage with the original Bronze Helm equipped.
13

Terra & the Genome Village

Terra · Bran Bal · Pandemonium▾
  • Terra is a parallel world — Zidane's true home planet. The party arrives via the portals opened at the 4 shrines.
  • Bran Bal: the Genome village. Zidane discovers his true nature as an artificial life form created by Garland. The most emotionally devastating section of the game — Zidane pushes his friends away.
  • After Zidane's breakdown: party members individually come to reassure him. This FFIX version of "You Are Not Alone" is one of the most acclaimed JRPG story moments.
  • Pandemonium: Garland's fortress above Bran Bal. 4-floor dungeon with the game's hardest pre-endgame enemies.
    — Floor 1 enemies: Epitaph (Darkness attacks), Behemoth (strong physical).
    — Floor 2: Dracozombie (undead Dragon — Phoenix Down one-shots).
    — Floor 3: Gargoyle (stone immune to magic), Malboro (status attacks — Ribbons required).
    — 8 chests total: Elixir ×4, Ether ×2, Remedy ×2.
  • Boss: Garland. HP ~32,768. Steal: Robe of Lords, Dark Matter. He casts Flare Star (damage proportional to level — level-reducing items help). Focus Steiner's sword magic and Dagger's Bahamut summon.
  • After Garland: Kuja turns on him and kills him. Kuja leaves for the Crystal World. Terra begins to die. Disc 3 ends.
14

Crystal World & Memoria

Crystal World · Memoria · The Source▾
Excalibur II — if your playtime is under 12 hours, it's in a chest on the final floor of Memoria before the last boss area. It's the strongest sword in the game for Steiner. If over 12 hours, it's inaccessible.
  • Memoria is the final dungeon — a crystalline space built from collective planetary memories. It has 6 major sections and takes 1–2 hours to fully clear.
  • Section 1 (Shores of Memory): basic enemies, 2 chests (Elixir, Protect Ring).
  • Section 2 (Lost Memory): enemies include Mover (give Elixirs for AP) and Behemoth King. 2 chests (Ribbon, Pumice Piece).
  • Section 3 (Chaos Shrine): reflects various locations from earlier in the game. Boss: Maliris (same as Earth shrine). 2 chests (Ultima Sword if Hades was defeated, Elixir).
  • Section 4 (The Void): Boss gauntlet — 3 bosses in sequence (Tiamat, Lich, Kraken — all stronger versions of the 4 shrine bosses). Stock up on Phoenix Downs and Elixirs.
  • Final area: Excalibur II chest (sub-12 hours only), then the save point and the final boss doors.
15

Final Bosses — Trance Kuja & Necron

The Source — Memoria End▾
  • Kuja (normal): HP ~43,000. Flare/Flare Star. Physical focus, heal aggressively.
  • Trance Kuja: HP ~62,000. Uses Flare Star repeatedly — deals damage proportional to average party level. Keep levels uneven (one very high, one very low) to reduce average. Ultima (his AoE) deals ~2,000–3,000 to all. Have Auto-Regen, Ribbons, and Protect equipped. Steal Ether from Trance Kuja. Dagger's Ark summon and Steiner's Shock skill deal 9,999 per use.
  • Necron (true final boss): HP ~55,535. He appears immediately after Trance Kuja — no recovery time. He uses Grand Cross (random status effects on all party members — Ribbons are essential) and Neutron Ring (heavy damage). Blue Shockwave nullifies your current HP to 0 unless you have Auto-Life/Phoenix protection.
Necron: Grand Cross inflicts random statuses — Ribbons on all 4 party members is the answer. Phoenix Summon with Phoenix Pinion items gives auto-revive. Ark and Bahamut Eidolons deal ~9,999 each. Keep HP above 5,000 at all times; his Neutron Ring hits for ~3,000–5,000 per character.
16

Sidequests — Ozma & Other Completables

Chocobo's Air Garden · Ozma · Chocographs▾
Ozma (Superboss)
  • Ozma is a perfectly spherical optional boss found in Chocobo's Air Garden — a floating island accessible only by a Gold Chocobo. HP ~55,535 (same as Necron). He has no elemental weakness and uses Doomsday (strong shadow damage to all), Meteor, and Curaga (heals himself).
  • Prerequisites: Complete all 9 Friendly Monster encounters (they weaken Ozma's defenses). Collect all 9 Chocographs from Hot & Cold. Finish the Chocobo tracking at every lagoon/forest/mountain. Have 6+ Dark Matter items.
  • Strategy: equip Shadow weapons and armor on your party — Ozma's Doomsday heals shadow-aligned characters. Use Pumice Piece (from clearing Chocographs) to teach Dagger the Ark summon. Ark + Doomsday self-healing = the key strategy.
Chocobo Hot & Cold — Full Completion
  • Play at Chocobo's Forest (forest areas), Chocobo's Lagoon (coastal), Chocobo's Air Garden (clouds). Dig up all Chocograph pieces to assemble the full Chocograph map.
  • Following Chocograph clues on the world map unearths buried treasures: Ore ×10, Phoenix Pinion ×10, Dead Pepper ×4 (used to make Choco dig in special spots), Ether ×15, and eventually access to the Air Garden.
  • Each Chocobo upgrade (Mountain > Sea > Sky > Paradise) unlocks new areas of the world map to dig.

Final Fantasy X

HD Remaster · PS2 · PS4 · PC · Switch

A pilgrimage through Spira — blitzball, aeons, and the spiral of death.

📖

Introduction & Game Basics

▼

Final Fantasy X is a linear story-driven RPG. Progress is automatic — there is no world map until the Calm Lands. The Sphere Grid governs all stat growth. Yuna summons aeons who fight independently. No ability to save anywhere — use Save Spheres.

Key Systems: Overdrive gauges fill as characters take/deal damage. Aeon Overdrives charge separately. The Customize system lets you attach abilities to equipment using items from monsters.
Point of No Return: Once you enter Inside Sin, you cannot return to the Calm Lands or any previous area. Complete all Celestial Weapon hunts, Dark Aeons (International), and Monster Arena before entering Sin.
⭐

Aeons Reference

▼
Valefor
Wind · Besaid

Ifrit
Fire · Kilika
Meteor Strike OD
Ixion
Thunder · Djose
Thor's Hammer OD
Shiva
Ice · Macalania

Bahamut
Non-elem · Bevelle
Mega Flare OD
Anima
Dark · Baaj Temple
Oblivion OD (99,999 ×16)
Yojimbo
Non-elem · Calm Lands
Zanmato (instakill, costly)
