Delta Attack OD
Celestial Weapons unlock aeon Overdrives — Yuna must clear the Remiem Temple chocobo race and defeat each aeon there to receive the Magus Sisters aeon.
⚠️

Missables & Time-Sensitive Items

▼
⚠️
Valefor 2nd Overdrive (Energy Blast) — Talk to the girl with the dog in Besaid Village before leaving on the ship. Missable after the S.S. Liki departs.
⚠️
Anima Fayth Spheres (4) — Must collect all 4 hidden fayth spheres in the original temples (Besaid, Kilika, Djose, Macalania) during first visit. Some require Airship revisit but the Besaid and Kilika spheres are easiest to get on first pass.
⚠️
Sun Crest (Tidus' Celestial Weapon) — Found in Zanarkand Ruins after defeating Yunalesca. Do not skip exploring the ruins before leaving. Missable if you never return (though airship access restores this).
⚠️
Blitzball Prizes — Wakka's Overdrives and Slots are tied to tournament wins. Start tournaments early; Attack Reels, Status Reels, Aurochs Reels are tournament prizes across multiple play-throughs.
⚠️
Clasko / Chocobo Ranch — Send Clasko to the Calm Lands during Mushroom Rock Road or Mi'ihen Highroad. If you proceed too far without sending him, the Chocobo Ranch sidequest becomes unavailable.
⚠️
Kimahri Blue Magic (Lancet) — Enemy-exclusive abilities like Aqua Breath (Chimera), White Wind (Dark Flan), Bad Breath (Malboro). Capture opportunities lost once areas are passed without using Lancet.
⚔

Sphere Grid, Aeons, Celestial Weapons & Boss Reference

▾
Sphere Grid — Optimization Guide
In the Expert Sphere Grid (HD/International), all characters start near the center and can move freely. In the Standard Grid, characters follow linear paths. Both grids require the same endgame approach: max stats (255 in all) and route characters through each other's sections for full coverage.
Tidus — Sphere Grid Priority
Path: Speed nodes → Strength nodes → Yuna's White Magic
Max Agility first (Tidus has the highest base speed). Then head through Auron's Strength path. Haste, Hastega, and Slow are Tidus's most important abilities for party utility. Overdrives: Spiral Cut (early) → Slice & Dice → Blitz Ace (endgame). Blitz Ace deals 8 hits — best with Break Damage Limit weapon.
Yuna — Sphere Grid Priority
Path: White Magic → Filler Spheres → Tidus Speed path
Cure/Cura/Curaga in sequence, then Nul-spells and Life/Full-Life. After core healing, branch into Tidus's path for Haste/Hastega access. Holy is her strongest damage spell — equip Magistral Rod (from Blitzball prize) for extra Magic stat. Overdrives: Grand Summon (boosts aeon's Overdrive gauge) is most useful in boss fights.
Auron — Sphere Grid Priority
Path: Strength nodes → HP nodes → Wakka's Attack Reels area
Auron has the highest Strength in the game. Max Strength first (requires 255 Str via Spheres), then HP. Armor Break/Mental Break/Magic Break/Power Break are his defining utility skills. Overdrives: Dragon Fang (Delay Buster) is the most useful — delays enemy turns. Tornado (Banishing Blade) deals party-level-scaled damage.
Wakka — Sphere Grid Priority
Path: Accuracy nodes → Luck nodes (eventually)
Wakka is the only character who can hit aerial and armored enemies with physical attacks by default. Status Reels (Blitzball prize — multiple tournaments) inflicts status effects including Petrify. Attack Reels (Blitzball prize) deals up to 9,999×12. Overdrives come from Blitzball tournament prizes — prioritize playing Blitzball in Luca before leaving.
Lulu — Sphere Grid Priority
Path: Magic nodes → MP nodes → Yuna's path (White Magic)
Max Magic stat for 9,999 Ultima and Flare. Lulu's Doll weapons let her multi-cast (Fury — spinning the right analog stick fills her Overdrive, then she casts a spell repeatedly). Overdrive Fury with Ultima: up to ~16 casts. Requires Break Damage Limit to exceed 9,999.
Kimahri — Sphere Grid Priority
Path: Any — Kimahri has no fixed path on Standard Grid
Best strategy: send Kimahri immediately into Rikku's Sphere Grid path for Steal and Use early, then branch into Auron's Strength path. He's the most versatile character but has the weakest natural stats — compensate by routing him through high-stat paths. Lancet (Enemy Skill equivalent) lets him learn Ronso Rage Blue Magic.
Rikku — Sphere Grid Priority
Path: Agility nodes → Luck nodes → Steal/Use area
Rikku's Use command and Mix Overdrive are the most powerful utility tools in FF10. Mix combinations: Hyper Mighty G (Turbo Ether + Blessed Gem = Auto-Haste/Protect/Shell/Regen/Reflect on all) is the single most powerful setup command in the game. Farm Blessed Gems (drop from Mandragoras in Calm Lands).
Celestial Weapons — Locations & Unlock Conditions
All Celestial Weapons require the Celestial Mirror first: get the Cloudy Mirror from Remiem Temple (race the Chocobo there), then power it up at Macalania Woods spring with Yuna and Tidus in the party. Celestial Weapons deal max damage regardless of defense — essential for Dark Aeons and Penance.
Tidus — Caladbolg
Calm Lands (Chocobo race NPC after unlocking airship)
Race the Chocobo Trainer on the Calm Lands and win (beat her time). The trainer appears near the northwest corner after the first story pass through. Requires Sun Crest (Zanarkand Dome — chest in the final dungeon area, get before leaving permanently) and Sun Sigil (Chocobo race with 0 balloons, 0 birds hit — the hardest minigame in the game, ~1:0.0 time). Ability: Ignores Defense, Break Damage Limit, Breaks HP Limit.
Yuna — Nirvana
Calm Lands — Monster Arena (capture all 10 Calm Lands fiend species)
Capture one of each species found in the Calm Lands (Skoll, Nebiros, Flame Flan, etc.) for the Monster Arena owner. He'll give Nirvana as a reward. Moon Crest: Besaid Beach (hidden chest). Moon Sigil: Remiem Temple — defeat all aeons in the temple challenge (Ifrit, Ixion, Shiva, Bahamut, Yojimbo, Anima, Magus Sisters). Ability: MP→1, Break Damage Limit.
Auron — Masamune
Unlock via Rusty Sword (Mushroom Rock Road, south cliff) → place at Statue of Mi'ihen
After placing the Rusty Sword, the chest appears on a cliff in Mushroom Rock Road. Mars Crest: Mi'ihen Old Road (chest at the end). Mars Sigil: Clear 10 Monster Arena Original Creations (not just capture — actually fight and beat the unlocked creations). Ability: Break Damage Limit, Might (low HP = higher damage).
Wakka — World Champion
Luca — Cafe by the harbor (talk to the bartender after winning enough Blitzball)
Requires winning the Blitzball League championship at least once. Jupiter Crest: Aurochs Locker Room in Luca (always available). Jupiter Sigil: Win Attack Reels, Status Reels, and Auroch Reels in Blitzball prize pools (league prizes, multiple tournaments required — the longest optional grind). Ability: Break Damage Limit, Ignore Defense.
Lulu — Onion Knight
Baaj Temple — sunken ruins underwater (after unlocking airship)
Dive in the lake at Baaj Temple (accessible via airship coordinates). Chest appears on the lake floor. Venus Crest: Farplane (Guadosalam — chest on the side path). Venus Sigil: Dodge 200 lightning bolts consecutively in the Thunder Plains without being hit. The hardest minigame for most players — requires ~20–40 minutes of perfect timing. Ability: Break Damage Limit, Magic Booster (×2 magic damage, ×2 MP cost).
Kimahri — Spirit Lance
Thunder Plains — activate all 3 Qactuar Stones (one north, two south area)
After pressing all 3 Qactuar Stone pillars (they glow when active), stand near the travel agency and pray at the small stone — a chest with Spirit Lance appears. Saturn Crest: Mt. Gagazet (treasure at the base of the climb path). Saturn Sigil: Capture all species in 6 different regions then return to Monster Arena (check with owner). Ability: Break Damage Limit, Piercing.
Rikku — Godhand
Airship password: GODHAND (input in ship's navigation terminal)
Type "GODHAND" (all caps) in the airship's password screen to unlock a chest in Mushroom Rock Road. Mercury Crest: Sanubia Desert west (chest in the sand). Mercury Sigil: Complete the Cactuar Village sidequest (find all 10 Cactuars in the Sanubia Desert, defeat Jumbo Flan after). Ability: Break Damage Limit, Gillionaire (doubles gil from battles).
Aeon Reference & Overdrive Strategies
Ifrit
Obtained: Besaid — given after defeating Valefor · Element: Fire
Overdrive: Hellfire (non-elemental massive damage). Useful in early water/ice areas where fire resistance matters. Ifrit's Strength scales well early. Use at Kilika Temple before Oblitzerator.
Valefor
Obtained: Besaid Village · Secondary Overdrive: Talk to dog in Besaid Village
Energy Blast (primary Overdrive) and Energy Ray (secondary — get from the dog in Besaid). Energy Ray deals more consistent damage. Valefor is the first aeon — her extra Overdrive is permanently missable if you don't revisit Besaid and talk to the dog before leaving the first time.
Yojimbo
Obtained: Calm Lands (Cavern of the Stolen Fayth) — negotiate price · Cost: Lowest offer accepted = 1/2 of his asking price + 1 gil
Pay Yojimbo gil during battle for actions: Daigoro (dog attack, low pay) → Kozuka (thrown blade) → Wakizashi (party hit) → Zanmato (instant kills ANYTHING — bosses, Dark Aeons, Penance). Zanmato rate increases with Compatibility (pay 1 gil repeatedly in non-boss fights) and higher payment. Pay at least 68,500 gil per turn for highest consistent Zanmato chance. Negotiate price: his first offer × 0.5 + 1 = minimum acceptable payment.
Anima
Obtained: Baaj Temple (airship) — requires all 4 Destruction Sphere treasures from Besaid/Kilika/Djose/Macalania Temples
Overdrive: Oblivion (16 hits of non-elemental damage — one of the highest damage Overdrives). Anima is the strongest standard aeon for boss fights. Collecting all Destruction Sphere treasures is mandatory — if you skipped any temple's sphere chest during the story, return before leaving via airship permanently (Kilika and Djose are revisitable; Macalania is not after the ice road collapses).
Magus Sisters
Obtained: Remiem Temple — defeat all aeons there, then collect Flower Scepter (Godhand chest) and Blossom Crown (Macalania — mushroom area behind the butterfly minigame)
Three aeons (Cindy, Sandy, Mindy) fight simultaneously. Only Yuna's Grand Summon Overdrive is available. "Go!" command orders all three to attack. Combine command lets them cooperate for Delta Attack — a powered-up three-hit. Mindy's Passado (multi-hit) is extremely powerful. Magus Sisters Overdrive: Deltascope (all three together).
Boss Quick Reference
Sinspawn Gui
Disc 1: Luca · HP: 6,000 (body) + 800 (heads) · Weakness: None
Auron lands after this boss — keep going. Kill the Glyph Spheres (heads) first to prevent Venom/Sleep attacks. Blitz team holds the line while the main party recovers.
Oblitzerator
Kilika Port · HP: 6,000 · Weakness: Lightning
Use the crane-control machina in the area (examine the control panel) to deal 5,000 damage, then finish with Thunder spells. Wakka's ball can hit aerial sections. Brings the party to early-game limitations — use Potions liberally.
Seymour (All Forms)
Macalania Temple / Guadosalam / Mt. Gagazet / Inside Sin · HP: 6,000–36,000 by form
Seymour Flux (Mt. Gagazet): uses Total Annihilation (party near-death). Keep party at 3,000+ HP. Lance of Atrophy + Full-Life kills undead immediately (use on the Mortibody to prevent Seymour healing). Mortibody heals Seymour every turn it's alive — kill it immediately each form. Seymour Omnis: Fires elemental attacks in rotating order — swap in elemental-resistant characters or use Nul-spells.
Evrae
Bevelle airship approach · HP: 32,000 · Weakness: Ice, Poison
Breath deals ~1,800 party damage. Move the airship back (L1/R1 buttons on the bridge) to keep Evrae out of breath range and let the ship's cannon do work. When Evrae is close: use Tidus's Hastega and Auron's Armor Break. Bio/Poison status works. It charges its Petrify Gaze at regular intervals — sub out petrified characters immediately.
Yunalesca
Zanarkand Dome · HP: 24,000 (form 1) / 48,000 (form 2) / 60,000 (form 3) · Weakness: None
Three-phase fight. Form 3 uses Mega Death (instant death to all non-Zombie characters). Solution: deliberately inflict Zombie status on your whole party before Form 3 — she'll cast Mega Death and it won't affect undead. Use Mega-Phoenix to heal Zombie after the fight. Break Tidus's Limit with Blitz Ace in Form 1&2 to quickly transition phases. Bring Esuna for Confuse/Sleep effects.
Braska's Final Aeon (Jecht)
Inside Sin · HP: 60,000 (form 1) / 112,000 (form 2) · Weakness: None
Form 1: Jecht uses physical attacks — straightforward. Keep Auron's Armor Break up. Form 2 (aeon form): uses Triumphant Grasp (kills one character outright) and Jecht Beam (Petrify + damage). Bring Rikku's Hyper Mighty G mix for Auto-Haste/Protect/Shell on party. Use aeons to absorb the hardest hits — Yuna's Grand Summon with Anima deals massive damage. Have Haste on all characters.
Yu Yevon
Inside Sin (after Braska's Final Aeon) · HP: 9,999 · Weakness: None · Auto-Regen
Anti-climactic final boss that regenerates each turn. Yu Yevon possesses and protects the aeons — defeat all possessed aeons first (they have Auto-Protect). Yu Yevon himself takes damage from every attack regardless. Party has Auto-Life cast on them automatically. Just deal damage — the fight is scripted to end after enough hits.
Penance (International/HD Only)
Airship (after defeating all 8 Dark Aeons) · HP: 12,000,000 (body) + 500,000 (each arm) · Weakness: None
Hardest boss in FF10. Requires Celestial Weapons (all 7), maxed Sphere Grid, all characters at 9,999 HP / 255 in all stats, and Ribbon accessories. Strategy: Overdrive→AP weapons, kill arms after each Penitence attack (arms use Obliteration — 99,999 damage without max stats). Tidus casts Hastega, Auron uses Armor Break, rotate Overdrives constantly. Yojimbo's Zanmato is the alternate strategy.
🌊

The Pilgrimage Begins

Zanarkand → Besaid → Kilika → Luca → Mi'ihen → Djose → Macalania

🏙️

S01 · Dream Zanarkand & Submerged Ruins

▼

The game opens with Tidus narrating before an attack on Zanarkand. After the cutscene, you control Tidus in a ruined city. Follow the path and defeat Sinscales.

Boss — Sin's Fin: HP ~2,000 · No special strategy needed. Attack until it retreats. Introduction to combat.

After the cutscene you're swept to the Submerged Ruins near Spira. Auron appears. Explore the ruins to find Potion ×4, Hi-Potion ×2, Phoenix Down ×2 in the first rooms.

  • Defeat the Sinscales and Sin's Fin (tutorial)
  • Follow the light into the water — cutscene with Auron
  • Collect chests in the ruins before the ladder
  • Auron/Tidus warp to Spira proper
Boss — Klikk: HP 1,500 · Rikku joins mid-fight. No weak points; just attack. Use Rikku's Mix if you want but unnecessary.
🏝️

S02 · Besaid Island

▼
MISSABLE — Valefor 2nd Overdrive: Before leaving Besaid on the S.S. Liki, talk to the girl with the dog near the shop. She gives a Aeon's Soul item. Interact with Valefor in the Chamber of Fayth again to unlock Energy Blast. This is permanently missable after the boat departs.

Explore Besaid Village fully. Talk to all NPCs. Open chests for Seeker's Ring, Potion ×4, Phoenix Down.

  • Enter the Besaid Temple and obtain Valefor (mandatory)
  • Talk to the girl with the dog near the shop — get Aeon's Soul
  • Re-enter Chamber of Fayth → interact with Valefor → Energy Blast unlocked
  • Buy supplies from the shop (Potions, Antidotes)
  • Board the S.S. Liki
Boss — Sinspawn Echuilles: HP 2,000 · Use Valefor's Energy Ray. Lulu's Water magic also effective. Aurochs NPCs help.
🔥

S03 · Kilika Island & Temple

▼

Kilika has been partially destroyed by Sin. Yuna performs the Sending. Then explore Kilika Port and the Kilika Woods.

  • Watch the Sending cutscene — important lore
  • Kilika Woods: defeat Sinspawn Geneaux to get through
  • Collect chests: Ether, Phoenix Down, Antidote ×2
  • Enter Kilika Temple — cloister of trials (push sphere into slot)
  • Yuna obtains Ifrit
Boss — Sinspawn Geneaux: HP 3,210 · Shell form immune to magic. Destroy tentacles first (they use Venom). When Geneaux opens, use Ifrit or fire magic from Lulu.
Sphere Grid tip: After Kilika, you should unlock at least 4–6 nodes for each character. Tidus toward Speed, Lulu toward Black Magic, Auron toward Strength.
⚽

S04 · Luca & Blitzball

▼

Luca is the major hub city. The Blitzball tournament is mandatory story. The Aurochs will almost certainly lose — it's scripted. After the tournament, blitzball becomes a fully optional minigame.

  • Explore all 5 Luca docks — find chests with Mega-Potion, Elixir
  • Talk to Shelinda near the stadium for lore
  • Watch the Blitzball matches (Besaid vs. Luca Goers is scripted loss)
  • Fiend attack on Luca — fight Sinscales/Sinspawn Echuilles with new party
  • Auron joins the party permanently
Boss — Sinspawn Gui: HP 6,000 + Arms 800 each · Arms attack with Venom. Destroy arms first, then focus the head. Overdrive Auron with Dragon Fang. Yuna should Valefor Energy Ray the head.
Blitzball long-term: Wakka's best Overdrives (Attack Reels, Status Reels, Aurochs Reels) come from tournament prizes. Play regularly throughout the game. Recruit Nimrook as goalkeeper early.
🛣️

S05 · Mi'ihen Highroad & Mushroom Rock Road

▼
MISSABLE — Clasko to Calm Lands: On Mushroom Rock Road, Clasko will ask what he should do. Tell him to quit the Crusaders and go to the Calm Lands. This unlocks the Chocobo Ranch sidequest later. If you don't do this here (or at Mi'ihen), the ranch is unavailable.
  • Mi'ihen Old Road: explore for Megalixir, Lv.2 Key Sphere (check all branches)
  • Rin's Travel Agency — buy Mega-Potions, rest
  • Mushroom Rock Road: meet Clasko — tell him to quit the Crusaders
  • Operation Mi'ihen — Crusaders + Machina vs. Sin (scripted failure)
  • Aftermath: many Crusaders dead; continue north
Boss — Sinspawn Gui (second encounter): Similar to Luca. Focus arms, then body. Sin retreats after battle — the Operation fails regardless.
⚡

S06 · Djose Temple & Moonflow

▼

Djose Temple grants Ixion. The Moonflow is a short transit area crossing the Shoopuf to Guadosalam.

  • Djose Temple cloister of trials: push spheres into the pillars to activate lightning platform; step on it to reach the chamber
  • Obtain Ixion (lightning aeon)
  • Moonflow North Bank: Rikku is kidnapped by an Al Bhed machina — fight Extractor
  • Rikku rejoins after rescue — she can now stay permanently
Boss — Extractor: HP 4,000 · Immune to lightning. Use Tidus/Wakka/Auron physical attacks. Sink it with Water (Rikku Mix: Grenade + Water Gem = Aqua Grenade for major damage).
Djose Sphere Grid area: After Ixion, Lulu should have Blizzara. Wakka's Dark Attack unlocked. Consider branching Yuna toward healing spells Cura/Esuna now.
❄️

S07 · Guadosalam · Thunder Plains · Macalania

▼

Seymour proposes to Yuna. You learn of Jecht's history with Spira. Then cross the dangerous Thunder Plains.

  • Guadosalam: enter the Farplane — Tidus sees his mother (cutscene)
  • Seymour proposes to Yuna — do not accept; it's a story choice that doesn't matter
  • Thunder Plains: dodge lightning bolts (hold X to dodge) — collect Protect Ring, Ether, Lv.3 Key Sphere from chests
  • Macalania Woods: solve the path puzzle (crystal branches light up); find Comet, Mega-Potion
  • Macalania Temple: cloister of trials with sliding ice sphere puzzle
  • Yuna obtains Shiva
Boss — Spherimorph: HP 12,000 · Changes elemental weakness each turn (check the color/element it absorbed). Cast opposite element. Seymour helps here.
Boss — Seymour (First): HP 6,000 · Anima joins him. Use Aeons — Valefor/Ifrit. When Anima appears (3,000 HP), summon an Aeon to take the Oblivion damage instead. Dispel Seymour's Shell then attack with Fira.
Thunder Plains 200 bolt dodge: Dodging 200 lightning bolts without being hit rewards Venus Sigil (for Lulu's Celestial Weapon). Not required now, but note the location.
🏜️

Al Bhed Home & Bevelle

Bikanel Island → Home → Bevelle → Via Purifico → Calm Lands

🏜️

S08 · Bikanel Island & Al Bhed Home

▼

After the lake ambush, the party is separated. Tidus, Rikku, and Wakka travel to the Al Bhed Home base through the Bikanel desert.

  • Bikanel Desert: sand worms are dangerous — run from Zu encounters; fight Sandragora for Mega-Phoenix drops
  • Collect Al Bhed Primers — many scattered in Home (if missed earlier, check them here)
  • Al Bhed Home under attack by Guado — fight through multiple waves
  • Rescue imprisoned summoners in Home basement — chests: Mega-Potion ×4, Elixir
  • Home is destroyed by Sin — escape via airship
Boss — Evrae Altana: HP 16,000 · On the airship gangway. Use the airship cannons (move back) when available — massive damage. When Evrae closes in, attack normally. Poison works well.
Al Bhed Primers: 26 total across the game. Completing them allows you to understand Al Bhed dialogue. The in-game shop lets you buy uncollected ones for 1,000 Gil each once on the airship.
⛪

S09 · Bevelle & Via Purifico

▼

Yuna is captured and forced to marry Seymour. The party invades Bevelle to rescue her. Bevelle is the most visually spectacular dungeon of the first half.

  • Via Purifico (underwater, Tidus/Rikku/Wakka path): defeat fiends and find Lv.4 Key Sphere
  • Via Purifico (Yuna path): labyrinth — follow the glyph lights to find the exit
  • Both groups fight separate bosses
  • Seymour Natus confrontation above Bevelle — defeat him
  • Party is tried and sentenced — escape to the Highbridge
Boss — Evrae: HP 32,000 · On the Bevelle bridge gangway. Same cannon/close-range pattern. Has Photon Wings (causes multiple status ailments). Use Esuna or White Wind. Poison is effective again.
Boss — Seymour Natus: HP 36,000 · Absorbs Holy. Use Bahamut's Mega Flare. Seymour's Mortibody restores his HP unless you destroy it first (HP 4,000). Focus Mortibody → then Seymour. Watch for Hellbiter (Zombie status) — use Holy Water.
Bevelle Temple Cloister: Missable chest — Knight Lance (Kimahri's best early weapon) is in the Bevelle cloister. Do not leave without it.
🌿

S10 · Calm Lands & Remiem Temple

▼

The Calm Lands is the game's main open area. Many sidequests branch from here. Do not enter the gorge yet — complete optional content first.

  • Calm Lands: accept Chocobo Training if Clasko was sent here earlier
  • Monster Arena: talk to the arena owner — start capturing fiends with Capture weapons
  • Remiem Temple (southeast via chocobo): race the chocobo to get Magus Sisters later; fight aeons Yuna sent earlier for items
  • Celestial Mirror: acquire at the Calm Lands from a woman on a chocobo (must beat her in a race); needed to power up Celestial Weapons
  • Seymour Flux battle on the Calm Lands path
Boss — Seymour Flux: HP 70,000 · Mortiorchis adds turns. Flux uses Lance of Atrophy (Zombie) and Full-Life (instakills Zombied characters). Bring Holy Waters. Bahamut Mega Flare + Anima if you have it. Dispel then hit hard.
Celestial Weapons (all 7): Each weapon needs the Cloudy Mirror → Celestial Mirror upgrade, then a Crest + Sigil. The Mirror is at the Calm Lands. Crests and Sigils are scattered across the world — see individual character sections.
🏔️

S11 · Mt. Gagazet & Zanarkand Ruins

▼

The Ronso guard Mt. Gagazet. Kimahri faces the Ronso brothers in a mandatory duel. Then the long underwater cave leads to the Zanarkand Ruins.

  • Mt. Gagazet: defeat Biran and Yenke (Kimahri solo fight)
  • Cave path: underwater tunnel — fight Geosgaeno if you want items (hard optional boss)
  • Mountain summit: Seymour Omnis ambush
  • Zanarkand Ruins: scattered chests with Lv.4 Key Sphere ×2, Mega Elixir
  • Dome interior: trigger memory spheres for lore
Boss — Biran & Yenke (Kimahri solo): HP ~6,000 each. Kimahri must solo. Use Lancet on each to steal their abilities — Thrust Kick (Biran), Nova (Yenke). Recover HP with Lancet when low.
Boss — Seymour Omnis: HP 130,000 · Changes element each turn (Mortiorchis dictates element). Cast opposite element or use non-elemental attacks. Ultima deals massive non-elemental damage. Dispel his barriers. Bahamut + Anima recommended.
Sun Crest (Tidus' Celestial): Found in a chest in the Zanarkand Ruins dome. Pick this up now — it's easy to miss.
💀

S12 · Yunalesca & The Truth of the Final Summoning

▼

The hardest story boss. Yunalesca reveals the truth: the Final Summoning kills the summoner. Yuna refuses. Fight.

  • Watch all the memory sphere lore in the dome first
  • Confront Yunalesca — mandatory fight after the dialogue
  • After the battle, collect the Sun Crest from the nearby chest if not yet done
  • Leave via the airship — Cid arrives
Boss — Yunalesca (3 forms): Total HP ~48,000 across phases.
• Phase 1 (HP ~16,000): Standard attacks. Cura spam to recover.
• Phase 2 (HP ~16,000): Uses Hellbind to Zombie one character; uses Mega Death (kills non-Zombie). Keep one character Zombied on purpose — equip Zombie Ward/Proof.
• Phase 3 (HP ~16,000): Adds Full Life (kills Zombie chars) + Regen (heals herself 4,000/turn). Dispel the Regen every turn, then attack hard. Bahamut + Anima demolish her.
Zombie strategy: Equip one character with Zombie-Ward (reduces zombie chance) or deliberately keep one Zombied to survive Mega Death. Heal Zombie with Holy Water. Keeping a Zombie-Proof accessory on Yuna ensures she can keep healing.
✨

The Airship & Inside Sin

Calm Lands sidequests → Inside Sin → Final Bosses

✈️

S13 · Airship & Final Preparations

▼
POINT OF NO RETURN: Entering Inside Sin locks you out of all sidequests. Complete everything below before proceeding.

The airship provides access to all prior locations. Use the Search function to find hidden input coordinates for secret areas.

  • Baaj Temple (airship coordinates X=11–16, Y=57–63): defeat Geosgaeno then collect fayth spheres + Anima
  • Remiem Temple: race chocobos, fight sent aeons, collect Magus Sisters
  • Monster Arena: capture all monsters in all areas (10 of each species) for unlock rewards
  • Celestial Weapons: complete all 7 (Tidus/Yuna/Wakka/Lulu/Rikku/Kimahri/Auron)
  • Blitzball: win all tournament prizes for Wakka's Overdrives
  • Sphere Grid: aim for all characters to have 99,999 HP if targeting post-game
Celestial Weapon quick list:
Tidus — Caladbolg: Calm Lands chocobo race (Sun Crest: Zanarkand; Sun Sigil: Calm Lands bird race)
Yuna — Nirvana: Monster Arena (clear all Calm Lands fiends; Moon Crest: Besaid beach; Moon Sigil: Remiem aeon fights)
Wakka — World Champion: Luca bartender (Attack Reels from tourney; World Champion Sigil: blitzball)
Lulu — Onion Knight: Thunder Plains chest (200 dodge; Venus Sigil: 200 consecutive dodges)
Rikku — Godhand: airship code GODHAND (Mercury Crest: Bikanel; Mercury Sigil: Calm Lands Agency)
Kimahri — Spirit Lance: Thunder Plains (3 lightning towers; Saturn Crest: Gagazet cave; Saturn Sigil: Butterfly hunt)
Auron — Masamune: Mushroom Rock code (Mars Crest: Mi'ihen old road; Mars Sigil: Monster Arena unlock)
🌑

S14 · Inside Sin

▼

Inside Sin is the final dungeon. It has multiple zones: Underwater City, Towers, and the core. No return after entry.

  • Underwater Ruins: navigate platforms — chests have Mega Elixir ×2, Elixir ×4
  • Towers of Light: fight waves of fiends
  • City of Sin (Sin's heart): multiple ambush battles
  • Braska's Final Aeon confrontation
  • Jecht (Final boss phase 1)
  • Yu Yevon (Final boss phase 2)
Boss — Braska's Final Aeon (Jecht): HP 60,000 · Uses Jecht Beam (Petrify), Triumphant Grasp (massive physical), and Overdrive (Ultimate Jecht Shot). Keep HP above 4,000 always. Use Zombie + Curaga trick: don't waste turns healing if you have Auto-Life. Bahamut Mega Flare takes off ~9,999 per turn.
Boss — Yu Yevon: HP low but cycles through 4 aeons. Each aeon is Zombie + attacked by your party. After all 4 aeons fall, attack Yu Yevon himself. He uses Curaga on himself (cast Zombie on Yu Yevon first — Curaga then hurts him). Very straightforward after Jecht.
Auto-Life: Equip all characters with Auto-Life (or cast Reraise) before the Jecht fight. Ultimate Jecht Shot can KO the entire party — Auto-Life immediately revives them.
🏆

S15 · Post-Game & Dark Aeons (HD Remaster)

▼

The HD Remaster includes Dark Aeons and Penance from the International version — the hardest content in the game.

  • Dark Valefor: Besaid Village — blocks return; HP 800,000. One-shots characters. Need 9,999 HP + Auto-Haste/Auto-Protect armor.
  • Dark Ifrit, Dark Ixion, Dark Shiva: on respective roads — similar HP range 800,000–1,200,000
  • Dark Bahamut: Zanarkand Ruins — HP 4,000,000. Mega Flare one-shots party. Need Auto-Life + Quick Hit spam.
  • Dark Anima: Mt. Gagazet — HP 8,000,000. Extremely dangerous Overdrive.
  • Dark Magus Sisters: Remiem Temple — HP 6–8M each. Fight individually.
  • Penance: Final superboss (airship, after all Dark Aeons defeated) — HP 12,000,000 with Arms at 500,000 each. Requires max stats + Break HP Limit (99,999 HP).
Boss — Penance: HP 12,000,000 · Two Arms (500,000 HP each) attack every turn. Destroy Arms immediately — they regenerate and deal catastrophic damage. Penance uses Obliteration (100,000+ to party). Strategy: Quick Hit (non-turn-ending attack), max stats via Sphere Grid overflow. Each character needs 255 in Strength/Magic/Agility and Break Damage Limit.
Max Sphere Grid: Use Don Tonberry trick — have one character solo Don Tonberry (accumulates massive Karma damage), then use Cactuar King for 10,000 Needles → farm Sphere Levels → expand grid. Time investment: 20–40 hours.

Chrono Trigger

DS · PC · SNES · PlayStation

A journey through time to prevent the destruction of the world by Lavos.

📖

Introduction & Game Basics

▼

Chrono Trigger is a non-linear RPG with multiple endings determined by when you fight Lavos. Combat uses Active Time Battle (ATB) with Dual and Triple Techs — party combination attacks. No random encounters in most areas — enemies are visible on the map.

New Game+: After beating the game once, New Game+ lets you fight Lavos immediately and reach alternate endings. Many endings require specific party compositions or actions.
Save points: Save anywhere in most versions. DS and PC versions add dungeons (Lost Sanctum, Dimensional Vortex) with unique gear.
👥

Party Reference

▼
Crono
600 AD · Swordsman
Lightning techs — Luminaire (best AoE)
Marle
600 AD · Princess
Ice + Healing — Arise (full revive all)
Lucca
1000 AD · Inventor
Fire magic — Flare (single huge damage)
Frog
600 AD · Knight
Water techs — Masamune attack bonus
Robo
2300 AD · Robot
Physical + healing beam — best all-around
Ayla
65M BC · Cavewoman
No magic; steal (Charm); strongest physical
Magus
12,000 BC · Warlock
Best magic stats; Dark Matter
Best Dual Techs: Crono + Frog = Blade Toss; Lucca + Robo = Fire Tackle; Marle + Robo = Aura Whirl (party heal). Best Triple Tech: Delta Force (Crono + Marle + Lucca) hits all enemies for ~2,000+.
⚠️

Missables & Side Quests

▼
⚠️
Lucca's Mother (580 AD sidequest) — Optional event to save Lucca's mother. Requires the pendant unlocked from 65M BC. Input code: LARA. Missable if you never return to 580 AD after the relevant story point.
⚠️
Toma's Grave / Rainbow Shell fragment — Toma's spirit in 600 AD tells you where the Rainbow Shell is buried. If you miss talking to Toma's grave with the pop bottle, this sidequest cannot complete (needed for the Sun Stone and Rainbow equipment).
⚠️
Sun Stone (Sunstone quest) — Place the Moon Stone in 65M BC and retrieve it in 1000 AD fully charged. Requires specific actions in both time periods and giving it to Lucca to make the Wonder Shot / Sun Shades. Can be missed if you charge it in the wrong order.
⚠️
Frog's Masamune upgrade — After Magus's castle, take the Masamune to Melchior (1000 AD) to have it reforged. Do this before entering the Ocean Palace — Frog gets a significant stat boost that matters for Azala and Lavos battles.
⚠️
Crono's Resurrection — Optional. Collect the Chrono Trigger (Egg of Time) from Gaspar at the End of Time. Use it at Death Peak after Crono dies at Lavos. If you skip this, Crono is permanently dead for the rest of the run (except NG+).
⚠️
Ayla's Charm (stolen items) — Certain unique items can only be obtained by Charming specific enemies. Key ones: Haste Helm from Yakra XIII, Elixir from Rust Tyranno, Speed Tab from various bosses. Items cannot be obtained otherwise.
⚔️

Equipment Reference — Weapons, Armor & Accessories

▼
Weapons — Best-in-Slot by Character
Crono
BEST: Rainbow Sword
From Rainbow Shell (Melchior, 1000 AD). 240 Atk. The highest-damage sword in the game. Upgrade path: Mop → Bronze Blade → Iron Blade → Steel Sabre → Silver Sword → Thunder Blade → Slasher → Aeon Blade → Rainbow Sword.
Marle
BEST: Valkerye / Stardust Bow
White Bow (Sun Stone quest) is a strong option. Sage Bow and Valkerye are available in endgame shops. Marle's role is primarily healing/support — her bow attack is secondary. Upgrade path: Sling → Iron Bow → Silver Bow → Lode Bow → Sage Bow → Valkerye.
Lucca
BEST: Wondershot
From Sun Stone quest. Deals completely random damage 1–9999 — the average is very high, especially with Magic stat investment. Also consider: Giga Arm (reliable, 165 Atk), Terra Arm (high attack). Upgrade path: Airgun → Pea Shooter → Hammer Arm → Megaton Arm → Plasma Arm → Ruby Arm → Dream Arm → Terra Arm → Giga Arm → Wondershot.
Frog
BEST: Masamune (reforged)
The reforged Masamune (Melchior after Magus's Castle, using the Broken Sword + Broken Hilt) gives Frog ~140 Atk and doubles his Water 2 damage. Frog's ultimate tech (Frog Squash) scales with Frog's HP — keep him healthy for maximum damage. The Masamune is also required to reach full potential.
Robo
BEST: Crisis Arm / Doom Finger
Crisis Arm deals damage proportional to low HP (crisis mode) — extremely powerful late game with careful HP management. Doom Finger has the raw highest attack stat (~185). Upgrade path: Tin Arm → Hammer Arm → Kaiser Arm → Giga Arm → Crisis Arm / Doom Finger. All found in chests or shops in the 600 AD and endgame areas.
Ayla
No weapons — Fists only
Ayla fights bare-handed and cannot equip weapons. Her attack power scales directly with level: at Level 70+, her fists deal ~250 base attack, competitive with best weapons. Prioritize Power Tabs and Speed Tabs on her. Her Charm ability also makes her essential in boss fights for unique steals.
Magus
BEST: Star Scythe / Vedic Scythe
Magus joins with Doom Scythe and can upgrade to Moon Edge, Darkseeker, Star Scythe. The Vedic Scythe is the strongest available (endgame shop, 190 Atk). Magus's real power is his magic — Dark Matter at 99 Magic hits for 9,999 on most targets. Equip Magic-boosting accessories over pure attack.
Armor — Full Catalog
Prism Dress
BEST female armor · Rainbow Shell
145 Defense. Available for Marle and Lucca (and Ayla). Forged from Rainbow Shell/Prism Stone by Melchior in 1000 AD after the Rainbow Shell trial. Also forges Prism Helm. Requires completing the Rainbow Shell sidequest.
Moon Armor
Best male armor · End-game shops
~130 Defense. Available for Crono, Frog, Robo, Magus. Found in endgame shops (Ioka Village, 65M BC after fighting strength) or deep chests. Best balanced armor for male characters without elemental absorption.
Dark Plate
Absorbs Shadow · Magus-specific areas
Absorbs Shadow damage, healing Magus when hit by Dark-element attacks. Magus's Dark Matter is Shadow — pairing this with Ozzie's final room strategy is the standard approach. Found in Magus's Castle chests or the Ocean Palace.
Red Plate
Absorbs Fire · Slash (Charm)
Absorbs Fire damage, healing the wearer when hit by fire attacks. Charm from Slash in Magus's Castle — the only source in the game. Invaluable against Retinite (fire wave) and some Black Omen enemies. One of the most valuable Charm targets in the game.
White Plate
Absorbs Lightning · Nizbel area
Absorbs Lightning damage. Found in 65M BC chests. Excellent if fighting Nizbel variants or Thunder Slash-users. Combine with Lightning techs to self-heal during specific fights.
Blue Plate
Absorbs Ice/Water
Absorbs Water/Ice damage. Found in chests in 12,000 BC area. Useful against Ocean Palace bosses and ice-using Zeal enemies. Equip on whoever is taking the most elemental hits.
Taban's Suit / Vest / Helm
Lucca only · Taban gives them
Three Lucca-exclusive pieces made by her father. Taban's Vest (fire immunity), Taban's Helm (fire/shadow resist), and Taban's Suit (strongest Lucca armor in non-Rainbow versions). Given automatically at story moments when Taban appears. Cannot be purchased or found in chests.
Zodiac Cape
High magic defense · End-game
~85 Defense, ~50 Magic Defense. Provides multi-elemental resistance. Good choice for whoever is absorbing the most magic in your party, particularly for Magus or Marle support builds. Found in Black Omen or late-game shops.
Helmets
Haste Helm
CRITICAL · Robo's 400-year forest
Auto-Haste at battle start — the most powerful single piece of headgear in the game. Given by Robo after he spends 400 years planting Fiona's Forest (S12). Cannot be bought or found elsewhere. Equip on whoever needs the fastest ATB gauge — typically your healer (Marle) or your main attacker (Crono).
Prism Helm
BEST helmet · Rainbow Shell
120 Defense. Forged alongside Prism Dress from Rainbow Shell by Melchior. Resists all status effects. Equip on a character not wearing the Haste Helm — Prism Helm + Moon Armor is the standard male endgame setup.
Dark Helm
Absorbs Shadow · Magus areas
Absorbs Shadow attacks. Pair with Dark Plate on Magus for near-invulnerability against shadow-element boss attacks in the Black Omen. Found in Ocean Palace or Magus's Castle chests.
Accessories — Key Items
Speed Tab
Permanent +1 Speed · Many sources
The most impactful permanent stat boost. Each Speed Tab permanently increases one character's Speed by 1. Sources: Charm from various bosses, found in chests throughout time eras. Priority: put Speed Tabs on Crono and Marle first — fast healer and fast attacker wins battles.
Power Tab
Permanent +1 Strength
Increases Strength permanently. Useful on Crono, Ayla, and Frog — your main physical attackers. Sources include chests in Guardia Forest, 600 AD areas, and Charm from certain enemies.
Magic Tab
Permanent +1 Magic
Increases Magic permanently. Priority targets: Magus (his Dark Matter scales with Magic — at 99 Magic it hits for 9,999), then Lucca (Wondershot's average scales with Magic), then Marle (heal power scales). Magic Tabs are rarer than Speed/Power Tabs.
Bandana
Speed +3 · Millennial Fair
Purchased with Silver Points at the Millennial Fair (S01). 40 Silver Points. The Speed bonus is immediate and permanent while equipped. One of the best early-game accessories — buy for Crono or Marle first.
Powerglove
Attack +5 · Millennial Fair
Purchased with Silver Points at the Millennial Fair. 40 Silver Points. Raw attack boost — equip on Crono or Ayla early. Good early game; replaced by better accessories after 65M BC unlocks.
Wall Ring
Auto Barrier/MBarrier
Equipping this ring gives the character auto-Barrier (halve physical damage) and MBarrier (halve magic damage) at the start of each fight. Extremely strong defensively — equip on your squishiest character (usually Lucca or Marle) during hard boss fights.
Frenzy Band
Auto-counter
Character automatically counter-attacks after being hit. Combined with Ayla's high Strength (no weapon needed, auto-counter deals bare-fist damage), this accessory turns Ayla into a damage powerhouse who counter-attacks every hit she takes.
Amulet
Status immunity
Provides resistance to Poison, Blind, and Confusion. Equip on your healer (Marle) to prevent her from being status-locked during boss fights when you need consistent healing.
Sun Shades
Lucca only · Sun Stone quest
Lucca-exclusive accessory crafted from the Sun Stone alongside the Wondershot. Gives +5 Magic. Combined with the Wondershot and maximum Magic Tabs on Lucca, her average damage output becomes devastating for boss fights.
Gold Earring / Silver Earring
Magic boosts · various shops
Silver Earring: +3 Magic. Gold Earring: +5 Magic. Equip these on Magus and Lucca as a priority. Magic-boosting accessories stack with base Magic stat and Magic Tabs — important for maximizing Magus's Dark Matter damage cap.
Charm Priority List: The most valuable items Ayla can Charm from enemies — Red Plate from Slash (Magus's Castle), Haste Helm from Yakra XIII (1000 AD Chancellor fight), Elixir from Rust Tyranno (Giant's Claw), Speed Tab from various Black Omen enemies. These cannot be obtained any other way.
✨

Tech Database — All Single, Dual & Triple Techs

▼

Techs are learned by accumulating Tech Points (TP) through battles. Single techs require one character; Dual Techs require two specific characters in the same party; Triple Techs require three specific characters. Higher-tier techs have more powerful effects.

Crono — Sword / Lightning
Cyclone
0 TP · Physical AoE
Crono spins his sword, hitting all enemies in range. Good early AoE before Wind Slash. Elemental: non-elemental physical.
Wind Slash
~10 TP · Line attack
Slashes across all enemies in a line. Wind element. Moderate damage, great for groups. Replaced by Lightning for single targets but Wind Slash stays useful for trash.
Lightning
~30 TP · Single target
Lightning-element magic attack on one target. Pairs with Marle's Ice for the Ice Sword dual tech. Nizbel is weak to Lightning — spam this for the defense-drop effect.
Luminaire
~80 TP · Full party AoE
Crono's ultimate — a massive sphere of lightning strikes all enemies. Non-elemental magic damage. The most powerful single AoE tech in the game. Essential for the Lavos fight and Black Omen trash clearing.
Marle — Ice / Support
Aura
0 TP · Heal one ally
Heals one character for moderate HP. Marle's primary healing tool early game. Scales with Magic stat.
Provoke
~10 TP · Status
Confuses an enemy into attacking itself or allies. Situationally useful for redirecting dangerous attacks. Not reliable against bosses.
Ice
~30 TP · Single ice attack
Ice-element magic on one enemy. Combines with Lucca's Fire for Antipode (shadow damage). Use against fire-element enemies (Heckran cave trash).
Ice 2
~50 TP · Multi-target ice
Hits multiple enemies with ice. Required for certain dual tech combinations. More efficient than Ice for groups.
Life
~60 TP · Revive
Revives one KO'd ally with low HP. Required tech — Marle is your primary resurrector.
Haste
~70 TP · Speed up ally
Dramatically speeds up one character's ATB gauge fill rate. Cast on Crono or Frog first — your main damage dealer going faster multiplies total DPS significantly.
Cure 2
~80 TP · Heal all allies
Heals the entire party. The most important support tech in the game. Use this after boss AoE attacks to restore everyone. Required for the Aura Whirl dual tech with Robo.
Life 2
~100 TP · Full revive
Revives one ally to full HP. Extremely powerful — brings back a fallen ally at maximum health. Expensive in TP to unlock but worth it for the endgame.
Lucca — Fire / Support
Fire
0 TP · Single fire
Basic fire magic. Heckran's weakness is Fire — spam this in Heckran Cave whenever he opens his chest plates. Combines with Marle's Ice for Antipode.
Napalm
~10 TP · AoE fire bomb
Drops a fire bomb on enemies in an area. Good early AoE damage. Fire element.
Protect
~30 TP · Defense buff
Halves physical damage taken by one ally. Cast on your frontline physical attacker (Crono or Frog) before hard bosses. Stacks with Wall Ring's Barrier effect? No — but Protect is free and powerful.
Fire 2
~50 TP · Stronger fire
Upgraded fire magic, stronger than Fire. Required for Antipode 2 and Antipode 3 dual tech combinations with Marle.
Hypnowave
~70 TP · Sleep AoE
Attempts to put all enemies to sleep. Very useful against trash encounters to skip fights entirely. Less effective against bosses.
Flare
~90 TP · Non-elemental magic
Lucca's ultimate — massive non-elemental magic damage to one target. Very powerful against enemies with fire immunity. Used in Frog Flare dual tech for massive single-target burst.
Frog — Water / Heal
Slurp
0 TP · Heal one
Heals one ally. Frog's minor healing — Slurp Cut is usually better for dealing damage while healing.
Slurp Cut
~10 TP · Slash + heal
Attacks one enemy AND heals Frog. Highly efficient — costs no MP to heal while dealing damage. Use every turn against moderate enemies.
Water
~30 TP · Single water
Water-element magic attack. Effective against fire enemies. Combines with Crono for dual techs.
Cure 2
~50 TP · Heal all
Heals the entire party. Frog becomes a secondary healer with this tech — very useful when Marle isn't in your party.
Water 2
~70 TP · Multi water
Hits multiple enemies with water. Required for the Frog Flare dual tech with Lucca. Strong against fire enemies.
Leap Slash
~80 TP · Jump attack
Frog leaps up and crashes down for high physical damage. Non-elemental.
Frog Squash
~100 TP · ULTIMATE
Frog's ultimate: summons a massive frog that crushes enemies. Damage scales with Frog's current HP — at high HP it deals devastating damage. Keep Frog healthy to maximize output. One of the most powerful single-character techs in the game.
Robo — Physical / Support
Laser Spin
0 TP · AoE laser
Robo spins and fires lasers hitting all enemies. Non-elemental magic damage. Good early AoE.
Robo Tackle
~10 TP · Single physical
Strong single-target tackle. Physical damage — ignores magic defense. Good against magic-resistant enemies.
Heal Beam
~30 TP · Heal all
Restores HP to all allies. Robo's most important support tech — lets him substitute for Marle as a party healer. Scales with Robo's Magic stat but is effective even without heavy Magic investment.
Area Bomb
~50 TP · AoE bomb
Drops a bomb on a group of enemies. Non-elemental damage.
Uzzi Punch
~80 TP · Multi-hit physical
Robo fires a series of rapid punches at one target. Physical damage, hits multiple times. Strong against high-magic-defense, low-physical-defense enemies.
Shock
~90 TP · Lightning AoE
Robo releases a massive electrical discharge hitting all enemies. Lightning element. Synergizes with Crono's Lightning for combined lightning-focused parties.
Rapid-fire Fist
~100 TP · ULTIMATE
Robo's ultimate — fires a rapid succession of extremely fast punches at one target for very high total physical damage. Effective against bosses with low physical defense.
Ayla — Physical / Charm
Kiss
0 TP · Heal + status cure
Heals one ally and cures status effects. Ayla's only healing tech. Status cure is the main draw — cures Poison, Confusion, Blind on one ally.
Rollo Kick
~10 TP · Line kick
Physical kick hitting enemies in a line. Non-elemental. Good early AoE physical damage.
Charm
~30 TP · Steal enemy item
The most important tech in the game for completionists. Charms (steals) a random item from an enemy — many unique items can ONLY be obtained this way. Does not deal damage. See Charm Priority List in Equipment section.
Tail Spin
~50 TP · AoE physical
Ayla spins with her tail, hitting all enemies. Non-elemental physical damage. Good crowd-clearing tool.
Triple Kick
~80 TP · 3-hit physical
Three kicks at one target — physical hits, non-elemental. Ayla's best single-target physical attack until Dino Tail. Good against bosses with strong magic defense.
Dino Tail
~100 TP · ULTIMATE
Ayla's ultimate — damage scales inversely with enemy HP (higher damage when enemy is at low HP). At very low enemy HP this deals maximum damage. Combine with other characters weakening a boss, then finish with Dino Tail for massive damage. Also classified as non-elemental physical.
Magus — Shadow / Magic
Lightning 2
Joins with this
Multi-target lightning magic. Available immediately when Magus joins. Good for clearing groups early in the Black Omen.
Fire 2
Joins with this
Fire magic. Available from joining.
Ice 2
Joins with this
Ice magic. Available from joining.
Dark Bomb
Early TP
Shadow-element bomb hitting one target. Magus's primary single-target shadow attack early.
Dark Mist
Mid TP
Shadow-element AoE attack. Hits multiple enemies. Good for clearing Black Omen trash encounters.
Dark Matter
~90 TP · ULTIMATE
Magus's ultimate — the most powerful single-target spell in the game. At 99 Magic stat it deals 9,999 damage. Non-elemental shadow magic. Use Magic Tabs and Gold Earrings to push Magus to 99 Magic for maximum Dark Matter output.
Key Dual Techs
Fire Sword / Fire Sword 2
Crono + Lucca
Crono's sword is enchanted with fire. Hits one target for fire-physical hybrid damage. Requires Crono's Lightning + Lucca's Fire (tier 1) or Lightning + Fire 2 (tier 2). Effective against ice-element enemies.
Ice Sword / Ice Sword 2
Crono + Marle
Crono's sword enchanted with ice. Hits one target for ice-physical hybrid. Requires Crono's Lightning + Marle's Ice (or Ice 2 for tier 2). Effective against fire-element enemies — particularly Magus-phase enemies.
Antipode 1 / 2 / 3
Marle + Lucca
The collision of Fire and Ice produces shadow damage — effective against neutral enemies. Tier 3 is one of the highest-damage dual techs. Requires Marle's Ice series + Lucca's Fire series at matching tiers. Antipode 3 hits the entire enemy party.
Aura Whirl
Marle + Robo
Combines Aura and Robo's Laser Spin to heal the entire party. Marle's healing tech + Robo's AoE = party-wide restoration. Useful when you need both healing and offensive pressure simultaneously.
Frog Flare
Lucca + Frog
Combines Lucca's Flare and Frog's Water 2 for massive single-target non-elemental damage. One of the highest-damage dual techs in the game. Use against single high-HP targets (Black Omen bosses).
Spin Cut
Crono + Frog
Physical spinning attack from both characters. High physical damage on one target. Requires Crono's Cyclone + Frog's Slurp Cut.
Gatling Kick
Ayla + Frog
Ayla and Frog kick a single target in rapid succession. Physical damage, very high hit count. Requires Ayla's Triple Kick + Frog's Leap Slash.
Twin Charm
Marle + Ayla
Both characters attempt to Charm the same enemy simultaneously, increasing steal success rate. Required Marle's Provoke + Ayla's Charm. Useful against tough enemies where a single Charm keeps failing.
Triple Techs
Delta Force
Crono + Marle + Lucca
The "standard" triple tech — a massive non-elemental magic explosion hitting all enemies. Requires Crono's Lightning + Marle's Ice 2 + Lucca's Fire 2. One of the highest-damage techs in the game for clearing groups. The go-to endgame AoE for trash clearing in the Black Omen.
3D Attack
Crono + Frog + Robo
The three characters converge for a triple physical attack on one target. Requires Cyclone + Leap Slash + Robo Tackle. Massive physical damage — use against high-magic-defense single bosses.
Final Kick
Crono + Marle + Ayla
Triple physical assault. Requires Crono's Cyclone + Marle's Aura + Ayla's Tail Spin. High physical damage on one target.
Dark Eternal
Magus + Marle + Lucca
Magus's only triple tech — combines his shadow magic with Marle and Lucca's elemental magic for massive shadow damage on all enemies. Requires Dark Matter + Ice 2 + Fire 2. Niche but devastating against shadow-neutral enemies that don't absorb it.
Lifeline
Marle + Robo + Frog
A healing triple tech — restores the entire party to full HP. Requires Marle's Cure 2 + Robo's Heal Beam + Frog's Cure 2. The most powerful healing combination in the game. Use before the Lavos Core phase when your party is depleted.
💀

Boss Quick Reference — HP, Weakness & Charm Targets

▼

All major boss HP values and weaknesses. Charm column = items stealable by Ayla's Charm tech (cannot be obtained any other way unless noted).

Yakra · S01
HP: ~920 · No weakness
First boss. Physical attacks + Lucca's Fire. Can shuffle around to hide the real Yakra — target the correct one. Charm: Magic Ring (useful early accessory).
Dragon Tank · S02
HP: ~300/600/900 (parts)
Three parts: Head (heals tank — destroy first), Right Wheel (attacks), Body (main HP). Use Cyclone/Wind Slash on the Head, then single-target the Wheel. Charm: nothing notable.
Heckran · S02
HP: ~2,100 · Weak: Fire
In Heckran Cave. He blocks physical attacks and opens his chest to absorb magic when defending. Wait for the "try your magic" taunt — only attack during this window with Lucca's Fire. Charm: nothing. Buy Potion+ from cave shop before entering.
Zombor · S03
HP: 880 each half
On the Zenan Bridge in 600 AD. Two halves: Top (Shadow weakness) and Bottom (Water weakness). Use Marle's Ice on Bottom, Magus-era shadow spell or Dark Bomb on Top. Charm: nothing useful.
Masa & Mune · S04
HP: ~1,200 / ~3,200 merged
Denadoro Mountains. Two phases — fight each separately, then fight their merged form. Wind element attacks. Crono's Wind Slash is reflected — use Lightning. Charm from Masa: nothing useful.
Nizbel · S05
HP: ~4,500 · Weak: Lightning
65M BC. Each Lightning hit temporarily reduces Nizbel's physical defense — follow with Crono physical attacks immediately. Repeat the cycle. Charm: Power Tab (very useful — get it!).
Azala + Black Tyranno · S06
HP: 3,500 / 7,000
Fight Azala first (she's a mage — Thunder attacks). When Black Tyranno is exposed, he uses Dino Tail which deals massive damage. Charm Elixir from Black Tyranno. Use Ice 2 (Marle) against the Tyranno. Azala: Charm Speed Tab.
Slash · Magus's Castle
HP: ~5,600 · No weakness
Magus's general. Physical powerhouse — high attack, fast. Charm: Red Plate (the only source of the Red Plate in the game — absorbs fire damage). This is the most valuable Charm in the game. Do NOT skip this.
Flea · Magus's Castle
HP: ~4,120 · No weakness
Magus's general. Spellcaster — uses magic attacks, Haste. Physical hits work well here. Don't let Flea build up repeated magic combo attacks. Charm: Magic Ring (good early accessory).
Magus · Magus's Castle
HP: ~6,666 · Rotating
The difficult fight. Magus cycles through elemental absorption phases (Fire → Ice → Lightning → Shadow). Attack only during the Shadow phase (Dark Bomb works) or use non-elemental attacks any time. Frog's techs deal bonus damage here due to the Masamune connection. Charm: nothing useful.
Golem · 600 AD
HP: ~7,000 · Copies
Golem copies your attack element and becomes immune to it. Use opposite elements each round. Eventually Golem runs out of counters — when it calls for "mama," it retreats. Charm: nothing. Don't panic-spam the same spell.
Yakra XIII · 1000 AD
HP: ~10,000 · No weakness
A Yakra descendant impersonating the Chancellor. Charm: Haste Helm — the ONLY source of the Haste Helm in the game. Ayla MUST be in your party. Use Charm on the first turn before doing any damage. Physical party with Luminaire cleanup.
Dalton Plus · 1000 AD
HP: ~10,000
Dalton evolved. Uses Golem Summon attack to swap the party. Has a Golem as a shield — destroy the Golem first, then attack Dalton. Charm: Aeon Blade (Crono weapon upgrade). Worth charming if your Crono isn't already at Rainbow Sword tier.
Rust Tyranno · Giant's Claw
HP: ~12,000 · Weak: Ice
600 AD optional. Marle's Ice 2, Ayla's Triple Kick. Charm: Elixir (fully restores HP/MP — stock up for the endgame). Uses Zap for ~400 to all — keep HP above 500.
Lavos Spawn × 3 · Death Peak
HP: ~2,000 shell each
Attack the shell only — the head is invincible and will counterattack if hit. Lightning attacks hit the shell for good damage. Three separate Spawns on the path up Death Peak.
Son of Sun · Black Omen
HP: ~— · Fire absorb main
Surrounded by 5 flame extensions. Only one is the "real" flame that doesn't heal Son of Sun. Attack randomly to identify — if the Son heals, that flame was wrong. Cycle through. Use Ice once the pattern is identified.
Queen Zeal · Black Omen
HP: ~30,000 · No weakness
The Black Omen's final boss before Lavos. Uses powerful magic attacks including Hallation (absorbs HP). Delta Force, Frog Flare, and Luminaire spam are the strategies. Keep HP above 400 at all times — her attacks hit hard. Charm: nothing unique.
Lavos Shell · Final
HP: ~30,000 total
Two side bits + center bit. Attacking center without destroying sides = game over instantly. Destroy LEFT side, then RIGHT side, then attack CENTER. Aim at the RIGHT BIT first (it casts Dreamless — healing Lavos). Left bit summons monsters. Center is the vulnerable core once both sides are destroyed.
Lavos Core · Final
HP: ~30,000 total
Three parts: Body (center) + Left Bit + Right Bit. The Left Bit heals Lavos — destroy it immediately. Right Bit casts powerful spells. Attack order: Left Bit → Right Bit → Body. Delta Force, Luminaire, and Dark Matter spam. Keep Marle casting Cure 2 every round.
Most Important Charm Targets: (1) Red Plate from Slash — Magus's Castle, only source; (2) Haste Helm from Yakra XIII — only source; (3) Elixir from Rust Tyranno — best consumable; (4) Power Tab from Nizbel — permanent stat boost; (5) Speed Tab from Masa (first fight). These are irreversible misses.
⏳

1000 AD — The Present

Guardia Castle · Millennial Fair · Truce

🎪

S01 · Millennial Fair & Guardia Dungeon

▼

The game opens at the Millennial Fair (1000 AD). Crono meets Marle — her pendant activates Lucca's teleporter and sends her back to 600 AD.

  • Explore the Fair: win Silver Points for accessories (Power Glove, Bandana, etc.)
  • Talk to Lucca at her booth — meet Marle; demonstration goes wrong
  • Follow Marle through the Gate to 600 AD (Truce Canyon)
  • Find Marle in Guardia Castle dungeon (she was mistaken for Queen Leene)
  • Defeat Yakra — first boss; rescue Marle
  • Return to 1000 AD through the Gate
Boss — Yakra: HP 920 · Uses Needle Spin (group poison). The real Chancellor is hidden among 7 boxes — check each box; the one that fights back is Yakra. Attack physically with Crono, heal with Marle.
Silver Points: At the Millennial Fair, play the soda minigame and Lucca's shooting range to earn points. Buy Power Glove for Crono early.
⚖️

S02 · Crono's Trial & Prison Break

▼

Back in 1000 AD, Crono is arrested for "kidnapping" Marle (Princess Nadia). The trial outcome depends on your earlier choices at the Fair.

  • Trial in Guardia Castle: earlier choices (returning Marle's pendant, helping the old woman, etc.) affect the verdict
  • Regardless of verdict, Lucca rescues Crono from prison
  • Escape the castle — fight guards, find the Gate in the castle sewers
  • Gate leads to 2300 AD (the ruined future)
Trial choices that help your verdict: Return the pendant at the Fair, stop the man harassing the girl near the Market, help the old woman, refuse Marle's pendant when offered. More positive choices = lighter sentence (doesn't affect story but changes dialogue).
🔥

2300 AD — The Ruined Future

Arris Dome · Lab 16 · Sewer Access · Death Peak

🌆

S03 · 2300 AD — The Ruined Future

▼

The future is devastated — Lavos struck in 1999 AD. Most of humanity lives in domes scavenging for food.

  • Arris Dome: defeat the Guardian (forced fight) to access food stores
  • Find the video recording of Lavos's rise — key lore moment; get the Seed and the Gate Key
  • Lab 16 ruins: navigate to Trann Dome (west of Arris)
  • Sewer Access: navigate the Sewer Access dungeon to reach the Proto Dome
  • Proto Dome: find the ruined robot — Robo joins the party here
  • Factory: Robo's old companions attack him — fight them to save Robo
  • Repair the Gate in the Factory to return to 1000 AD
Boss — Guardian (+ Bits): HP 2,400 (Guardian) + 600 (each Bit). Destroy the Bits first — they use Cure Beam to heal the Guardian. After Bits are gone, Lightning + Fire attacks on the Guardian.
Boss — R-Series (Robo's brothers): HP 880 each × 6. They come in pairs. Lucca's Fire attacks are very effective. Crono's Slash + Marle's Cure to manage HP.
⚔️

600 AD — The Middle Ages

Zenan Bridge · Tata and the Frog · Magus's Castle · Denadoro Mountains

🏰

S04 · 600 AD — Zenan Bridge & Frog's Quest

▼

600 AD is war-torn — Guardia is at war with Magus's army. Frog (Glenn) seeks the Masamune to defeat Magus.

  • Zenan Bridge: fight Zombor (guardian of the bridge)
  • Retrieve the broken Masamune from Tata in Porre — he's a fake hero
  • Denadoro Mountains: find the two Masamune pieces (hilt + blade)
  • Bring the pieces to Melchior in 1000 AD to have the sword reforged
  • Return to 600 AD with the repaired Masamune — Frog joins permanently
  • Enter Magus's Castle from the north
Boss — Zombor: HP 1,100 (top) + 900 (bottom) · Fire on bottom half, Ice on top half. Use both — Crono's Lightning also works on both. Marle's Ice 2 is key.
Boss — Masa & Mune (Masamune spirits): HP 1,200 / Fused: 3,100 · They merge into Masamune. Use Lightning + physical. Frog's Water techs once he joins.
Frog's Masamune upgrade: After getting the Masamune, before Magus's Castle, bring it to Melchior in 1000 AD (his hut near Guardia). Frog gets +5 to all stats from the reforged sword.
🗡️

S05 · Magus's Castle

▼

Magus's Castle is the most elaborate dungeon in 600 AD. Six mini-bosses guard the path to Magus.

  • Enter from the north of 600 AD map
  • Four mini-bosses in sequence: Flea (magic user), Slash (swordsman), Ozzie (avoid his traps)
  • Flea's room — fight Flea Plus first, then Flea himself
  • Slash's room — hit him with Frog's Slurp Slash
  • Ozzie's traps — step on the glowing tile to defeat each Ozzie formation
  • Magus's chamber — the climactic fight; a Gate opens and sends party to 65M BC
Boss — Flea: HP 4,120 · Uses powerful magic. Frog's Water techs. Don't use magic when he reflects — watch for the Barrier color change.
Boss — Slash: HP 3,200 · Fast physical attacker. Frog's Slurp Slash + Crono's Lightning hits hard. Keep HP above 200 — Slash's Slurp can 1-hit a character.
Boss — Magus: HP 6,666 · Changes barrier mid-fight (Fire → Ice → Lightning → Dark). Attack with the opposite element. After his barrier drops, use Crono's Lightning 2 / Frog's Frog Squash for high damage. Dark Matter is his most dangerous attack (party ~600 damage).
🦕

65,000,000 BC — Prehistory

Ioka Village · Laruba · Tyranno Lair · Sun Keep

🦕

S06 · 65,000,000 BC — Ayla & the Reptites

▼

The Gate from Magus's Castle throws the party to prehistoric 65M BC. Ayla joins here. The Gate Key was stolen by Kino — Ayla retrieves it. Then into the Reptite Lair and Tyranno Lair.

  • Ioka Village: talk to Ayla — she knows where the Gate Key is (Kino has it)
  • Forest Maze: find Kino; he returns the Gate Key
  • Laruba Village: Reptites attacked and burned it
  • Reptite Lair: rescue Kino from the Reptites
  • Tyranno Lair: final prehistoric dungeon — two floors, many Reptite enemies
  • Azala and Black Tyranno final boss; Lavos falls in aftermath (cutscene)
Boss — Nizbel II: HP 4,096 · Absorbs electricity; use Water or Fire. Ayla's Charm can steal a Speed Tab. After taking damage, discharges lightning — heal immediately.
Boss — Azala & Black Tyranno: HP 3,500 (Azala) + 20,000 (Tyranno) · Destroy Azala first (she heals Tyranno). Azala is weak to Lightning; Tyranno is weak to Ice. Crono + Marle: Aura Whirl to heal; Lucca's Fire 2 + Frog's Ice 2 on alternate turns.
Sun Keep & Moon Stone: In 65M BC, place the Moon Stone in the Sun Keep (cave northwest of map). It needs millions of years to charge. Pick it up in 1000 AD fully charged for the Sun Stone quest.
Ayla's Charm: Ayla can steal (Charm) unique items from many bosses. Key targets: Rust Tyranno → Elixir, various bosses → Speed Tabs and Power Tabs. Farm these early.
🌌

12,000 BC — The Dark Ages & Zeal

Enhasa · Kajar · Zeal Palace · Ocean Palace · Black Omen

🌌

S07 · 12,000 BC — The Kingdom of Zeal

▼

Queen Zeal seeks to harness Lavos's power from the Ocean Palace. The Gurus are scattered across time. Schala, the queen's daughter, aids the party secretly.

  • Enhasa and Kajar: explore for Magic Capsule, Speed Tab, and lore books
  • Zeal Palace: get the Epoch (time machine); learn about the Mammon Machine
  • Mountain of Woe: defeat Giga Gaia to free Guru of Life (Melchior)
  • Ocean Palace: fight through to stop Zeal; Crono dies here (or use the Pendant)
  • Escape and arrive at the End of Time and the Black Bird
Boss — Giga Gaia: HP 8,000 (head) + 2,000 each arm. Destroy arms first (they heal the head and cast spells). Lightning 2 on the head; Frog's Water on arms.
Boss — Lavos Spawn (Ocean Palace): HP 4,000 (shell) + 1,000 (head). Attack the shell — the head absorbs all damage if targeted. Hitting the shell reduces HP until the head is exposed.
Crono's Death: At the Ocean Palace, Crono sacrifices himself against Lavos. He is permanently dead until you complete the Chrono Trigger (Egg of Time) sidequest. Gaspar at the End of Time provides the Egg. Use it at Death Peak in 2300 AD to resurrect Crono.
🏴

S08 · Black Omen & Key Sidequests

▼

After the Ocean Palace, the Black Omen rises. Complete sidequests before the final dungeon.

  • Crono's Resurrection: Get Chrono Trigger from Gaspar (End of Time) → Death Peak (2300 AD) → fight 3x Lavos Spawn → use the Egg at the top
  • Sun Stone quest: Retrieve charged Moon Stone from 1000 AD Sun Keep → give to Lucca → get Wonder Shot + Sun Shades
  • Rainbow Shell quest (600 AD): Talk to Toma's ghost with the pop bottle → Giant's Claw dungeon → bring the shell to 1000 AD → forge Rainbow / Prism Dress / Prism Helm
  • Lucca's Mother (580 AD): Use pendant at the time machine → go to 580 AD → enter Lucca's house → input code LARA at the machine to save her legs
  • Magus recruitment: After Ocean Palace, Magus is on North Cape. Confront him — choose to fight (he joins after) or leave him
Prism gear: Rainbow Shell forged into Prism Dress (best female armor) and Prism Helm (best helm). Rainbow Sword for Crono is arguably his best weapon. All from the Rainbow Shell + Sunstone quest line.
Lucca's Mother sidequest: Go to 580 AD via the Epoch. Enter Lucca's house in Truce — a machine has trapped her mother (Lara). The code to stop the machine is LARA. If you enter the wrong code or skip this, Lara stays crippled (as in the original timeline). This is permanent.
🌑

S09 · Black Omen Dungeon

▼

The Black Omen is a massive flying dungeon. It can be entered in 12,000 BC, 600 AD, or 1000 AD for bonus items. Entering in an earlier era means fighting through it again in later eras for more loot.

  • Floor 1: Mystic Mist room — fight Nus to pass (don't attack the blue Nu)
  • Floor 2: Plasma beam corridors — hug the walls to avoid damage
  • Floor 3: Azala clones — fight Golem Twins
  • Floor 4: Alien cells — fight Mammon Machine (again)
  • Floor 5: Queen Zeal (Phase 1) then Queen Zeal (Phase 2)
Boss — Golem Twins: HP 3,500 each · Mirror elemental attacks back. Use physical attacks only — no magic. Robo's Laser Spin + Ayla's Triple Kick + Frog's physical hits.
Boss — Queen Zeal (Final Form): HP 32,000 · Photon Beam hits entire party for ~400. Periodic Black Hole instakills one character. Use Luminaire (Crono), Antipode 3 (Lucca + Marle), or Dark Matter (Magus). Heal aggressively — Robo's Heal Beam keeps everyone alive.
🌍

S10 · Final Battle — Lavos

▼

Lavos can be challenged multiple ways: through the Black Omen → Zeal, through the Gate in the sewers (2300 AD), or directly from the End of Time (unlocks alternate endings in New Game+).

  • Lavos Shell: destroy the Left Bit and Right Bit (they spawn more bits and heal the shell) — then attack the main body
  • Lavos's Body: three forms inside — a node that casts spells + two arms
  • Lavos Core: the true final boss — three parts (Left, Core, Right)
Boss — Lavos Shell: Attack the Right Bit first (counters with Fire 2), then Left Bit (Ice 2), then focus the shell's body. Don't let bits fully charge — Bits use Dreamless on the party.
Boss — Lavos Body (Outer): Three targets. Center can be targeted directly. Left uses Magic, Right uses physical. Kill Right first, then Left, then Center. Resurrect immediately if the Center attacks with Dreamless.
Boss — Lavos Core (Inner): HP 30,000 (Core) + 6,000 (Left) + 4,000 (Right). LEFT SHELL must die before attacking the Core — attacks on Core while Left Shell is alive are reflected back. Kill Left, then Right, then Core. Luminaire + Dark Matter + Magic in every turn. Heal when party falls below 300 HP. Use Elixirs freely.
Best party for Lavos: Crono (Luminaire), Marle (Arise + Hastes), Magus (Dark Matter). Or: Crono, Lucca, Frog for triple-tech Delta Force AoE on Bits. Keep everyone at full HP entering each phase.
🔄

S11 · New Game+ & Alternate Endings

▼

Chrono Trigger has 13 alternate endings depending on when you fight Lavos and what you've done. New Game+ preserves your levels, items, and techs.

  • The Dream Project: Beat Lavos at the very start of New Game+ → developer credits room
  • Beyond Time: Normal ending — defeat Lavos after completing everything; best cutscenes
  • Apocalypse: Lose to Lavos at the Ocean Palace → bad ending
  • The Legendary Hero: Beat Lavos before going to 600 AD second time
  • The Reunited: Beat Lavos after reviving Crono but before Black Omen
  • What the Prophet Seeks: Beat Lavos in 12,000 BC as "Magus" — special Magus ending
Ozzie's Fort (600 AD sidequest): After Magus joins, return to 600 AD — a new dungeon, Ozzie's Fort, opens. Fight Flea, Slash, Ozzie again for the final time. Ozzie's defeat is triggered by a cat running past him. Rewards: Ozzie Pants (worst equipment, comedic).
🏯

S12 · Ozzie's Fort & Fiona's Shrine

▼

After Magus joins the party (or after Ocean Palace), two sidequests open in 600 AD and 1000 AD.

  • Ozzie's Fort (600 AD): New dungeon in the northwest of the 600 AD map. Fight Flea+, Slash+, and Ozzie one final time. Ozzie's defeat is triggered by a cat running past him — no attack needed. Reward: Ozzie Pants (comedic worst-in-game armor).
  • Fiona's Shrine (1000 AD): Fiona and Marco need help restoring a forest devastated long ago. Leave Robo at the shrine (he spends 400 years planting trees). Return from 2300 AD to see the restored Fiona's Forest — Robo rejoins and the party rests around a campfire (key lore scene).
  • After the campfire scene, talk to Robo to get the Haste Helm (one of the best helmets).
Boss — Flea+ & Slash+: Enhanced versions. Slash+ has much higher physical damage — front-attack with Robo/Ayla. Flea+ casts powerful magic — use Frog's Water 2 or Crono's Lightning 2.
Boss — Ozzie Final: HP 2,000 · Don't attack Ozzie directly — he reflects all damage. Instead, hit the four floor tiles to open trapdoors, or wait for the cat to run through. The cat triggers Ozzie's final undoing.
☀️

S13 · Sun Stone · Rainbow Shell · Lucca's Mother

▼

Three major sidequests that yield the best equipment and an emotional character moment. Complete all three before challenging Lavos or entering the Black Omen.

  • Sun Stone: Place the Moon Stone (found in Sunken Desert) in the Sun Keep of 65M BC. Travel to 2300 AD Sun Keep to retrieve it (now fully charged). Give to Lucca → she crafts the Wonder Shot (Lucca's best weapon) and Sun Shades (Lucca's best helm).
  • Rainbow Shell (Giant's Claw, 600 AD): Talk to Toma's grave in 600 AD with the Pop (Soda) — he reveals the shell is in the Giant's Claw (northeast of map, former Tyranno Lair). Fight King Guardia's false accusation trial in 1000 AD using the shell as evidence. Forge: Rainbow Sword (Crono's best), Prism Dress (best female armor), Prism Helm.
  • Lucca's Mother (580 AD): During the Epoch-enabled era exploration, visit 580 AD. Enter Lucca's house. The machine has caught her mother's (Lara's) legs. Input the code LARA to stop the machine. This prevents Lara's disability and alters Lucca's backstory permanently.
Boss — Rust Tyranno (Giant's Claw): HP 12,000 · Weak to Ice. Marle's Ice 2, Frog's Water 2. Ayla can Charm an Elixir from it. Uses Zap attack — keep everyone above 200 HP.
Rainbow Shell trial: After getting the shell, 1000 AD triggers a trial accusing King Guardia of selling the Rainbow Shell. Present the shell and the original deposition document as evidence. If you skip this event, you cannot forge the Prism gear.
💫

S14 · Crono's Resurrection & Death Peak

▼

Crono died at the Ocean Palace. To resurrect him, get the Chrono Trigger (Egg of Time) from Gaspar (the Old Man at the End of Time) and use it at Death Peak in 2300 AD.

  • Talk to Gaspar at the End of Time — he gives you the Chrono Trigger (Egg of Time)
  • Travel to Death Peak in 2300 AD (southeast of the map)
  • Climb Death Peak: 3 Lavos Spawn guard the summit — fight them
  • At the summit, use the Chrono Trigger → choose the Crono clone from the fair → Crono is restored
  • Crono rejoins with all his levels and gear intact
Boss — Lavos Spawn (×3): HP 4,000 (shell) each. Target only the shell — the head reflects attacks. Use physical hits or Frog/Magus magic. Each is a solo fight on the path up the mountain. Bring Elixirs.
Do this before the Black Omen: Crono's Luminaire tech is the most powerful AoE in the game and essential for both the Black Omen and Lavos. Skipping his resurrection makes the endgame significantly harder.
🔚

S15 · All 13 Endings Guide

▼

Chrono Trigger has 13 endings determined by when you challenge Lavos and what conditions you met. New Game+ lets you access all of them.

  • Ending 1 — Beyond Time (True Ending): Defeat Lavos after reviving Crono, completing all sidequests, and defeating Queen Zeal in the Black Omen. Best cutscenes.
  • Ending 2 — Reunion: Defeat Lavos after Ocean Palace but without reviving Crono. Marle's pendant moment.
  • Ending 3 — The Dream Project: New Game+ only — defeat Lavos immediately from the End of Time without doing anything. Dev room appears with the game's creators as NPCs.
  • Ending 4 — The Successor of Guardia: Beat Lavos during the Masamune quest (before going to 600 AD the second time).
  • Ending 5 — Good Night: Beat Lavos after visiting 600 AD but before going to 2300 AD.
  • Ending 6 — The Legendary Hero: Beat Lavos after going to 2300 AD but before the Hero Medal quest.
  • Ending 7 — The Unknown Past: Beat Lavos after the Hero Medal but before visiting the Factory.
  • Ending 8 — People of the Times: Beat Lavos after the Factory but before getting the Gate Key from 65M BC.
  • Ending 9 — The Oath: Beat Lavos after the Gate Key but before Magus's Castle.
  • Ending 10 — Dino Age: Lose to Azala in 65M BC, then beat Lavos — Azala's dinosaurs take over the present.
  • Ending 11 — What the Prophet Seeks: Beat Lavos in 12,000 BC while playing as "Magus." Special ending focused on Magus's true goal.
  • Ending 12 — Memory Lane: Beat Lavos after Ocean Palace but before getting the Epoch repaired. Slideshow of party memories.
  • Ending 13 — Apocalypse: Lose to Lavos at the Ocean Palace event. Dark game-over ending.
New Game+ strategy: On your first NG+ run, aim for Ending 3 (The Dream Project) immediately, then Ending 11 (Prophet Seeks) — these require specific conditions that are easy to hit. Then go for the true ending (Beyond Time) in a clean save.
